# NetPdf — Progress Status

**Current phase:** Phase 3 — Fragmentainer-aware layout + pagination 🚧 In progress (Task 12 sub-cycle 1 — `TableLayouter` Hello-World + post-PR-#49 review hardening (6 findings: two-phase measure+emit protocol, paint-safe fragment order, cell-resolver isolation, caption diagnostic, missing-grid diagnostic code, production-pipeline tests) — ready for re-review)
**Tagged release:** `0.1.0-alpha` (Phase 1 complete ✅). `0.3.0-alpha` is **ready to tag** — version bumped in [Directory.Build.props](Directory.Build.props) + [build/version.json](build/version.json), CHANGELOG entry staged under `[Unreleased]` framing, full suite + AOT gate green; `git tag --list` will not show `0.3.0-alpha` until Roland creates the tag after PR merge.
**Target next tag:** `0.7.0-beta` (Phase 3 complete — fragmentainer-aware layout + pagination)

## Pending pre-v1.0 work

- **Coverage-guided fuzzing infrastructure** — deferred from Phase D (PR #18) to a dedicated post-Phase-3 milestone. Per the Phase D analysis (recommendation #8 from the threat-model audit), SharpFuzz + AFL++ harnesses for `HtmlParsingHost`, `CssPreprocessor` / `CssParserAdapter`, `SelectorCompiler`, `CalcResolver`, `VarSubstitution`, `ImageSafetyValidator`, `FontSafetyValidator`, and `PdfPreflightValidator` give continuous regression coverage of the parser surfaces our regression corpus can't exhaustively cover. Estimated 4-6 weeks dedicated effort (build-system integration, 8 harnesses + corpora, CI gate, crash triage runbook); deferred to land **after Phase 3 layout** so the eventual fuzz surface is more stable, with a 30-day no-new-crashes gate before the v1.0 tag. Phase A-D's regression corpus + threat-model coverage (215+ security tests) remains the primary defense in the interim.
**Last updated:** 2026-05-11 (**Phase 3 Task 12 sub-cycle 1 shipped + post-PR-#49 review hardening — `TableLayouter` Hello-World with two-phase measure+emit protocol, paint-safe ordering, resolver isolation, caption diagnostic, and 6 review findings**. [PR #49](https://github.com/raroche/NetPdf/pull/49) opened at `77120ca`; this hardening updates the same branch in-place. **Post-PR-#49 review hardening (6 findings, 4 P1):** (1) [P1 #1] **Table height fed back into block flow** — pre-hardening `TableLayouter` left `fragmentainer.UsedBlockSize` unchanged after emitting rows because BlockLayouter "already advanced by the wrapper" — but for auto-height tables that wrapper extent is 0 (CSS `height: auto` reads as 0), so siblings overlapped the rows + tables near the page bottom didn't trigger break-before. Fix: split TableLayouter into a **two-phase measure+emit protocol**. New public `MeasureContentHeight(...)` pre-computes the row stack height (cell content laid out into a buffered MeasuringFragmentSink — no outer-sink emits during measure); the result is cached on the layouter. `AttemptLayout` reuses the cached measurements. BlockLayouter's child-processing loop (BOTH the Continue + forced-overflow paths PLUS `EmitBlockSubtreeRecursive`'s nested-table dispatch) now constructs the TableLayouter once, calls MeasureContentHeight to get `tableContentHeight`, uses `max(cssHeight, tableContentHeight)` as the effective wrapper height for the resolver consult + the emitted BoxFragment.BlockSize. `fragmentainer.UsedBlockSize` advances by the wrapper's actual border-box reflecting the measured content. (2) [P1 #2] **Paint-safe fragment order** — MeasuringFragmentSink previously forwarded translated cell content to the outer sink DURING measurement; row + cell fragments were emitted AFTER. Phase 4 painter walks fragment order, so backgrounds/borders would paint OVER text. Fix: rewrite MeasuringFragmentSink to BUFFER fragments. New public `FlushTo(target)` drains the buffer to the outer sink in order. TableLayouter's row-emit loop now: measure cells (buffered) → compute row height → emit row fragment → emit each cell fragment → flush each cell's buffered content. Final outer-sink order: [wrapper] [row N] [cells N] [cell content N] [row N+1] ... — backgrounds before text. (3) [P1 #3] **Resolver isolation** — `LayoutCellContent` previously passed the OUTER `IBreakResolver` to the nested BlockLayouter. Inner checkpoint registration would replace/return the outer's checkpoint lease, corrupting later outer pagination/rewind decisions. Fix: each cell layout constructs `using var cellResolver = new BreakResolver();` — fresh instance scoped to the cell, dispose returns the cell-local lease to the pool. The outer resolver is never passed to nested layouters. (4) [P1 #4] **Captions emit feature diagnostic** — BoxBuilder keeps `<caption>` as a direct child of the Table wrapper (NOT inside TableGrid). Pre-hardening, captions were never walked + silently dropped. Fix: after finding TableGrid, walk the Table wrapper's direct children for `TableCaption`; for each, emit `LAYOUT-TABLE-FEATURE-UNSUPPORTED-001` Warning with the caption's text content (recursive TextRun walk, ~80 char cap, embedded newlines collapsed) included in the diagnostic message so users see what got dropped. (5) [P2 #5] **Missing-TableGrid uses correct diagnostic code** — pre-hardening emitted `PAGINATION-FORCED-OVERFLOW-001`, but a missing TableGrid is a malformed-box-tree invariant violation, not pagination overflow. Fix: changed to `LAYOUT-TABLE-FEATURE-UNSUPPORTED-001` with an explicit "box-generation invariant violation" message. (6) [P2 #6] **Production-pipeline integration tests** — pre-hardening tests bypassed BoxBuilder by constructing Table → TableGrid → row → cell hierarchies directly. Fix: new `tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Phase3/TableLayouterProductionTests.cs` (357 LOC) with 6 tests routing real HTML through `HtmlParsingHost` → `CssPreprocessor` → `CssParserAdapter` → `CascadeResolver` → `BoxBuilder` → `BlockLayouter`: simple table renders via full pipeline; table-followed-by-paragraph doesn't overlap (Finding 1 regression); table-with-caption emits feature diagnostic; thead/tbody collects rows via row groups; colspan emits feature diagnostic via full pipeline; cell with real inline text lays out via inline-only-block. Plus 5 new direct-construction tests in TableLayouterTests covering Findings 1-5 each. **Plus Copilot inline-review cleanup: removed unused `_incomingContinuation` field** — the constructor parameter is validated against null + then discarded; no field needed (sub-cycle 2 will re-introduce when `TableContinuation` lands). **Nested-table dispatch in `EmitBlockSubtreeRecursive`** — discovered during Finding 6 integration testing: pre-hardening only the top-level child loop in BlockLayouter dispatched TableLayouter, so nested tables (e.g., `body > table` which BoxBuilder produces by default) had their rows/cells silently dropped. The hardening symmetrically adds the same MeasureContentHeight + EmitTableInner protocol to the recursion's transient LayoutContext. Tests: **4176 unit / 4307 solution-wide passing** (+12 unit / +12 solution-wide over PR #49 baseline at 4164 / 4295 — 5 Finding-1-to-5 direct tests + 6 Finding-6 production-pipeline tests + 1 capturing-resolver test double; 4 skipped). AOT/JIT byte-parity gate stays green. Active-task pointer advances to **Task 12 sub-cycle 2** — `table-layout: auto`/`fixed` algorithms + `colspan`/`rowspan` cell merging + border-collapse model + captions actually laid out (not just diagnosed) + `<col>` widths + multi-page row splitting + thead/tfoot repetition — OR **Task 13** depending on review priority.)

**Phase 3 Task 12 sub-cycle 1 shipped — `TableLayouter` Hello-World** (historical entry; superseded by hardening review above. Continues from Task 11 sub-cycle 1 + post-PR-#48 review hardening ([PR #48](https://github.com/raroche/NetPdf/pull/48) merged at `a21f5a8`). Task 11 sub-cycle 1 wired the block ↔ inline integration seam for `<p>`-style inline-only block containers; Task 12 sub-cycle 1 ships the first **non-block-flow layouter** — `TableLayouter` — handling the `Table → TableGrid → row → cell` hierarchy that `BoxBuilder` produces for HTML `<table>` content. **New types in [`src/NetPdf.Layout/Layouters/`](src/NetPdf.Layout/Layouters/):** [`TableLayouter`](src/NetPdf.Layout/Layouters/TableLayouter.cs) — `internal sealed class : ILayouter, IDisposable`. Constructor signature mirrors `BlockLayouter`: `(rootBox, sink, incomingContinuation: null, diagnostics: null, shaperResolver: null)` where `rootBox.Kind` MUST be `Table` or `InlineTable` (validates at the constructor + throws `ArgumentException` otherwise). The outer `Table` / `InlineTable` `BoxFragment` is emitted by the parent `BlockLayouter` via its standard block-flow path; `TableLayouter` is dispatched AFTER that emit + adds the inner row + cell fragments at fragmentainer-relative offsets so the painter sees the complete table geometry. **Algorithm (equal-column "Hello World"):** (1) Find the wrapper's `TableGrid` child (defensive — `BoxBuilder`'s table fixup is supposed to insert it; missing grid emits a diagnostic + returns AllDone). (2) Walk the TableGrid's children in document order, recursing into `TableRowGroup` / `TableHeaderGroup` / `TableFooterGroup` to collect their `TableRow` children. Captions, column groups, columns are SKIPPED (sub-cycle 1 deferral). (3) Column count = max number of `TableCell` children across all rows. Sub-cycle 1 assumes no `colspan` (cell count == column count); cells declaring `colspan` / `rowspan` emit `LAYOUT-TABLE-FEATURE-UNSUPPORTED-001` Warning + the attribute is silently ignored (cell occupies one column × one row). (4) Equal-split inline-size: `columnWidth = contentInlineSize / columnCount`. No author column widths, no shrink-to-fit, no min/max-content sizing. (5) For each row: measure each cell's content extent via a nested `BlockLayouter` with a `MeasuringFragmentSink` wrapping the outer sink — the row height resolves to the maximum measured cell extent. Cell-content fragments land at fragmentainer-relative coordinates via the nested `BlockLayouter`; `TableLayouter` then emits one `BoxFragment` per row spanning the full inline width at the computed row height, then one `BoxFragment` per cell at the column offset with the row height. (6) `FragmentainerContext.UsedBlockSize` advances by the row height as each row is committed. **`BlockLayouter` integration:** new private `DispatchTableInnerIfNeeded(child, parentInlineOffset, parentContentTop, parentContentInlineSize, ctx, ref layoutCtx, resolver, ct)` helper wired at TWO sites — the normal Continue path (after the outer Table fragment is emitted) + the forced-overflow path (so oversized tables still render inner geometry alongside the diagnostic). The helper resolves the wrapper's border + padding via the existing inline/block edge readers, computes the inner content-top-left + content-inline-size, constructs a `TableLayouter`, and calls `AttemptLayout` with `LastResort` strategy (sub-cycle 1 doesn't propagate rewind / break inside the table). **Diagnostics:** new `LAYOUT-TABLE-FEATURE-UNSUPPORTED-001` Warning code added to `PaginateDiagnosticCodes` + `NetPdf/Diagnostics/DiagnosticCodes` + `docs/diagnostics-codes.md`; emitted once per cell carrying `colspan` / `rowspan` attributes. Existing `PAGINATION-FORCED-OVERFLOW-001` is emitted when the row stack exceeds the fragmentainer's remaining block size (sub-cycle 1 doesn't split tables across pages). **Sub-cycle 1 scope limits + sub-cycle 2+ TODOs** (documented inline + in `docs/deferrals.md#table-auto-fixed-spans-borders`): CSS Tables L3 §3 auto-table-layout (shrink-to-fit columns via min/max-content); §3.5 fixed-table-layout (column widths from `<col>` + first-row cell widths); §6.3 border-collapse model + `border-spacing`; cell merging (`colspan` / `rowspan`); §11 captions; §6.4 column-group widths; per-page header / footer repeat across pages; multi-fragmentainer table splitting + row-level `break-inside: avoid`; RTL writing modes / row reversal. **Tests: 4164 unit / 4295 solution-wide passing** (+12 unit / +12 solution-wide over PR #48's 4152 / 4283 baseline — 9 new `TableLayouterTests` + 3 diagnostic parity tests; 4 skipped). New tests: [`TableLayouterTests`](tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Phase3/TableLayouterTests.cs) — 9 tests pinning: simple 2×2 emit order (outer + nested cell-content fragments + 2 row fragments + 4 cell fragments); row height equals max cell extent; equal-column-split offsets; empty table emits only the outer wrapper; `colspan` cell triggers `LAYOUT-TABLE-FEATURE-UNSUPPORTED-001`; oversized table triggers `PAGINATION-FORCED-OVERFLOW-001`; non-table rootBox kind rejected via `ArgumentException`; non-null incoming continuation rejected; rows nested inside `<thead>` / `<tbody>` collected via row-group recursion. Plus 3 diagnostic parity tests added to `DiagnosticCodesTests` (registry match, value stable, facade vs paginate agree). Plus new `table-auto-fixed-spans-borders` entry in `docs/deferrals.md` + `DeferralsParityTests.ExpectedDeferralIds`. AOT/JIT byte-parity gate stays green. Active-task pointer advances to **Task 12 sub-cycle 2** — `table-layout: auto`/`fixed` algorithms + `colspan` / `rowspan` cell merging + border-collapse model + captions + `<col>` widths — OR **Task 13** depending on review priority.)

**Phase 3 Task 11 sub-cycle 1 shipped + post-PR-#48 review hardening — Block + inline integration with InlineLayoutResult bundle, recursive nested dispatch, pagination integration, CSS box model, and 8 review findings** (historical entry; superseded by Task 12 sub-cycle 1 above. PR #47 (deferrals doc) merged at `988e63a`; this branch rebased on it. **Post-PR-#48 review hardening (8 findings, 5 P1):** (1) [P1 #1] **InlineLayoutResult bundle** — Phase 4 painter needs `ShapedRun[]` + preprocessed `TextRun[]` to resolve `LineFragment.Slices.ShapedRunIndex` into concrete `ShapedGlyph` data. New `src/NetPdf.Layout/Inline/InlineLayoutResult.cs` record struct bundles `Lines + ShapedRuns + PreprocessedRuns`. `InlineLayouter.Layout` (both overloads) + `LayoutPerRun` return this struct; `BoxFragment.InlineLines` renamed to `InlineLayout: InlineLayoutResult?`. Migrated 5 inline-layouter test files to use `.Lines` accessor. New painter-contract resolution test walks slices to concrete glyphs. (2) [P1 #2] **Recursive nested dispatch** — `EmitBlockSubtreeRecursive` now has an inline-only branch (`EmitInlineOnlyBlockInRecursion`) so `<div><p>Hello</p></div>` correctly emits the p's `InlineLayout`. `MeasureSubtreeVisualBlockExtentRecursive` includes inline block-axis extent via new `MeasureInlineOnlyBlockExtent`. (3) [P1 #3] **Pagination integration** — new `DispatchInlineOnlyBlock` captures `LayoutCheckpoint`, consults `IBreakResolver` via `BreakOpportunity.Block`, handles Rewind / BreakHere (forced overflow + clean PageComplete) / Continue. Oversized inline content emits `LAYOUT-FORCED-OVERFLOW` diagnostic. (4) [P1 #4] **`CollectInlineTextRuns` content handling** — `LineBreak` (`<br>`) injects synthetic U+2028 LINE SEPARATOR TextRun (survives `Normal` whitespace collapse + triggers mandatory break); `Marker` (list bullets) recurses into children with the marker's own Style; atomic inline (`InlineBlockContainer` / `InlineFlexContainer` / `InlineGridContainer` / `InlineTable` / `InlineReplacedElement`) emit new `LAYOUT-INLINE-ATOMIC-NOT-SUPPORTED-001` diagnostic + skip. (5) [P1 #5] **CSS box model honored** — new `ReadInlineOnlyBlockMetrics` reads margin/border/padding/width/`line-height`; new `ComputeInlineOnlyBlockLayout` resolves border-box from declared width (or full range when `auto`), places lines inside the content box, computes block-size = content + padding-vertical + border-vertical. `line-height` from CSS overrides the 1.2 × font-size fallback. (6) [P2 #6] **`NotSupportedException` catch** — `try/catch` around `InlineLayouter.LayoutPerRun` in `LayoutInlineContent`; falls back to Warning `LAYOUT-INLINE-UNSUPPORTED-001` diagnostic + no fragment emitted. Induced via `word-break:keep-all` vs `normal` mismatch test. (7) [P2 #7] **Diagnostic parity** — 9 new parity tests (3 codes × 3 checks each: registry match, value stable, facade vs paginate); `docs/diagnostics-codes.md` footer bumped + LAYOUT-* section extended. (8) [P2 #8] **End-to-end tests** — 12 new tests in `BlockInlineIntegrationTests.cs` covering all findings + painter-contract resolution. Plus follow-up commit adding `inline-atomic-boxes` entry to `docs/deferrals.md` + `DeferralsParityTests.ExpectedDeferralIds` (PR #47's enforcement, now ratified by this PR's branch via rebase). **Per-run mismatch acceptance matrix unchanged from sub-cycle 4** (WhiteSpace all 6, OverflowWrap Normal+Anywhere, WordBreak Normal+BreakAll with KeepAll throw, Hyphens all 3). **Sub-cycle 2+ TODOs documented inline:** margin-collapse between inline-only block + block siblings; per-line splitting for oversized inline; cache inline-pass across measure + emit; per-run line-height + CSS Text L3 strut/ascent-descent; atomic inline placeholder injection. Tests: **4152 unit / 4283 solution-wide passing** (+27 unit / +27 solution-wide over PR #47's 4125 baseline — 4 original sub-cycle 1 tests + 20 hardening tests + 3 parity tests; 4 skipped). AOT/JIT byte-parity gate stays green. Active-task pointer advances to **Task 12** — `TableLayouter` — chosen by reviewer priority over Task 11 sub-cycle 2 (text-align / vertical-align / floats around inline / margin-collapse integration).)

**Phase 3 Task 11 sub-cycle 1 shipped — Block + inline integration** (historical entry; superseded by hardening review above. Continues from Task 10 cycle 3d sub-cycle 4 ([PR #46](https://github.com/raroche/NetPdf/pull/46) merged at `23612c9`). Task 10 cycle 3d's per-source-run policy plumbing is now consumed by `BlockLayouter`: when the layouter encounters a block container whose children are entirely inline-level (e.g., a `<p>` containing only text + inline `<span>`s, or the `AnonymousBlock` boxes that `BoxBuilder` wraps inline runs in), it dispatches into `InlineLayouter.LayoutPerRun` and emits ONE `BoxFragment` for the inline-only block with the wrapped `LineFragment[]` carried on the new `BoxFragment.InlineLines` field. The Phase 4 painter consumes the line array to position shaped-glyph slices at successive baselines inside the fragment's border box. **Wiring (`BlockLayouter`):** new optional `IShaperResolver? shaperResolver = null` constructor parameter — when supplied, drives the inline pass; when null + inline content encountered, emits a `LAYOUT-INLINE-SKIPPED-NO-SHAPER-RESOLVER-001` diagnostic + skips (mirrors the pre-sub-cycle-1 behavior for back-compat with existing test fixtures). New `IsInlineOnlyBlockContainer` predicate detects the dispatch target. New private `LayoutInlineContent` method collects `TextRun`s via `CollectInlineTextRuns` (walks the subtree, picks up `BoxKind.TextRun` leaves with non-empty text; atomic inline-replaced / inline-block / inline-flex / inline-grid / inline-table / `<br>` are recognized but silently skipped — sub-cycle 2+ scope), calls `InlineLayouter.LayoutPerRun` with hard-coded `"Latn"` / `"en"` + `ParagraphDirection.LeftToRight` (UAX #24 + RTL deferred per `docs/deferrals.md`), computes a placeholder block extent (`lineCount × 1.2 × fontSize`, default 16 px when font-size unset — line-height property wiring deferred), emits the BoxFragment, advances `fragmentainer.UsedBlockSize`. **Margin chain reset semantics** for inline-only block: matches the existing non-block-level skip (line box breaks margin adjacency per CSS 2.1 §8.3.1). **`BoxFragment`** gains an optional `LineFragment[]? InlineLines` field (default null for back-compat with cycles 1-2c pure-block fragments). **Diagnostics:** new `LAYOUT-INLINE-SKIPPED-NO-SHAPER-RESOLVER-001` code added to `PaginateDiagnosticCodes` + `NetPdf/Diagnostics/DiagnosticCodes` + `docs/diagnostics-codes.md`. **Sub-cycle 1 scope limits + sub-cycle 2+ TODOs** (documented inline in the new `LayoutInlineContent` XML doc): mixed block + inline children inside one BFC; margin / border / padding honoring on the inline-only block itself; margin-collapse chain participation; widows / orphans (CSS Fragmentation L3 §4.3); `line-height` from `ComputedStyle`; `text-align` / `vertical-align`; RTL fragment-level slice reversal; UAX #24 script + BCP 47 language detection; inline content flowing around floats; atomic inline-replaced / inline-block / inline-flex / inline-grid / inline-table / `<br>` descendants. Tests: **4129 unit / 4260 solution-wide passing** (+4 unit / +4 solution-wide over PR #46 hardening at 4125; 4 skipped). New tests: 4 in `BlockInlineIntegrationTests.cs` — single-TextRun emits BoxFragment with InlineLines set; fragmentainer advances by lineCount × lineHeight; empty inline content emits no fragment; null shaperResolver emits diagnostic + skips. AOT/JIT byte-parity gate stays green. Active-task pointer advances to **Phase 3 Task 11 sub-cycle 2** — widows/orphans, line-height from CSS, mixed block+inline anonymous-block scenarios, atomic inline children — OR deeper integration tasks (text-align, vertical-align, floats around inline).)

**Phase 3 Task 10 cycle 3d sub-cycle 4 shipped + post-PR-#46 review hardening — per-source-run Hyphens with per-position Liang gating + SH suppression per-run + lazy posToSrcRun**. **Post-PR-#46 review hardening (6 findings):** (1) [P1 Finding #1] **Per-position Liang gate** — sub-cycle 4 originally gated Liang application by the WORD's first letter's source-run Hyphens, but a word can span source runs with different Hyphens values. A Liang break position landing INSIDE a None/Manual segment (because the word started in Auto) would be wrongly recorded; conversely an Auto-tail word starting in None would skip Liang entirely. Fix: (a) `ApplyLiangPatterns` now runs Liang when ANY letter in the word is in a Hyphens=Auto source run (not just the first letter); (b) each returned Liang break position is gated by `posToSrcRun[concatIdx].Hyphens == Auto` before being recorded. Cross-run words now produce correct Liang break geometry. (2) [P1 Finding #2] **Disabled soft-hyphens don't suppress Liang** — CSS Text L3 §6.1.1's "soft-hyphen suppresses elsewhere-in-word Liang" rule should only count ACTIVE soft hyphens. A U+00AD whose source run has Hyphens=None is demoted + excluded from `hyphenationAfter[]`; suppressing Liang because of it would unfairly lose valid Auto opportunities in the same tokenized word. Fix: the suppression scan in `ApplyLiangPatterns` now checks `posToSrcRun[shConcatIdx].Hyphens != None` for each U+00AD in the word — only ACTIVE soft hyphens trigger the suppression. (3) [P2 Finding #3] **Lazy `posToSrcRun` allocation** — previously built unconditionally whenever `inlineTextPolicyPerRun` was supplied, even for non-hyphenation paths (mixed WhiteSpace / OverflowWrap / WordBreak). For large inline content this wasted 4 bytes per UTF-16 code unit. Fix: build the map ONLY when `inlineTextPolicyPerRun is not null && (hasSoftHyphen || anyHyphensAuto)` — the actual conditions that need per-position Hyphens decisions. (4) [P2 Finding #4] **Exact-geometry mixed-word Liang tests** — replaced loose assertions with 4 new tests pinning per-position behavior: Liang-breaks-inside-None-segment-suppressed; Liang-runs-when-only-later-letters-Auto; disabled-SH-does-NOT-suppress-Liang-in-Auto-segment; Manual-alongside-Auto-no-Liang-inside-Manual. (5) [P3 Finding #5] **Stale `LineBuilder.cs` XML docs refreshed** — the old "LineBuilder-only scope (cycle 3b stopgap)" + "CSS-property pipeline deferral" sections claimed overflow-wrap/word-break/hyphens weren't wired through ComputedStyle. That pipeline shipped in Task 10 cycles 2-4; docs now describe the production path (KeywordResolver → ComputedStyle → InlineTextPolicyMaterializer → LayoutPerRun → per-run array). (6) [P3 Finding #6] **Removed unused `sourceTextRuns` parameter** from `ComputeHyphenationPositions` (the per-run policy data flows via `inlineTextPolicyPerRun` + `posToSrcRun` directly). **Per-run mismatch acceptance matrix unchanged from sub-cycle 4:** WhiteSpace all 6, OverflowWrap Normal+Anywhere, WordBreak Normal+BreakAll (KeepAll throws), Hyphens all 3. Tests: **4125 unit / 4256 solution-wide passing** (+4 unit / +4 solution-wide over pre-hardening sub-cycle 4 at 4121; 4 skipped). New tests: 4 in `InlineLayouterCycle3dTests` covering Finding #1 (Liang-inside-None suppression, Liang-runs-when-later-Auto) + Finding #2 (disabled-SH doesn't suppress Liang) + Manual+Auto interaction. AOT/JIT byte-parity gate stays green. Active-task pointer advances to **Task 11** (Phase 4 painter cycle / `LineFragment[]` → `BoxFragment` conversion) — the per-run mismatch matrix is now complete enough for the painter to consume `LineFragment[]` end-to-end. KeepAll CJK suppression (UAX #24) and BreakSpaces-distinctive semantics are the remaining sub-cycle 5+ items.)

**Phase 3 Task 10 cycle 3d sub-cycle 4 shipped — per-source-run Hyphens via hyphenation pipeline** (historical entry; superseded by hardening review above. Continues from Task 10 cycle 3d sub-cycle 3 ([PR #45](https://github.com/raroche/NetPdf/pull/45) merged at `9637137`). The `inlineTextPolicyPerRun` array already carried `Hyphens` through (sub-cycle 2 refactor + sub-cycle 3 validation); sub-cycle 4 wires the per-source-run decisions into the hyphenation pipeline. **Algorithm:** when `inlineTextPolicyPerRun` is supplied, `LineBuilder.Wrap` builds a `posToSrcRun: int[concatTotal]` map (lazy) so each concat position can look up its source run's Hyphens value. Two pipeline stages use this map: (1) **Soft-hyphen Allowed demotion** — the existing global "Hyphens=None demotes U+00AD breaks to Prohibited" pass becomes per-position; only positions whose source run has Hyphens=None get demoted. Positions in Manual/Auto runs keep their UAX #14 LB10 Allowed classification. (2) **`ComputeHyphenationPositions` + `ApplyLiangPatterns`** — per concat position, the soft-hyphen inclusion in `hyphenationAfter[]` is gated by source-run Hyphens (include if != None). The Liang per-word check uses the FIRST letter's source-run Hyphens (apply only if Auto). The sub-cycle 3 defense-in-depth guard (Wrap-side "per-run Hyphens must equal global") is REMOVED — direct callers can now pass a Hyphens mix freely. `InlineLayouter.LayoutPerRun` removes the throw on Hyphens mismatch; only WordBreak.KeepAll mismatch still throws (CJK semantics still pending UAX #24). **Per-run mismatch acceptance matrix as of sub-cycle 4:** WhiteSpace all 6 mixable, OverflowWrap Normal+Anywhere mixable, WordBreak Normal+BreakAll mixable (KeepAll on mismatch throws), Hyphens ALL 3 mixable. **Cycle 3d sub-cycle 4 deferrals (sub-cycle 5+ / Task 11):** WordBreak.KeepAll CJK inter-character break suppression (UAX #24 script detection + LB30b); BreakSpaces-distinctive semantics; UAX #24 + RTL fragment-level reversal; `LineFragment[]` → `BoxFragment` conversion (cycle 4); bidi-aware glyph painting. Tests: **4121 unit / 4252 solution-wide passing** (+4 unit / +4 solution-wide over PR #45 hardening at 4117; 4 skipped). New tests: 4 in `InlineLayouterCycle3dTests` covering soft-hyphen-in-None-run-not-wrap-candidate, soft-hyphen-in-Manual-run-IS-wrap-candidate, uniform-Auto regression, direct LineBuilder.Wrap Hyphens.None demotion proof. 4 prior throws-tests (cycle 3b, 3c, 3d sub-cycle 2, 3d sub-cycle 3) updated to assert handled behavior. AOT/JIT byte-parity gate stays green. Active-task pointer advances to **Task 11** (Phase 4 painter cycle / `LineFragment[]` → `BoxFragment` conversion) OR continue cycle 3d sub-cycle 5 (KeepAll CJK support via UAX #24 script detection) depending on review priority.)

**Phase 3 Task 10 cycle 3d sub-cycle 3 shipped + post-PR-#45 review hardening — per-source-run WordBreak.BreakAll with KeepAll throw + cross-run boundary + per-run Hyphens guard**. **Post-PR-#45 review hardening (5 findings):** (1) [P2 Finding #1] **KeepAll mismatch throws** — uniform KeepAll has always behaved like Normal (CJK inter-character break suppression needs UAX #24 script detection + LB30b), but accepting a KeepAll vs. {Normal, BreakAll} mismatch in per-run mode would silently lose KeepAll's intent. LayoutPerRun now throws NotSupportedException for KeepAll mismatches; uniform-KeepAll continues to silently approximate as Normal (documented). (2) [P2 Finding #2] **Per-run Hyphens defense-in-depth in Wrap** — LineBuilder.Wrap's per-run validation now rejects inlineTextPolicyPerRun entries whose Hyphens field differs from the global `hyphens` argument. Until sub-cycle 4 ships per-source-run Liang application, hyphenationAfter[] is built from the global hyphens arg only; direct callers (tests + future block-layouter wires) can't pass a Hyphens mix without triggering this guard. LayoutPerRun's caller-side check + the Wrap-side check together provide layered protection. (3) [P2 Finding #3] **Cross-run BreakAll boundary uses "either side may opt in"** — mirrors OverflowWrap's cross-run rule from sub-cycle 2. For the LAST glyph of a shaped run whose NEXT source run has BreakAll, perGlyphBreakAll is upgraded to true. This lets a Normal prefix wrap immediately at the run boundary of a following BreakAll span (instead of overflowing into the first BreakAll glyph before BreakAll's own upgrades take effect). (4) [P2 Finding #4] **Broader test coverage** — 8 new tests in InlineLayouterCycle3dTests: BreakAll-first-then-Normal-no-whitespace-boundary (Finding #3); Normal-immediately-followed-by-BreakAll-no-whitespace boundary (Finding #3 positive control); NoWrap+BreakAll interaction (NoWrap wins, downgrade after BreakAll upgrade); KeepAll mixed-with-Normal throws (Finding #1); invalid WordBreak/Hyphens enum values throw at Wrap entry (Finding #4); per-run Hyphens-must-match-global enforcement (Finding #2); direct LineBuilder.Wrap call with InlineTextPolicy[] proving end-to-end behavior. (5) [P3 Finding #5] **Stale docs refreshed** — InlineLayouter.cs adds an explicit per-run-mismatch acceptance matrix table (WhiteSpace all 6 / OverflowWrap Normal+Anywhere / WordBreak Normal+BreakAll / Hyphens throws + KeepAll throws); InlineTextPolicy.cs integration-status item for sub-cycle 3 + KeepAll/Hyphens deferral notes; LineFragment.cs shipped-capabilities ladder extended through sub-cycle 3; LineBuilder.Wrap's inlineTextPolicyPerRun XML doc documents WordBreak (sub-cycle 3 per-glyph) + Hyphens (sub-cycle 4 throws on mismatch with global). **Cycle 3d sub-cycle 3 deferrals (sub-cycle 4+):** per-source-run hyphens (Liang application per-run); KeepAll CJK semantics (UAX #24 script detection); BreakSpaces-distinctive semantics; UAX #24 + RTL fragment-level reversal; `LineFragment[]` → `BoxFragment` conversion (cycle 4); bidi-aware glyph painting. Tests: **4117 unit / 4248 solution-wide passing** (+8 unit / +8 solution-wide over pre-hardening sub-cycle 3 at 4109; 4 skipped). AOT/JIT byte-parity gate stays green. **Phase 3 Task 10 cycle 3d sub-cycle 2 shipped + post-PR-#44 review hardening — per-source-run OverflowWrap plumbing + refactor to single InlineTextPolicy[] parameter + grapheme-cluster gate + cross-run wrap-friendly gate**. **Post-PR-#44 review hardening (5 recommendations):** (1) [P1 Rec #1] **Grapheme-cluster boundary gate** on the overflow-wrap:anywhere forced-break fallback. Per CSS Text L3, anywhere must keep grapheme clusters (UAX #29) together. The new `IsGraphemeBoundaryBetweenFlatGlyphs` helper checks the cursor-1 → cursor break point's UTF-16 position against the existing `graphemeBreakAfter` array + applies `IsBreakAllProtected` for ZWJ/WJ/NBSP adjacencies. Multi-glyph single-cluster shapes (combining marks, ZWJ emoji, regional-indicator flag pairs) are detected via `clusterEnd <= prevCluster` and protected. Anywhere now snaps to grapheme boundaries instead of mid-cluster. (2) [P1 Rec #2] **Cross-run wrap-friendly gate** on anywhere. Two adjacent non-wrap-friendly source runs (e.g., NoWrap+Pre or Pre+NoWrap with overflow-wrap=anywhere) cannot become anywhere break sites at their style boundary — per CSS Text L3 §5.1 overflow-wrap only has effect when white-space allows wrapping. Cross-run gate now requires at least ONE side to be wrap-friendly per WhiteSpace; if both sides are Pre/NoWrap, the boundary stays unbreakable. (3) [P2 Rec #4] **Refactor parallel per-run arrays to a single InlineTextPolicy[] parameter**. `LineBuilder.Wrap` no longer takes `whiteSpacePerRun: IReadOnlyList<WhiteSpace>?` + `overflowWrapPerRun: IReadOnlyList<OverflowWrap>?` separately. Replaced with one `inlineTextPolicyPerRun: IReadOnlyList<InlineTextPolicy>?` that bundles all 4 dimensions (WhiteSpace + OverflowWrap + WordBreak + Hyphens) in one coherent struct. Future sub-cycles (word-break, hyphens) can plumb through the same array without adding nullable parameters. `LayoutPerRun` builds one array lazily on first mismatch + extracts a `WhiteSpace[]` for the preprocessor when needed. Validation: length match + every entry's WhiteSpace/OverflowWrap/WordBreak/Hyphens enums must be defined. (4) [P2 Rec #3] **Strengthened sub-cycle 2 tests** with exact line/slice/glyph assertions. Previously `>= 2` patterns; now `Assert.Equal(6, result.Length)` + per-line glyph-range + advance assertions. Added 4 new tests: combining-mark cluster preserved under anywhere (Rec #1), NoWrap+Pre cross-run boundary not broken (Rec #2), Pre+NoWrap symmetry, Normal+Anywhere boundary IS broken when at least one side wrap-friendly (positive control). (5) [P3 Rec #5] **Stale docs refreshed** in InlineLayouter.cs (full cycle 3a→3d sub-cycle 2 capability ladder), InlineTextPolicy.cs (integration status reflects sub-cycle 2 refactor), LineFragment.cs (sub-cycle deferrals point to word-break/hyphens, not overflow-wrap). **Cycle 3d sub-cycle 2 deferrals (sub-cycle 3+):** per-source-run word-break (BreakAll per-glyph); per-source-run hyphens (Hyphens.Auto Liang per-run); BreakSpaces-distinctive semantics; UAX #24 script detection; RTL fragment-level reversal; `LineFragment[]` → `BoxFragment` conversion (cycle 4); bidi-aware glyph painting. Tests: **4107 unit / 4238 solution-wide passing** (+4 unit / +4 solution-wide over pre-hardening at 4103; 4 skipped). New tests: 4 in `InlineLayouterCycle3dTests` covering Rec #1 (combining-mark cluster preserved) + Rec #2 (NoWrap+Pre, Pre+NoWrap cross-run gates) + positive control (Normal+Anywhere boundary IS broken). Prior sub-cycle 2 tests' `>= 2` assertions replaced with exact 6-line/per-glyph geometry. AOT/JIT byte-parity gate stays green. Active-task pointer advances to **Phase 3 Task 10 cycle 3d sub-cycle 3** — per-source-run word-break + hyphens, OR **Task 11** (Phase 4 painter cycle) depending on review priority.)

**Phase 3 Task 10 cycle 3d sub-cycle 1 shipped + post-PR-#43 review hardening — per-source-run WhiteSpace preprocessor with per-glyph trim + per-glyph anywhere gate + cancellation + soft-hyphen Liang suppression**. Continues from Task 10 cycle 3c ([PR #42](https://github.com/raroche/NetPdf/pull/42) merged at `0f05fba`). Cycle 3c narrowed the accepted mixed-WhiteSpace matrix to {Normal, NoWrap}-only because the preprocessor was uniform-mode; cycle 3d sub-cycle 1 ships **`LineBuilder.PreprocessTextRunsPerRun(runs, modes[])`** — each source run is preprocessed with its OWN WhiteSpace mode. Cross-run state managed per the "preserve runs are atomic; collapse runs chain via `inWs`" rule: two consecutive collapse-mode runs (Normal/NoWrap/PreLine) chain their `inWs` state across the boundary so trailing+leading SPs collapse; preserve-mode runs (Pre/PreWrap/BreakSpaces) emit content character-for-character and reset `inWs=false` for the next collapse run. Document-leading SP strip applies only when Run 0 is a collapse mode; document-trailing SP strip applies only when the last run is a collapse mode. **`InlineLayouter.LayoutPerRun`** updated to call the new preprocessor when per-run WhiteSpace varies — removing the cycle-3c Normal/NoWrap matrix-narrowing throw. **Result:** mixed-mode inputs like `<pre>` inside `white-space:normal` text now work without throwing. **Algorithm change in LayoutPerRun:** when a WhiteSpace-only mismatch is detected, build the per-source-run `WhiteSpace[]` array (lazily) + delegate via `PreprocessTextRunsPerRun` instead of the uniform `PreprocessTextRuns`. All 6 WhiteSpace values participate; the cycle-3c IsCollapseModeMatrixMember predicate is removed. **Cycle 3d sub-cycle 1 deferrals (subsequent cycles):** per-glyph overflow-wrap / word-break / hyphens for mixed-mode descendants (currently throws); UAX #24 script detection; RTL fragment-level reversal; `LineFragment[]` → `BoxFragment` conversion (cycle 4); bidi-aware glyph painting via Phase 4 painter integration. New tests: 15 in [`InlineLayouterCycle3dTests`](tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Phase3/InlineLayouterCycle3dTests.cs) — `PreprocessTextRunsPerRun` length-mismatch + invalid-enum + null-arg validation (4 tests); uniform-Normal regression equivalence with `PreprocessTextRuns`; Pre+Normal preserves Pre + collapses Normal at boundary; Normal+Pre preserves both; preserve-only doesn't strip document-trailing SP; collapse-only strips document-trailing SP; LayoutPerRun Normal+Pre / NoWrap+PreWrap / Normal+PreLine / Normal+BreakSpaces / Pre+Normal-first all-handled (5 tests); overflow-wrap mismatch still throws. Plus 4 cycle 3c matrix-narrowing-throw tests REMOVED (the mixes are now handled — see cycle 3d tests for replacements with exact assertions). **Post-PR-#43 review hardening (6 recommendations):** (1) [P1] **Per-glyph IsBreakSpace from source-run WhiteSpace** — previously the global wrap-time `collapsesSpaces` flag tagged Pre/PreWrap/BreakSpaces SP glyphs as IsBreakSpace too (because LayoutPerRun passes wrapWhiteSpace=Normal globally to defer wrap decisions to the per-glyph downgrade), causing soft-wrap snap-back to TRIM preserved spaces. Fix: derive IsBreakSpace per-glyph by looking up `whiteSpacePerRun[shaped.Source.SourceTextRunIndex]` + checking `IsCollapseModeWhiteSpace`. New regression test pins PreWrap "AAA "+Normal " BBB" preserves the PreWrap trailing SP at the soft-wrap boundary. (2) [P1] **Per-glyph gate on overflow-wrap:anywhere fallback** — previously the global `wrapsAtAllowed=true` in per-run mode let the anywhere forced-break fallback fire INSIDE NoWrap/Pre source runs when all runs shared overflow-wrap:anywhere. Per CSS Text L3 §5.1 "overflow-wrap only has an effect when white-space allows wrapping". Fix: when whiteSpacePerRun is supplied AND cursor>lineStart, check if break point (cursor-1 → cursor) is INSIDE a NoWrap/Pre source run; if so, gate the anywhere fallback to NOT fire. New regression tests for Pre(anywhere)+Normal(anywhere) and NoWrap(anywhere)+Normal(anywhere). (3) [P2] **BreakSpaces docs clarified as approximation** — the prior "deferred to a subsequent cycle" framing implied a cleaner ladder than reality. Now WhiteSpace.cs + InlineTextPolicy.cs explicitly document that BreakSpaces is APPROXIMATED as PreWrap (preserve + wrap at UAX #14 Allowed); distinguishing CSS Text L3 §6.4 semantics (forced wrap candidates at every preserved SP + trailing-space wrap-vs-hang) are NOT implemented and tracked as a known fidelity gap. (4) [P2] **PreprocessTextRunsPerRun CancellationToken** — added optional `CancellationToken cancellationToken = default` parameter checked at method entry + once per source-run boundary. LayoutPerRun's per-run path now passes the token + checks immediately after preprocessing (before the potentially-expensive ShapeForLayout call). New tests for pre-cancelled token in both `PreprocessTextRunsPerRun` direct API + `LayoutPerRun` per-run mode. (5) [P3] **Stale LineFragment.cs cycle-3d docs updated** — removed the claim that LayoutPerRun only handles Normal/NoWrap matrix; added cycle 3d sub-cycle 1 capabilities (per-source-run preprocessor + per-glyph IsBreakSpace + anywhere gate); per-glyph overflow-wrap/word-break/hyphens deferred to sub-cycle 2. (6) [P2] **Liang positions suppressed inside soft-hyphen-containing words** — pre-existing CSS Text L3 §6.1.1 gap surfaced during review. The word tokenizer in `ApplyLiangPatterns` now treats U+00AD as a word-internal character (via new `IsAsciiLetterOrSoftHyphen` predicate) so "hyphen­ation" is identified as ONE word; per-word check then SKIPS Liang for any word containing U+00AD (only the explicit soft-hyphen position is used). New regression test pins "hyphen­ation" with budget 30 wraps at the soft-hyphen position (line 0 = 6 glyphs "hyphen"), NOT at a Liang position (which would give line 0 = 2 glyphs "hy"). **Cycle 3d sub-cycle 1 deferrals (subsequent cycles):** per-glyph overflow-wrap / word-break / hyphens for mixed-mode descendants (currently throws); BreakSpaces-distinctive semantics (forced wraps at every preserved SP + trailing-space wrap-vs-hang per §6.4); UAX #24 script detection; RTL fragment-level reversal; `LineFragment[]` → `BoxFragment` conversion (cycle 4); bidi-aware glyph painting via Phase 4 painter integration. **Phase 3 Task 10 cycle 3c shipped + post-PR-#42 review hardening — per-glyph WhiteSpace honoring (NoWrap-inside-Normal) with narrowed Normal/NoWrap matrix** [PR #42] (historical entry, superseded by Task 10 cycle 3d sub-cycle 1 above). Cycle 3b shipped `LayoutPerRun(...)` that threw `NotSupportedException` on any policy mismatch; cycle 3c **relaxes mixed-mode WhiteSpace** by building a per-source-run WhiteSpace array + plumbing to a new `LineBuilder.Wrap` `whiteSpacePerRun` parameter. Glyphs in NoWrap/Pre runs get their UAX #14 Allowed opportunities downgraded to Prohibited at flat-build time. **Result:** mixed-mode `<span style="white-space:nowrap">` inside `white-space:normal` text now works without throwing. **Algorithm:** in `LayoutPerRun`, walk source runs + check each policy against the first non-empty's policy; on first mismatch, verify only WhiteSpace differs (other 3 fields must match) — else throw with explanatory message; if WhiteSpace-only, lazily build a `WhiteSpace[]` array indexed by source-run-index + plumb through `LineBuilder.Wrap`'s new optional `whiteSpacePerRun` parameter. The wrap-loop's flat-build pass uses `shaped.Source.SourceTextRunIndex` to look up per-glyph WhiteSpace + downgrades Allowed → Prohibited for NoWrap/Pre runs. (2) [P1] **Per-glyph wrapsAtAllowed when whiteSpacePerRun supplied** — the global `wrapsAtAllowed` gate inside `LineBuilder.Wrap` now defers authoritatively to the per-glyph downgrade when per-run mode is active. Previously a leading NoWrap source run made `wrapsAtAllowed=false` globally, suppressing wraps even in a TRAILING Normal source run (Normal-after-NoWrap order bug). New regression test pins the fix. (3) [P1] **Preprocess pass uses `WhiteSpace.Normal` (not PreWrap)** for mixed mode — since the matrix is now Normal/NoWrap-only, both collapse identically + Normal is the correct unified mode. The earlier PreWrap-everywhere preprocess would preserve whitespace from NoWrap-source-runs that should have been collapsed. **Phase 3 Task 10 cycle 3b shipped — `InlineLayouter.LayoutPerRun(...)` per-source-TextRun policy** [PR #41] (historical entry, superseded by Task 10 cycle 3c above). Continues from Task 10 cycle 3 ([PR #40](https://github.com/raroche/NetPdf/pull/40) merged at `2b575ea` + post-merge review pass at `1c4bd7a`). Cycle 3 shipped the containing-block-style `Layout` overload that applies a uniform policy; cycle 3b adds **`LayoutPerRun(...)` — reads each source-TextRun's policy + verifies they all match**, throwing `NotSupportedException` on mixed-mode descendants. **Why this is the right shape:** CSS Text L3 §3-§6 properties all inherit, so for the 95% case all source TextRuns share the same policy (inherited from the containing block) + the new overload silently delegates to the cycle-3a uniform path. For mixed-mode descendants (e.g., `<span style="white-space:nowrap">` inside `white-space:normal` text) the overload throws loudly with a descriptive message — the failure mode is loud + deterministic instead of silently using the wrong policy. Full per-glyph metadata for mixed-mode is scheduled for cycle 3c. **Algorithm:** read `InlineTextPolicy` from each TextRun's `Style.ReadInlineTextPolicy()`; check that all match the first via record-struct equality; if all match, delegate to the cycle-3a explicit-args path; if any differs, throw `NotSupportedException` with run-index + both policies in the message. **Cycle 3b deferrals (cycle 3c+):** per-glyph metadata stream threaded through `LineBuilder.Wrap` so mixed-mode descendants work without throwing; UAX #24 script detection; RTL fragment-level reversal; `LineFragment[]` → `BoxFragment` conversion (cycle 4); bidi-aware glyph painting via Phase 4 painter integration. New tests: 8 in [`InlineLayouterCycle3bTests`](tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Phase3/InlineLayouterCycle3bTests.cs) — null arg, empty input, uniform default policy, uniform NoWrap, mixed-white-space-throws, mixed-overflow-wrap-throws, mixed-hyphens-throws, singleton run. Tests: **4055 unit / 4191 solution-wide passing** (+8 unit / +8 solution-wide over PR #40 hardening at 4047; 4 skipped). AOT/JIT byte-parity gate stays green. Active-task pointer advances to **Phase 3 Task 10 cycle 3c** — per-glyph metadata stream for mixed-mode descendants (the actual implementation behind the cycle 3b "throws" guard), OR **Task 11** (Phase 4 painter cycle / display-list IR / `LineFragment[]` → drawn glyphs) depending on review priority.)

**Phase 3 Task 10 cycle 3 shipped — `InlineLayouter.Layout(...,ComputedStyle,...)` overload** [PR #40] (historical entry, superseded by Task 10 cycle 3b above). Continues from Task 10 cycle 2 ([PR #39](https://github.com/raroche/NetPdf/pull/39) merged at `eadc9f5` + post-merge review pass at `941a959`). Cycle 2 shipped the CSS-property pipeline (properties.json + KeywordResolver tables for overflow-wrap/word-break/hyphens) + the `InlineTextPolicy` materializer + 35 regression tests; cycle 3 ships **the convenience `Layout` overload that reads the wrap-time policy from a containing-block ComputedStyle**, closing the cycle-1/2 gap where callers manually passed 4 wrap-policy enums. Now the integrating block-layouter just passes the block's own `ComputedStyle` + the chain auto-resolves the policy bundle via `InlineTextPolicyMaterializer.ReadInlineTextPolicy()`. **Algorithm:** validate args → read `InlineTextPolicy` via the cycle-2 materializer → delegate to the cycle-1+2 explicit-args `Layout` overload. The cycle-2 materializer's cross-property folds (`word-break:break-word` → bumps overflow-wrap to Anywhere; `overflow-wrap:break-word` → folds to Anywhere; `white-space:break-spaces` → folds to Normal) all flow through the new convenience path. **Cycle 3 simplification:** policy is read from ONE containing-block style + applied uniformly. Mixed-mode descendants (`<span style="white-space:nowrap">` inside `white-space:normal` text) require per-glyph policy metadata flowing through Wrap — scheduled for cycle 3b. The cycle 3a path covers the 95% case for invoice/report content where all descendants inherit the paragraph's settings. **Cycle 3 deferrals (cycle 3b/4):** per-source-TextRun policy with per-glyph metadata (mixed inline descendants); UAX #24 script detection; RTL fragment-level reversal; `LineFragment[]` → `BoxFragment` conversion (cycle 4); bidi-aware glyph painting via Phase 4 painter integration. New tests: 7 in [`InlineLayouterCycle3Tests`](tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Phase3/InlineLayouterCycle3Tests.cs) — null arg validation, default ComputedStyle uses defaults, NoWrap suppresses wrap, OverflowWrap.Anywhere splits, WordBreak.BreakAll splits, Hyphens.Auto + Liang patterns split, word-break:break-word cross-property fold via materializer. Tests: **4043 unit / 4179 solution-wide passing** (+7 unit / +7 solution-wide over PR #39 hardening at 4036; 4 skipped). AOT/JIT byte-parity gate stays green. Active-task pointer advances to **Phase 3 Task 10 cycle 3b** — per-source-TextRun policy plumbing with per-glyph metadata for mixed inline descendants, OR Task 11 (Phase 4 painter cycle) depending on review priority.)

**Phase 3 Task 10 cycle 2 shipped — CSS property pipeline for `overflow-wrap` / `word-break` / `hyphens`** [PR #39] (historical entry, superseded by Task 10 cycle 3 above). Continues from Task 10 cycle 1 ([PR #38](https://github.com/raroche/NetPdf/pull/38) merged at `6159aca`). Cycle 1 shipped the `InlineLayouter.Layout(...)` facade with explicit wrap-policy parameters; cycle 2 ships **the CSS-property → cascade → ComputedStyle pipeline** for the three CSS Text L3 §5+§6 keyword properties that aren't yet routed through the source-gen'd CSS infrastructure. **Changes:** `src/NetPdf.Css/properties.json` adds three rows — `hyphens` (Keyword, default `manual`, inherit), `overflow-wrap` (Keyword, default `normal`, inherit), `word-break` (Keyword, default `normal`, inherit) — alphabetically inserted; `NetPdf.SourceGen` regenerates `PropertyId.OverflowWrap` / `PropertyId.WordBreak` / `PropertyId.Hyphens` constants. `src/NetPdf.Css/ComputedValues/PropertyResolvers/KeywordResolver.cs` registers admitted-keyword tables for the three new ids: `OverflowWrap` admits `normal | anywhere | break-word`; `WordBreak` admits `normal | break-all | keep-all | break-word`; `Hyphens` admits `none | manual | auto`. The `break-word` keyword for `overflow-wrap` (deprecated alias for `anywhere` per CSS Text L3 §5.1) + the legacy `word-break: break-word` (folds to `overflow-wrap: anywhere` per the spec note) are accepted by the keyword tables; the layout-side enums currently model only the live values, so cascade-level resolution stores the keyword id but the InlineLayouter mapping for these legacy aliases lands when the materializer wires up (cycle 3). **Cycle 2 deferrals (cycle 3):** per-source-TextRun policy plumbing (the integrating `InlineLayouter` reads `InlineTextPolicy` per source-TextRun's `ComputedStyle` + bundles into per-glyph metadata so mixed inline descendants like `<span style="white-space:nowrap">` inside `white-space:normal` text work correctly; cycle-2 ships only the materializer, not the full plumbing); UAX #24 script detection; RTL fragment-level reversal; `LineFragment[]` → `BoxFragment` conversion (cycle 4). Currently the keyword-id slot is the cascade source-of-truth + the `InlineTextPolicy` struct is the layout-side bundle; `InlineLayouter.Layout` still receives explicit args at cycle 2. New tests: 14 in [`KeywordResolverTests`](tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Css/ComputedValues/PropertyResolvers/KeywordResolverTests.cs) — admitted-keyword cases for each enum value of `OverflowWrap` / `WordBreak` / `Hyphens` + invalid-keyword diagnostic + ASCII case-insensitivity. Tests: **4006 unit / 4136 solution-wide passing** (+14 unit / +14 solution-wide over the post-PR-38 hardening at 3992; 4 skipped). AOT/JIT byte-parity gate stays green. **Phase 3 Task 10 cycle 1 shipped — `InlineLayouter` Itemize→Shape→Wrap facade** [PR #38] (historical entry, superseded by Task 10 cycle 2 above). Continues Task 9 from cycle 3b sub-cycle 3 ([PR #37](https://github.com/raroche/NetPdf/pull/37) merged at `90a01db` + post-merge review pass at `c7af145`). The cycle 1 ship is a thin facade — wrap-time policy passed as explicit parameters identical to `LineBuilder.Wrap`'s signature; the CSS-property pipeline (properties.json → KeywordResolver → ComputedStyle → InlineLayouter argument) lands in cycle 2. **Cycle 1 deferrals (subsequent cycles):** per-source-TextRun policy plumbing — mixed inline descendants like `<span style="white-space:nowrap">` inside `white-space:normal` text need per-glyph metadata carrying through Wrap (cycle 2); CSS property pipeline (cycle 2 — properties.json + KeywordResolver + ComputedStyle for white-space, overflow-wrap, word-break, hyphens; currently single-arg-per-pass at the LineBuilder seam); UAX #24 script detection (cycle 3); RTL fragment-level reversal (cycle 3); `LineFragment[]` → `BoxFragment` conversion + emission into `IBlockFragmentSink` (cycle 4); bidi-aware glyph painting via Phase 4 painter integration (cycle 4). **Phase 3 Task 9 cycle 3b sub-cycle 3 shipped — CSS `hyphens` + Liang auto-hyphenation** [PR #37] (historical entry, superseded by Task 10 cycle 1 above). Continues Task 9 from cycle 3b sub-cycle 2 ([PR #36](https://github.com/raroche/NetPdf/pull/36) merged at `1414f21`). New types in [`src/NetPdf.Layout/Inline/`](src/NetPdf.Layout/Inline/): [`Hyphens`](src/NetPdf.Layout/Inline/Hyphens.cs) — byte enum (None=0, Manual=1, Auto=2) per CSS Text L3 §6.1. **`LineBuilder.Wrap` updates:** new `Hyphens hyphens = Hyphens.Manual` parameter (7th positional, CSS default) + `Hyphenator? hyphenator = null` parameter (Liang engine — falls back to `EnUsHyphenation.Default` when null + Auto mode). When `hyphens != Hyphens.None`, a precomputed `hyphenationAfter[concatTotal]` boolean array marks soft-hyphen (U+00AD) positions (Manual + Auto) + Liang-pattern positions (Auto only via `Hyphenator.FindHyphenationPoints` per ASCII-letter word). The flat-build pass upgrades Prohibited boundaries to Allowed at hyphenation positions. When `hyphens == Hyphens.None`, the wrap pass actively demotes UAX #14's BA classification of U+00AD soft-hyphen to Prohibited (per §6.1: "words are not hyphenated, even if soft-hyphens explicitly suggest opportunities"). **Cycle 3b sub-cycle 3 simplifications:** visible-hyphen-on-break rendering (CSS Text L3 §6.1.1 + display-list IR — Phase 4 painter cycle); ASCII-letter-only word tokenizer for Liang patterns (UAX #29 word-segmentation deferred); en-US patterns regardless of language (per-language pattern routing scheduled for Task 10 InlineLayouter integration); `hyphenate-character`, `hyphenate-limit-chars`, `hyphenate-limit-lines`, `hyphenate-limit-zone` (CSS Text L4) deferred. **Cycle 3b complete with this ship — sub-cycles 1+2+3 cover the wrap-pass CSS-Text-L3 §3-§6 surface.** New tests: [`LineBuilderHyphenationTests`](tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Phase3/LineBuilderHyphenationTests.cs) — 10 tests covering: arg-validation (undefined Hyphens throws); Manual mode soft-hyphen breaks; None ignores soft-hyphen (active demotion); Auto soft-hyphen still works; Auto null-hyphenator falls back to EnUs default; Manual does NOT apply Liang patterns; Auto applies Liang patterns to split long word ("hyphenation"); Auto with explicit hyphenator override; Auto short word below leftMin/rightMin no hyphenation; default Wrap mode is Manual. Tests use the synthetic Latin font (no system-font dependency); Liang pattern logic is exercised via the production `EnUsHyphenation.Default` so the pattern set + word tokenizer integration is end-to-end. Tests: **3954 unit / 4084 solution-wide passing** (+10 unit / +10 solution-wide over sub-cycle 2 hardening pass at 3944; 4 skipped). AOT/JIT byte-parity gate stays green. **Phase 3 Task 9 cycle 3b sub-cycle 2 shipped — CSS `overflow-wrap` + `word-break`** [PR #36] (historical entry, superseded by Task 9 cycle 3b sub-cycle 3 above). Continues Task 9 from cycle 3b sub-cycle 1 ([PR #35](https://github.com/raroche/NetPdf/pull/35) merged at `8dc32d1` + post-merge review pass at `10f40f4`). Sub-cycle 1 shipped white-space preprocessing + Pre/NoWrap wrap-time mode; sub-cycle 2 ships **overflow-wrap + word-break** for forcing wraps when no UAX #14 candidate exists. New types in [`src/NetPdf.Layout/Inline/`](src/NetPdf.Layout/Inline/): [`OverflowWrap`](src/NetPdf.Layout/Inline/OverflowWrap.cs) — byte enum (Normal=0, Anywhere=1) per CSS Text L3 §5.1; [`WordBreak`](src/NetPdf.Layout/Inline/WordBreak.cs) — byte enum (Normal=0, BreakAll=1, KeepAll=2) per CSS Text L3 §5.2. **`LineBuilder.Wrap` updates:** new `OverflowWrap overflowWrap = OverflowWrap.Normal` + `WordBreak wordBreak = WordBreak.Normal` parameters (5th + 6th positional, before `cancellationToken`). When `wordBreak == BreakAll`, the flat-build pass upgrades every Prohibited per-glyph opportunity to Allowed (forces aggressive glyph-level wrapping). When `overflowWrap == Anywhere` AND the line would overflow AND no Allowed candidate exists in `[lineStart, cursor)`, a forced break fires at `cursor - 1` (single-glyph-wider-than-line case still emits 1 glyph and starts fresh). Both args validated up-front with descriptive `ArgumentOutOfRangeException`. **Composition rules:** OverflowWrap.Anywhere only fires under overflow + no candidate (preserves UAX #14 candidates as preferred); WordBreak.BreakAll respects Pre/NoWrap's `wrapsAtAllowed=false` rule (Pre's strict no-wrap policy wins over BreakAll). KeepAll has no observable effect for Latin/Cyrillic/Greek content (CJK semantics activate when UAX #24 lands in cycle 4). **Cycle 3b sub-cycle 2 deferrals (sub-cycle 3):** hyphenation via Liang patterns (primitives in `NetPdf.Text.Hyphenation`); `overflow-wrap: break-word` (deprecated alias for `anywhere` with subtle min-content-size differences); per-source-TextRun policy (Task 10). New tests: [`LineBuilderOverflowWrapTests`](tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Phase3/LineBuilderOverflowWrapTests.cs) — 10 tests covering: 2 arg-validation (undefined OverflowWrap + WordBreak); OverflowWrap.Normal cycle-3a-fallback overflow; OverflowWrap.Anywhere unbreakable-run forces per-glyph break; OverflowWrap.Anywhere prefers UAX #14 candidate when available (snap-back to SP, not per-glyph); WordBreak.BreakAll glyph-level wrap; WordBreak.KeepAll no-effect for Latin; NoWrap+Anywhere combo (Anywhere fires when NoWrap leaves no candidate); Pre+BreakAll (Pre's no-wrap policy wins); default Normal matches cycle-3a behavior. Tests use the synthetic Latin font (no system-font dependency). Tests: **3939 unit / 4069 solution-wide passing** (+10 unit / +10 solution-wide over sub-cycle 1's 3929; 4 skipped). AOT/JIT byte-parity gate stays green. Active-task pointer advances to **Phase 3 Task 9 cycle 3b sub-cycle 3** — hyphenation via Liang patterns + soft-hyphen support.)

**Phase 3 Task 9 cycle 3b sub-cycle 1 shipped — CSS `white-space` preprocessing + wrap-time `Pre`/`NoWrap` mode** [PR #35] (historical entry, superseded by Task 9 cycle 3b sub-cycle 2 above). Continues Task 9 from cycle 3a ([PR #34](https://github.com/raroche/NetPdf/pull/34)). Cycle 3a wrapped raw input AS-IS (no white-space preprocessing); cycle 3b sub-cycle 1 ships **CSS Text L3 §4.1 white-space processing** + wrap-time `Pre`/`NoWrap` honoring as the foundation for cycle 3b sub-cycles 2–3 (overflow-wrap, hyphenation). New types in [`src/NetPdf.Layout/Inline/`](src/NetPdf.Layout/Inline/): [`WhiteSpace`](src/NetPdf.Layout/Inline/WhiteSpace.cs) — byte enum (Normal=0, Pre=1, NoWrap=2, PreWrap=3, PreLine=4) covering the 5 most-common CSS Text L3 §3 values. `break-spaces` deferred. New static method on [`LineBuilder`](src/NetPdf.Layout/Inline/LineBuilder.cs): `PreprocessWhitespace(text, mode)` → `string` — applies CSS Text L3 §4.1 collapse / preserve rules per mode. **Algorithm:** Normal/NoWrap collapses any run of {SP, TAB, LF, CR, FF} into a single SP + strips leading/trailing whitespace; Pre/PreWrap pass through unchanged; PreLine collapses SP+TAB runs to single SP but preserves LF+CR (segment breaks) and strips end-of-line trailing SP per §4.1.2. **`LineBuilder.Wrap` updates:** new `WhiteSpace whiteSpace = WhiteSpace.Normal` parameter (4th positional, before `cancellationToken`); when mode is `Pre` or `NoWrap` the wrap loop suppresses Allowed-break wrapping (only Mandatory breaks split lines). Plus `WhiteSpace` value validated up-front with descriptive `ArgumentOutOfRangeException`. **Cycle 3b sub-cycle 1 deferrals (sub-cycles 2/3):** `overflow-wrap: anywhere` + `word-break: break-all` (sub-cycle 2 — forced break at any glyph when no candidate exists); hyphenation via Liang patterns (sub-cycle 3 — primitives already exist in `NetPdf.Text.Hyphenation`); CSS Text L3 §4.1.1 segment-break-transformation rules (CR-LF→LF normalization belongs in the HTML preprocessor, not the inline pass); preserved-tab tab-size handling for Pre mode; per-run white-space mode (cycle 3b currently applies one mode for the whole inline pass — per-source-TextRun white-space lands when InlineLayouter integrates in Task 10); `break-spaces` mode (rarely needed for v1 invoice/report content). New tests: [`LineBuilderWhitespaceTests`](tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Phase3/LineBuilderWhitespaceTests.cs) — 20 tests covering: 3 PreprocessWhitespace arg-validation (null text, undefined mode, empty text returns empty for all 5 modes); 4 Normal-mode cases (collapse consecutive spaces incl. tabs/CRLF, strip leading/trailing, pure-whitespace collapses to empty); Pre + PreWrap pass-through invariants; NoWrap collapse-like-Normal; PreLine collapse-spaces-preserve-LF + end-of-line-SP-strip + CRLF-preserved; Wrap-time NoWrap suppresses Allowed wrap (one overflowing line) but still honors Mandatory; Wrap-time Pre suppresses Allowed wrap; Wrap-time PreWrap + PreLine wrap at Allowed; Wrap-time undefined-WhiteSpace throws. Tests use the synthetic Latin font (no system-font dependency). Tests: **3917 unit / 4047 solution-wide passing** (+20 unit / +20 solution-wide over cycle 3a's review pass at 3897; 4 skipped). AOT/JIT byte-parity gate stays green. Active-task pointer advances to **Phase 3 Task 9 cycle 3b sub-cycle 2** — `overflow-wrap` + `word-break` (forced break at any glyph when no candidate exists).)

**Phase 3 Task 9 cycle 3a shipped — `LineBuilder.Wrap` UAX #14 line-break + naive greedy wrapping** [PR #34] (historical entry, superseded by Task 9 cycle 3b sub-cycle 1 above). Continues Task 9 from cycle 2 ([PR #33](https://github.com/raroche/NetPdf/pull/33)). Cycle 2 wired up shaping (step 3 of the 6-step inline pipeline); cycle 3a ships **steps 4 + 6 — UAX #14 break-opportunity scan + greedy line wrapping** as MVP. New types in [`src/NetPdf.Layout/Inline/`](src/NetPdf.Layout/Inline/): [`ShapedRunSlice`](src/NetPdf.Layout/Inline/ShapedRunSlice.cs) — readonly record struct (`ShapedRunIndex`, `GlyphStart`, `GlyphLength`, `SliceAdvance`) representing one contiguous glyph slice from a single `ShapedRun` that fits on a single line; [`LineFragment`](src/NetPdf.Layout/Inline/LineFragment.cs) — readonly record struct (`Slices[]`, `TotalAdvance`, `EndsWithMandatoryBreak`) representing one wrapped line ready for the painter. New static method on [`LineBuilder`](src/NetPdf.Layout/Inline/LineBuilder.cs): `Wrap(sourceTextRuns, shapedRuns, availableInlineSize, ct)` — returns `LineFragment[]`. **Algorithm:** rebuild concat text; run `LineBreakAlgorithm.FindBreaks` (UAX #14); flatten glyphs across all shaped runs into a `(runIdx, glyphIdxInRun, advance, opportunity)` array indexed by global glyph position; walk with two cursors (`lineStart`, `cursor`) tracking the most recent `Allowed` opportunity in `[lineStart, cursor]`; on overflow snap back to candidate + emit; on `Mandatory` (LF/CR/NEL/¶/etc.) force fragment boundary; when no candidate exists overflow is allowed (cycle 3b adds `overflow-wrap`). Each emit groups consecutive same-run glyphs into one `ShapedRunSlice`. **Cycle 3a deferrals (cycle 3b/c):** white-space variants (`pre`/`pre-wrap`/`pre-line`/`nowrap`); `overflow-wrap: anywhere` + `word-break: break-all`; hyphenation via Liang patterns (primitives already exist in `NetPdf.Text.Hyphenation`); `text-align` (start/end/center/justify); `vertical-align` baseline shifts; RTL fragment-level reversal (cycle 2 already produces RTL glyph arrays in HarfBuzz visual order; cycle 3c reverses fragment-level slice order for RTL paragraphs); UAX #24 per-run script detection; integration with `InlineLayouter` (Task 10). New tests: [`LineBuilderWrapTests`](tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Phase3/LineBuilderWrapTests.cs) — 14 tests covering empty input, 7 arg validations (null sourceTextRuns/shapedRuns + 5 inline-size cases: zero/negative/NaN/+∞), single short run fits in one line, soft-wrap on space separator (UAX #14 LB18), mandatory break at LF (LB5), long unbreakable run overflows without snap-back (no candidate fallback), multi-shaped-run line emits one slice per run, total-advance equals sum-of-slice-advances invariant, cancellation token observed at line emission. Tests use the synthetic Latin font (no system-font dependency). Tests: **3884 unit / 4014 solution-wide passing** (+14 unit / +14 solution-wide over the cycle 2 review pass's 3870; 4 skipped). AOT/JIT byte-parity gate stays green. Active-task pointer advances to **Phase 3 Task 9 cycle 3b** — white-space variants + `overflow-wrap` + hyphenation.)

**Phase 3 Task 9 cycle 2 shipped — `LineBuilder.Shape` shaping integration via `HbShaper`** [PR #33] (historical entry, superseded by Task 9 cycle 3a above). Continues Task 9 from cycle 1 (PR #32). Cycle 1 shipped steps 1+2 of the 6-step inline pipeline (bidi → itemize → shape → break-opp → measure → wrap); cycle 2 ships **step 3 — shape — plus the per-run advance measurement** half of step 5. New types in [`src/NetPdf.Layout/Inline/`](src/NetPdf.Layout/Inline/): [`ShapedRun`](src/NetPdf.Layout/Inline/ShapedRun.cs) — readonly record struct (Source ItemizedRun + ShapedGlyph[] + TotalAdvance) carrying HarfBuzz output + the run's summed inline-axis advance for cycle 3's wrap pass; [`IShaperResolver`](src/NetPdf.Layout/Inline/IShaperResolver.cs) — `IDisposable` interface that resolves an `HbShaper` for a given `ComputedStyle` (the line builder doesn't construct shapers itself; resolution + caching is an injected concern so production can ship a font-registry-backed resolver while tests can drive the line builder with a synthetic-font resolver). New static method on [`LineBuilder`](src/NetPdf.Layout/Inline/LineBuilder.cs): `Shape(sourceTextRuns, itemizedRuns, resolver, scriptIso15924="Latn", language="en")` — returns `ShapedRun[]` parallel to `itemizedRuns`. **Algorithm:** rebuild concat text from sourceTextRuns (cycle 2 trade-off: O(N) extra string copy avoids changing `Itemize`'s signature; cycle 3 may pool); for each itemized run resolve a shaper via `IShaperResolver.Resolve(style)`, slice the concat text via `Utf16Start`+`Utf16Length`, derive `ShapingDirection` from `IsRtl`, call `HbShaper.Shape(slice, direction, scriptIso15924, language)`, sum each glyph's `XAdvance` into `TotalAdvance`. **Cycle 2 deferrals (subsequent cycles):** UAX #24 per-run script detection — cycle 2 passes `scriptIso15924`+`language` uniformly to every run, cycle 3 will detect script per-run + add a script-change boundary in `Itemize`; UAX #14 line-break opportunities (cycle 3); line wrapping with `text-align`/`white-space`/`overflow-wrap`/`word-break`/`vertical-align` (cycle 3); `LineFragment[]` output (cycle 3); integration with `InlineLayouter` (Task 10); inline content flowing around floats — completes the float story from Task 8 (Task 10 + cycle 4). New tests: [`LineBuilderShapingTests`](tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Phase3/LineBuilderShapingTests.cs) — 13 tests covering empty input, 5 null-arg validations (sourceTextRuns/itemizedRuns/resolver/scriptIso15924/language), single-LTR-run roundtrip with positive XAdvance per glyph, total-advance equals sum-of-glyph-advances invariant, source-itemized-run preserved on output, multi-run inputs (one ShapedRun per ItemizedRun + glyph counts match), `Source.Utf16Start` offsets are concat-text-relative, resolver invoked once per itemized run, resolver receives correct source-style per run. Tests use a synthetic-font resolver wrapping [`SyntheticFont.Build()`](tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Text/Fonts/OpenType/SyntheticFont.cs) — no system-font dependency. (Note: `HbShaper` is sealed so the test can't intercept its `Shape` call to pin script/language/direction passthrough at the resolver layer; those invariants are deferred to integration tests in cycle 3 / Task 10 once the full pipeline can be exercised end-to-end with real glyph outputs.) Tests: **3865 unit / 3995 solution-wide passing** (+17 unit / +17 solution-wide over PR #32's 3848; 4 skipped). AOT/JIT byte-parity gate stays green.
