**Phase 3 Task 8 cycle 2 shipped — flow-around-floats + cross-fragmentainer deferral** [PR #31] (historical entry, superseded by Task 9 above). Continues Task 8 from cycle 1 (PR #30). Cycle 1 tracked floats + resolved `clear` but in-flow blocks ignored floats for sizing (visually overlapped). Cycle 2 adds [`FloatManager.GetAvailableInlineRange(blockY, containingStart, containingEnd)`](src/NetPdf.Layout/Layouters/FloatManager.cs) — returns `(InlineStart, InlineEnd)` reduced by any float whose vertical extent intersects `blockY`. Per CSS 2.2 §9.5: a non-floating block shrinks its inline-size to leave room for floats on both sides. **`BlockLayouter` updates:** the outer loop calls `GetAvailableInlineRange` at each child's hypothetical-Y; `borderBoxInlineSize` derives from `availInlineEnd - availInlineStart - margins`; the fragment's `InlineOffset` anchors at `availInlineStart + marginInlineStart` so blocks visually flow PAST left floats. **Cross-fragmentainer float deferral** per Fragmentation L3 §5: new private `WouldFloatOverflow` peek + dispatch — when a float would overflow + the page has prior emitted content, returns `PageComplete` with the float as the resume target (cross-page float per CSS Fragmentation L3 §5). Float-on-empty-page that's taller than ANY page falls back to cycle 1's emit + `PAGINATION-FORCED-OVERFLOW-001`. **Cycle 2 deferrals (subsequent cycles):** nested in-flow blocks use parent's content-area only — they don't dynamically re-query floats at their nested-Y (cycle 3); a single block ignores cycle-2's float-bottom — it doesn't widen below the float's bottom (cycle 3); float CONTAINING block alignment to nested parent vs BFC-wide (cycle 3); inline content + line-boxes flowing around floats (Phase 3 Task 9-10 LineBuilder). New tests: 9 unit tests in [`FloatManagerTests`](tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Phase3/FloatManagerTests.cs) — `GetAvailableInlineRange` left-only/right-only/both-sides/no-floats/y-above-top/y-at-bottom/stacked-floats/oversized/non-finite-rejection; 7 integration tests in [`BlockLayouterTests`](tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Phase3/BlockLayouterTests.cs) (`Task8c2_*`) — block-after-left-float/right-float/both-sides, block-past-float-bottom, trailing-float-defers-with-prior-content, oversized-float-on-empty-page-still-emits-with-diagnostic, float-with-margins-uses-margin-box-for-overflow-check, float-fits-doesn't-defer. The post-PR-30 `PostPr30_trailing_float_overflow_emits_diagnostic` test was rewritten as `PostPr30_trailing_float_overflow_when_no_prior_emission_still_diagnoses` to pin the cycle-2 fallback case (taller-than-any-page floats). Tests: **3825 unit / 3955 solution-wide passing** (+19 unit / +19 solution-wide over PR #30's 3806; 4 skipped). AOT/JIT byte-parity gate stays green. Active-task pointer advances to **Phase 3 Task 9** (`LineBuilder` — bidi/itemize/shape/break/wrap) — the keystone task for inline content. After Task 9 lands, the inline-flow-around-floats integration completes the float story.)

**Phase 3 Task 8 cycle 1 shipped — `FloatManager` scaffolding + `clear` resolution** [PR #30] (historical entry, superseded by Task 8 cycle 2 above). New types in [`src/NetPdf.Layout/Layouters/`](src/NetPdf.Layout/Layouters/): [`FloatManager`](src/NetPdf.Layout/Layouters/FloatManager.cs) — per-BFC float tracker (`PlaceFloat`, `GetClearedBlockY`, `Snapshot`/`RestoreFrom`); `FloatRecord` (placed-float record); `FloatSide` enum (Left/Right after writing-mode resolution); `ClearKind` enum (None/Left/Right/Both/InlineStart/InlineEnd matching the source-gen'd CSS keyword indices). New extensions on [`ComputedStyleLayoutExtensions`](src/NetPdf.Layout/Layouters/ComputedStyleLayoutExtensions.cs): `ReadKeywordOrDefault` (typed-keyword decode), `ReadFloatSide` (PropertyId.Float → FloatSide?), `ReadClearKind` (PropertyId.Clear → ClearKind). Cycle 1 resolves `inline-start`/`inline-end` as `left`/`right` (LTR-only assumption; cycle 3 will resolve against `LayoutContext.WritingMode` + `IsRtl`). **`BlockLayouter` integration:** new `_floatManager` field per layouter instance (one per BFC root); `AttemptLayout`'s main loop dispatches floats via the new `EmitFloat` helper before the in-flow box-model math (out-of-flow per CSS 2.2 §9.5; doesn't advance the in-flow cursor or affect the margin-collapse chain). Non-floating blocks with `clear` consult `_floatManager.GetClearedBlockY` BEFORE the resolver consult; clearance also resets the collapse chain (per §8.3.1 clearance creates a new collapse boundary). **Cycle 1 deferrals (subsequent cycles):** blocks DON'T resize around floats (cycle 2 — `GetAvailableInlineRange` + integration with the box-model inline-axis pipeline); cross-fragmentainer floats per Fragmentation L3 §5 (cycle 2); float interaction with negative margins / `shape-outside` / multi-column / abs-pos (cycle 3); inline content flowing around floats (Phase 3 Task 9-10 — needs `LineBuilder`). New tests: [`FloatManagerTests`](tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Phase3/FloatManagerTests.cs) — 28 unit tests covering `PlaceFloat` (left/right alignment, same-side stacking, opposite-side independence, arg validation), `GetClearedBlockY` (each `ClearKind` value, no-floats baseline, no-pull-below-input invariant, NaN guard), `Snapshot`/`RestoreFrom` (capture, null-restore, replay, no-aliasing, type guard); 10 integration tests in [`BlockLayouterTests`](tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Phase3/BlockLayouterTests.cs) (`Task8_*`) — left/right float emission, out-of-flow cursor independence, `clear:left|right|both`, two-stacked-left-floats, floats don't break margin-collapse chain between in-flow blocks, `inline-start` LTR resolution, clearance-resets-collapse-chain. Tests: **3798 unit / 3928 solution-wide passing** (+38 unit / +38 solution-wide over PR #29's 3760; 4 skipped). AOT/JIT byte-parity gate stays green. Active-task pointer advances to **Phase 3 Task 8 cycle 2** — block + line-box inline-size reduction around floats — OR alternatively **Phase 3 Task 9** (`LineBuilder`) if the reviewer prefers to ship inline-flow next.)

**Phase 3 Task 7 cycle 2c shipped — subtree-aware pagination (atomic MVP)** [PR #29] (historical entry, superseded by Task 8 above). Continues Task 7 from cycle 2b (PR #28). Pre-cycle-2c the outer break decision + cursor advance both used the box's OWN `borderBoxBlockSize`, so containers with overflowing block-level descendants silently clipped past the fragmentainer + subsequent siblings visually overlapped the overflow. Cycle 2c adds [`MeasureSubtreeVisualBlockExtent`](src/NetPdf.Layout/Layouters/BlockLayouter.cs) — a pre-measure pass returning the maximum block-axis extent reached by any descendant (max of own border-box + descendant bottoms, applying adjacent-margin collapse). The chunk-fit + cursor-advance both use this measured extent so: (a) oversized subtrees trigger a break-before via the resolver pushing the entire subtree to the next page atomically per CSS Fragmentation L3 §5; (b) subtrees that can't fit any page commit via the existing forced-overflow forward progress + emit `PAGINATION-FORCED-OVERFLOW-001` (pre-fix this case was silent — outer measure missed the overflow); (c) siblings AFTER an overflowing subtree are positioned past the overflow's bottom edge with no visual overlap. Non-flow block kinds (Table/Flex/Grid/Replaced) are atomic to the measure pass — only their own border-box size contributes (same `IsBlockFlowContainerOwnedByBlockLayouter` predicate gating as `EmitBlockSubtreeRecursive`). Recursion uses the existing `MaxRecursionDepth=256` DoS guard. **Cycle 2c MVP scope.** Subtrees are paginated ATOMICALLY (push wholly to next page OR forced-overflow). True mid-subtree splits — parent's first half on page 1 + parent's second half on page 2 — are deferred to **cycle 2d** with a new failing-skip pin (`Cycle2d_oversized_subtree_splits_across_two_pages_at_inner_break`). Mid-splits require recursive continuation tokens (`BlockContinuation.NestedContinuation`) + break consultation inside `EmitBlockSubtreeRecursive` + recursive resume on retry. New tests: 6 cycle 2c regression tests in [`BlockLayouterTests`](tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Phase3/BlockLayouterTests.cs) — `Cycle2c_nested_overflow_pushes_subtree_to_next_page_when_prior_content_exists` (oversized subtree after a fitting sibling triggers break-before with continuation pointing at parent), `Cycle2c_nested_overflow_on_fresh_page_emits_with_diagnostic` (subtree taller than any page commits via forced-overflow + emits diagnostic — pre-fix silent), `Cycle2c_subsequent_sibling_does_not_overlap_overflowing_subtree` (sibling after an overflowing parent positioned at parent's subtree-extent bottom, not parent's own bottom), `Cycle2c_leaf_box_subtree_extent_equals_own_border_box` (sanity — cycle 1 leaf-only behavior unchanged), `Cycle2c_subtree_extent_respects_margin_collapse_between_nested_siblings` (collapse applied during the measure pass), `Cycle2c_subtree_extent_treats_table_as_atomic_using_own_height` (Table/Flex/Grid/Replaced not recursed into). The cycle 2c deferral pin from cycle 2b is now ACTIVATED + replaced by the 6 explicit tests above. Tests: **3755 unit / 3885 solution-wide passing** (+6 unit / +6 solution-wide over PR #28's 3749; 4 skipped — the 2 cycle-3 deferral pins + 1 capture harness + the new cycle-2d deferral pin; the cycle-2c pin is now removed). AOT/JIT byte-parity gate stays green. Active-task pointer advances to **Phase 3 Task 7 cycle 2d** — true mid-subtree pagination splits — OR alternatively to **Phase 3 Task 8** (`FloatManager`) if the reviewer prefers to ship the float interaction next.)

**Phase 3 Task 7 cycle 2b shipped — recursive nested-block layout** [PR #28] (historical entry, superseded by cycle 2c above). Continues Task 7 from cycle 2 (PR #26). Cycles 1 + 2 walked `_rootBox.Children` only; a `div > p` tree emitted only the `div` fragment. Cycle 2b adds [`EmitBlockSubtreeRecursive`](src/NetPdf.Layout/Layouters/BlockLayouter.cs) — a private helper that walks each emitted child's block-level descendants + emits a `BoxFragment` for each at correctly nested offsets relative to the parent's content area. The recursion runs from BOTH the Continue path + the forced-overflow path, so nested descendants render even when the outer block is forced through overflow forward-progress. Adjacent-margin collapse (§8.3.1 — same `MarginCollapse.Collapse` helper used by the outer loop) is applied between nested siblings; non-block children still break adjacency. **Cycle 2b deferrals (still — to subsequent commits):** auto-height resolution per §10.6.3 (cycle 3 — `ReadLengthPxOrZero` returns 0 for auto so a container with `height: auto` + children renders with a 0-sized parent fragment but the children still emit at correct offsets); cross-subtree pagination splits (cycle 2c — currently each top-level subtree is atomic for pagination); parent / first-child margin collapse + BFC root suppression (cycle 3 — needs BFC detection); logical-axis property reads (cycle 3); width/height auto resolution (cycle 3). New tests in [`BlockLayouterTests`](tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Phase3/BlockLayouterTests.cs): `Cycle2b_layouter_emits_fragments_for_nested_block_descendants` (div > p → 2 fragments), `Cycle2b_layouter_recurses_through_three_levels` (root > section > article > h1 → 3 fragments at correctly nested offsets), `Cycle2b_nested_children_apply_inline_offsets_inside_parent_padding` (child's InlineOffset = parent contentLeft + child marginLeft), `Cycle2b_nested_siblings_apply_margin_collapse` (two block siblings inside a parent → collapse applies), `Cycle2b_nested_non_block_children_are_skipped` (TextRun siblings are silently skipped, only the block sibling emits). The cycle-2 deferral pin `Cycle2_Layouter_lays_out_nested_block_descendants` is now ACTIVATED + replaced by these 5 explicit tests. Tests: **3741 unit / 3871 solution-wide passing** (+8 unit / +8 solution-wide over PR #27's 3733; 3 skipped — the 2 cycle-3 deferral pins + 1 capture harness; the cycle-2 nested-recursive-layout pin is now removed). AOT/JIT byte-parity gate stays green. Active-task pointer advances to **Phase 3 Task 7 cycle 2c** — cross-subtree pagination splits — OR alternatively to **Phase 3 Task 8** (`FloatManager`) if the reviewer prefers to ship the float interaction next.)

**Phase 3 Task 7 cycle 2 shipped — adjacent-sibling margin collapse per CSS 2.1 §8.3.1** (historical entry, superseded by cycle 2b above). Continues Task 7 from cycle 1 (PR #22). Cycle 1 laid out blocks by SUMMING adjacent margins (`marginEnd_N + marginStart_{N+1}`); CSS 2.1 §8.3.1 specifies these must COLLAPSE to a single margin per the formula `max(positives) - max(absolute values of negatives)`. **New types:** [`MarginCollapse`](src/NetPdf.Layout/Layouters/MarginCollapse.cs) — pure-static `Collapse(m1, m2)` helper implementing the spec formula. Commutative + tested in isolation; will be shared across `BlockLayouter` + future `FlexLayouter` / `GridLayouter` / `TableLayouter` collapse paths. **`BlockLayouter` updates:** introduces `prevBlockMarginEnd` + `isFirstBlockOnPage` state per attempt; for each block child, computes `effectiveTopGap` (= `marginStart` for first block, else `MarginCollapse.Collapse(prevBlockMarginEnd, marginStart)`) + `topShift` (= `effectiveTopGap` for first, else `effectiveTopGap - prevBlockMarginEnd`); the `BlockOffset` of the emitted fragment becomes `fragmentainer.UsedBlockSize + topShift`. The `marginBoxBlockSize` (drives `chunkBlockSize` for the resolver's fit-check) now uses `topShift`-not-`marginStart` so collapse is reflected in pagination accounting. **Cross-page collapse suppression** per CSS Fragmentation L3 §6.1 — the layouter resets the collapse chain on each page entry: `prevBlockMarginEnd = 0` + `isFirstBlockOnPage = true` at `AttemptLayout` entry, so the first block on a fresh page applies its FULL marginTop without collapsing across the page break. **Cycle 2 deferrals (still — to subsequent commits):** parent/first-child + parent/last-child collapse (cycle 3 — needs recursive layout + BFC detection); BFC root suppression (cycle 3 — needs `display: flow-root` / `overflow` / float / abs-pos detection); empty-box collapse (cycle 3 — synthetic empty-box path); recursive nested-block layout (cycle 2b — separate commit); logical-axis property reads (cycle 3); width/height auto resolution (cycle 3). New tests: [`MarginCollapseTests`](tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Phase3/MarginCollapseTests.cs) — 24 theory cases covering both-positive, both-negative, mixed-sign, zero-with-negative, commutativity, idempotence on equal margins, plus extreme-magnitude cases. Updated [`BlockLayouterTests`](tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Phase3/BlockLayouterTests.cs) — 6 new collapse-specific tests (positive-positive max, mixed-sign difference, both-negative most-negative, three-block collapse chain, cross-page first-block-uses-full-marginTop, single-block-no-phantom-collapse) + 2 existing test math updates (`Layouter_stacks_multiple_blocks_with_collapse` rename + offset 220 instead of 225; `Layouter_returns_PageComplete_when_next_block_overflows` cumulative now 490 instead of 500 — the 10px savings is the collapse). The cycle-2 deferral pin `Cycle2_Layouter_collapses_adjacent_margins` is now ACTIVATED by the new tests; the cycle-2 nested-recursive-layout pin remains skipped until cycle 2b ships. Tests: **3699 unit / 3830 solution-wide passing** (+27 unit / +27 solution-wide over cycle 1's 3672; 4 skipped including the 3 cycle-2/3 deferral pins still active). AOT/JIT byte-parity gate stays green. Active-task pointer advances to **Phase 3 Task 7 cycle 2b** — recursive nested-block layout (or, if reviewer prefers, ship cycle 2 standalone + open cycle 2b as a separate PR).)

**Phase 3 Task 7 cycle 1 shipped — BlockLayouter scaffolding + project-reference flip** (historical entry, superseded by cycle 2 above). Per the Phase 3 plan §"BlockLayouter" — the first real layouter implementing [`ILayouter`](src/NetPdf.Paginate/ILayouter.cs). Walks the block-level children of a root [`Box`](src/NetPdf.Layout/Boxes/Box.cs), stacks them vertically, consults the [`IBreakResolver`](src/NetPdf.Paginate/IBreakResolver.cs) at every block boundary, emits [`BoxFragment`](src/NetPdf.Layout/Layouters/BoxFragment.cs) into an [`IBlockFragmentSink`](src/NetPdf.Layout/Layouters/IBlockFragmentSink.cs) as each box is positioned. **Project-reference flip:** pre-Task-7 [`NetPdf.Paginate.csproj`](src/NetPdf.Paginate/NetPdf.Paginate.csproj) referenced [`NetPdf.Layout.csproj`](src/NetPdf.Layout/NetPdf.Layout.csproj) — but the reference was DEAD (Paginate never used any Layout types). Per the file layout in [CLAUDE.md](CLAUDE.md) layouters live in `NetPdf.Layout` + must implement `ILayouter` from `NetPdf.Paginate` — requiring `Layout → Paginate`, not the reverse. Cycle 1 flips the dependency: Paginate becomes a leaf-ish node (depends only on the facade for the diagnostic parity test); Layout depends on Paginate so layouters can implement `ILayouter` + consume `IBreakResolver` / `FragmentainerContext` / `LayoutCheckpoint` directly. **New types in [`src/NetPdf.Layout/Layouters/`](src/NetPdf.Layout/Layouters/):** [`BoxFragment`](src/NetPdf.Layout/Layouters/BoxFragment.cs) (record struct: Box + InlineOffset + BlockOffset + InlineSize + BlockSize; the layouter's per-box output, ready for Phase 4's painter); [`IBlockFragmentSink`](src/NetPdf.Layout/Layouters/IBlockFragmentSink.cs) (extends `NetPdf.Paginate.IFragmentSink` from Task 5 — `Emit(fragment)` + `Cursor` + `RollbackTo(cursor)` for rewind support); [`ComputedStyleLayoutExtensions`](src/NetPdf.Layout/Layouters/ComputedStyleLayoutExtensions.cs) (decodes typed `ComputedSlot` payloads — cycle 1 covers resolved-px lengths only; cycle 3 will add percentage resolution + auto handling per CSS 2.1 §10.3); [`BlockLayouter`](src/NetPdf.Layout/Layouters/BlockLayouter.cs) (the layouter itself). **Cycle 1 algorithm:** for each block-level child, read margin / padding / border / height as CSS px (auto + percentage default to 0 — cycle 3 wires real resolution); compute margin-box block-axis extent; consult resolver via `BreakOpportunity.Block`; on `Continue` emit fragment + advance `fragmentainer.UsedBlockSize`; on `BreakHere` return `LayoutAttemptOutcome.PageComplete` with `BlockContinuation(ResumeAtChild, ConsumedBlockSize)`; on `Rewind` propagate `LayoutAttemptOutcome.NeedsRewind` with the named checkpoint. Inline / atomic children skipped (Task 10 `InlineLayouter` will handle them). **Cycle 1 deferrals (subsequent commits on this branch):** margin collapsing per CSS 2.1 §8.3.1 (cycle 2); BFC root detection + intrinsic sizing modes (cycle 3); width/height auto resolution per §10.3.3 + §10.6.2 (cycle 3); percentage resolution against containing-block (cycle 3); float interaction (Phase 3 Task 8); avoid-break / break-inside metadata extraction from ComputedStyle (cycle 3 wires the `BreakInside` / `BreakBefore` / `BreakAfter` properties through to `BreakOpportunity` flags). New [`BlockLayouterTests`](tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Phase3/BlockLayouterTests.cs) — 12 tests covering: single block fits + emits fragment with correct offset/size; inline-axis offset uses MarginLeft + size uses ContentInlineSize - margins; multi-block stacking with correct sequential block-axis offsets; page-break dispatch when next block overflows + `BlockContinuation` shape; resume-from-continuation on the second page; non-block children silently skipped; empty root returns `AllDone`; constructor null-arg validation; `OperationCanceledException` thrown when token fires; force-break dispatch via custom resolver; `IBlockFragmentSink.Cursor` increments on emit + `RollbackTo` truncates. Tests: **3660 unit / 3791 solution-wide passing** (+12 unit / +12 solution-wide over Task 5's 3648 baseline; 1 skipped). AOT/JIT byte-parity gate stays green. Active-task pointer advances to **Phase 3 Task 7 cycle 2** — margin collapsing per CSS 2.1 §8.3.1.)

**Phase 3 Task 5 shipped — bounded retry coordinator + 6-recommendation review pass + 2 Copilot fixes** (historical entry, superseded by Task 7 above). Per the Phase 3 plan §"Re-layout loop discipline" + Task 5's spec — the orchestrator that drives an [`ILayouter`](src/NetPdf.Paginate/ILayouter.cs) through up to 2 retries with progressively-relaxed [`LayoutAttemptStrategy`](src/NetPdf.Paginate/ILayouter.cs) (Strict → DropAvoidInside → LastResort), emitting [`PAGINATION-FORCED-OVERFLOW-001`](docs/diagnostics-codes.md) when the LastResort attempt fires. **New types in [`src/NetPdf.Paginate/`](src/NetPdf.Paginate/):** [`ILayouter`](src/NetPdf.Paginate/ILayouter.cs) (the layouter-facing contract real layouters implement in Tasks 7+); `LayoutAttemptResult` (record struct with `Outcome` + `Continuation` + `RewindTo` + `Cost` + factory helpers `PageComplete` / `AllDone` / `NeedsRewind`); `LayoutAttemptOutcome` enum (`PageComplete` / `AllDone` / `NeedsRewind`); `LayoutAttemptStrategy` enum (`Strict` / `DropAvoidInside` / `LastResort`); [`LayoutRetryCoordinator`](src/NetPdf.Paginate/LayoutRetryCoordinator.cs) (`MaxRetries=2` per the plan's bound; `Run(layouter, fragmentainer, ref layout, resolver)` returns the layouter's terminal result, never `NeedsRewind` to its caller). **New diagnostic infrastructure in [`src/NetPdf.Paginate/Diagnostics/`](src/NetPdf.Paginate/Diagnostics/):** [`PaginateDiagnostic`](src/NetPdf.Paginate/Diagnostics/PaginateDiagnostic.cs) (record struct mirroring `NetPdf.Diagnostic`); `PaginateDiagnosticSeverity` enum (`Info` / `Warning` / `Error`); [`PaginateDiagnosticCodes`](src/NetPdf.Paginate/Diagnostics/PaginateDiagnosticCodes.cs) (string constants — the diagnostic-codes parity test verifies these match the facade's `NetPdf.DiagnosticCodes.PAGINATION-*`); [`IPaginateDiagnosticsSink`](src/NetPdf.Paginate/Diagnostics/IPaginateDiagnosticsSink.cs) (interface — same pattern as `NetPdf.Css.Diagnostics.ICssDiagnosticsSink`, kept inside Paginate so the assembly doesn't reference the public facade). **Algorithm:** for-loop over `attempt ∈ [0..MaxRetries]`; map attempt to strategy via `AttemptToStrategy`; emit `PAGINATION-FORCED-OVERFLOW-001` BEFORE the LastResort attempt runs (so consumers see the warning even if the layouter has issues); call `layouter.AttemptLayout(fragmentainer, ref layout, resolver, strategy)`; if outcome is not `NeedsRewind`, return; otherwise `RewindTo.RestoreInto(fragmentainer, ref layout)` (per Phase 3 Task 4 review fix #6 the restore reseats `layout.Fragmentainer` if a speculative swap occurred) + advance to next attempt. Defensive: a layouter contract violation (returning `NeedsRewind` on the LastResort attempt) is caught + escalated to a synthetic `PageComplete` rather than infinite-looping. New [`LayoutRetryCoordinatorTests`](tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Phase3/LayoutRetryCoordinatorTests.cs) — 22 tests covering: `AttemptToStrategy` mapping (5 theory cases including saturation past `MaxRetries`); trivial PageComplete + AllDone (no retries, no diagnostic emission); single-retry success; double-retry success with diagnostic emitted at LastResort; layouter contract violation defense (LastResort still returning `NeedsRewind`); null-sink handling; diagnostic message includes page index; checkpoint restoration via a `StateMutatingMockLayouter` that mutates state on attempt 0 + verifies state is restored on attempt 1; null-arg validation (using try/catch since `ref LayoutContext` can't cross lambda boundaries); `LayoutAttemptResult` factory helpers; `PaginateDiagnosticCodes` string-literal pinning + parity check with facade's `NetPdf.DiagnosticCodes`. **PR #21 review pass — 6 user recommendations + 2 Copilot inline fixes** (a59365e + b9c…): (1) **NeedsRewind requires non-null RewindTo** — `LayoutAttemptResult.ValidateOrThrow` enforces the invariant; coordinator throws `InvalidOperationException` rather than silently retrying from dirty state; the `NeedsRewind` factory is non-nullable so direct construction with null is impossible. (2) **Fragmentainer sync after restore** — coordinator now reassigns its local `fragmentainer` from `layout.Fragmentainer` after every `RestoreInto`, so the next `AttemptLayout` receives the captured (post-speculative-swap-undo) instance. (3) **Fragment-output rollback** — new optional `IFragmentSink` interface; coordinator calls `RollbackTo(checkpoint.FragmentOutputCursor)` on rewind so layouters that emit fragments incrementally can discard them. Layouters that emit only on `PageComplete` leave the sink null. (4) **`IBreakResolver : IDisposable`** — both `BreakResolver` + `OptimizingBreakResolver` implement `Dispose()` returning the final held lease via the lease-token CAS. The integrating layout pipeline drives via `using var resolver = ...`. (5) **Wire `PAGINATION-OPTIMIZER-FALLBACK-001`** — `OptimizingBreakResolver` constructor now accepts an optional `IPaginateDiagnosticsSink`; emits the diagnostic on every batched fallback (with the `FallbackReason` from `OptimizerResult`). Closes the gap where future layouters could silently drop the diagnostic by forgetting to inspect `FellBackToGreedy`. (6) **`CancellationToken` threaded through** — `LayoutRetryCoordinator.Run` + `ILayouter.AttemptLayout` accept a token (default `None`); coordinator checks it before each attempt + layouters check inside long-running inner loops. Mock layouters in tests propagate the token. (7) **Original-page-index in diagnostic** — coordinator captures `fragmentainer.PageIndex` at entry so the forced-overflow message reports the page that originally had problems (rather than 0 after restoration). (8) [Copilot] XML doc on `LayoutAttemptResult.PageComplete` no longer says "zero cost" — accepts any non-negative cost. Tests updated for the new `ILayouter` signature (added `CancellationToken`); 17 new regression tests covering: invariant violation throws, Fragmentainer sync after restore, `RollbackTo` called with captured cursor, two-rewind rollback sequencing, no-rollback when fragmentSink null, resolver `Dispose` returns held lease, `using var resolver` releases on scope exit, `OptimizingBreakResolver` emits fallback diagnostic on `FellBackToGreedy`, no-emit-when-no-fallback, null-sink-no-throw, cancellation before first attempt, cancellation between retries, `PageComplete` non-zero cost. Tests: **3648 unit / 3779 solution-wide passing** (+18 unit / +18 solution-wide over the cycle-1 baseline of 3630; 1 skipped). AOT/JIT byte-parity gate stays green.

Tests: **3648 unit / 3779 solution-wide passing**. AOT/JIT byte-parity gate stays green. Active-task pointer advances to **Phase 3 — Fragmentainer-aware layout + pagination** (Tasks 6-30 ahead — `LayoutContext ref struct` was already shipped with Task 1, so Task 7 `BlockLayouter` is next; followed by `FloatManager`, `LineBuilder`, `InlineLayouter`, `TableLayouter`, `MulticolLayouter`, `FlexLayouter`, `GridLayouter`, `AbsoluteLayouter`, @page rules, page-margin boxes, generated content, W3C conformance integration, performance tuning, `0.7.0-beta` tag).)

**Phase 3 Task 4 shipped — bounded DP optimizer + 7-recommendation review pass + 8 Copilot inline fixes** (historical entry, superseded by Task 5 above). Per the Phase 3 plan §"Bounded DP optimizer" — replaces the Task 1 greedy stub with a real cost-minimizing implementation, then hardened with the user's 7 review recommendations + Copilot's 8 inline comments. **Cycle 1 — bounded DP optimizer.** New types in [`src/NetPdf.Paginate/`](src/NetPdf.Paginate/): [`Optimizer`](src/NetPdf.Paginate/Optimizer.cs) (Knuth-Plass-style sliding-window DP with 2-page lookahead — at each page boundary enumerate `(b1, b2)` candidate pairs minimizing `Score(b1) + Score(b2)`, commit `b1` only, slide forward); [`OptimizerResult`](src/NetPdf.Paginate/OptimizerResult.cs) (record carrying `BreakIndices` + `TotalCost` + `FellBackToGreedy` + `FallbackReason`); [`OptimizingBreakResolver`](src/NetPdf.Paginate/OptimizingBreakResolver.cs) (production `IBreakResolver`, delegates batched to `Optimizer.Optimize`, streaming degrades to greedy). [`IBreakResolver`](src/NetPdf.Paginate/IBreakResolver.cs) extended with `ResolveBreaks(opportunities, ctx)`; greedy [`BreakResolver`](src/NetPdf.Paginate/BreakResolver.cs) Task-1 stub gets matching impl. **Cycle 2 — 7 review recommendations + 8 Copilot inline comments.** (1) [Rec #1 + Copilot #2 + Copilot #6] **Terminal-break semantics fix** — pre-fix the DP committed at least one break for any non-empty input even when the entire remainder fit on one page. New early-exit: if the tail past `pageStart` fits on a single fragmentainer AND no forced break is reachable, commit no break. (2) [Rec #2 + Copilot #1 + Copilot #8] **Page-local cost scoring** — added `pageStart` parameter (default 0) to [`CostModel.Score`](src/NetPdf.Paginate/CostModel.cs); the trailing-blank ratio now computes against `(opportunity.UsedBlockSize - pageStart)`, recovering correct per-page measurements when the optimizer batches across pages. Coordinate-space contract clarified in `IBreakResolver` XML doc — streaming uses per-fragmentainer `UsedBlockSize`, batched uses cumulative-across-window. (3) [Rec #3] **Per-window DP budget caps** — new `MaxCandidatesPerPage = 256` (single-page candidate cap) + `MaxPairEvaluations = 65_536` (cumulative pair-evaluation budget across the run); either trip falls back to greedy. Pathological inputs (1000 zero-height candidates piling onto one page) now degrade gracefully rather than blowing the O(k²) inner loop. (4) [Rec #4] **Forced-break tightening** — when an author-forced break is reachable on the current page, commit at exactly its position without running `(b1, b2)` optimization. Section-boundary rewards no longer insert extra earlier breaks before a forced break. (5) [Rec #5] **Paragraph-aware widow scoring** — new `ParagraphId` field on `BreakOpportunity` (default 0); the optimizer counts subsequent same-`ParagraphId` line opportunities for accurate `lineCountAfterBreak` widow scoring. Layouters that don't supply `ParagraphId` get a heuristic fallback counting consecutive `LineBoundary` opportunities. (6) [Rec #6] **`LayoutContext.Fragmentainer` restoration** — [`LayoutCheckpoint.Capture`](src/NetPdf.Paginate/LayoutCheckpoint.cs) now snapshots `layout.Fragmentainer` into a new `CapturedFragmentainerRef` field; `RestoreInto` reseats `layout.Fragmentainer` back to it on rewind. Pre-fix a speculative attempt that swapped to a cloned fragmentainer left `layout.Fragmentainer` pointing at the discarded clone after restore. (7) [Rec #7] **Lease-token pool ownership** — [`LayoutCheckpointPool`](src/NetPdf.Paginate/LayoutCheckpoint.cs) now stamps a unique lease token (via `Interlocked.Increment` on a `long` counter) onto each rented checkpoint; `Return` uses an atomic CAS to compare the caller's lease token against the checkpoint's currently-stamped value. Stale-after-rerent + immediate double-return + concurrent multi-thread Returns are all rejected by a single mechanism — replacing the prior `ConcurrentDictionary<LayoutCheckpoint, byte> _inPool` belt-and-suspenders. New `CheckpointLease` readonly struct wraps the rented checkpoint + the token; `IBreakResolver.RegisterCheckpoint(CheckpointLease)` propagates the lease through the resolver-internal Return path. (8) [Copilot #3, #4, #5] **Single-chunk-too-tall detection** — `CostModel.Score` adds `BreakInsideAvoidViolation` penalty when `ChunkBlockSize > contentBlockSize` regardless of position; greedy fallback in `Optimizer` + `BreakResolver.ResolveBreaks` also commit + apply the overflow cost when a chunk on a fresh page (`pageSoFar == 0`) exceeds the fragmentainer extent. (9) [Copilot #7] **PROGRESS.md duplicate "Last updated" fixed** — only the topmost entry now has the prefix; historical entries demoted to bare paragraphs. New [`PaginationOptimizerTests`](tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Phase3/PaginationOptimizerTests.cs) — **60 tests** (+24 over cycle 1) covering: cycle-1 scenarios (forced/avoid/overflow/multi-page/section-boundary/streaming/lease-mgmt/null-arg), the new terminal-break semantics (single-fitting + multi-fitting return empty), page-local scoring (`pageStart` validation + recovery), `ChunkBlockSize > page` (cost-model + DP + greedy), paragraph-aware widow scoring, forced-break-displacement-by-section-reward defense, unreachable-forced-break later-iteration commit, per-page cap fallback, pair-eval-budget fallback, fragmentainer restoration after speculative swap, capture stamps `CapturedFragmentainerRef`, stale-lease rejection after re-rent, double-return rejection via lease token, default-lease no-op, `using`-block dispose, lease-token uniqueness, cumulative-`UsedBlockSize` end-to-end. Foundation tests updated for the lease API throughout. Tests: **3599 unit / 3729 solution-wide passing** (+24 unit over cycle-1's 3575; 1 skipped). AOT/JIT byte-parity gate stays green. Active-task pointer advances to **Phase 3 — Fragmentainer-aware layout + pagination** (Tasks 5-30 ahead — re-layout loop with bounded retry, BlockLayouter, FloatManager, InlineLayouter, TableLayouter, MulticolLayouter, FlexLayouter, GridLayouter, AbsoluteLayouter, @page rules, page-margin boxes, generated content, W3C conformance integration, performance tuning, `0.7.0-beta` tag).)

**Phase 3 Task 1 shipped — pagination foundation** (historical entry, superseded by Task 4 above). Per the Phase 3 plan's strong emphasis on "build the paginator first" the first PR delivers the layouter-facing interfaces every later layouter consumes: [`FragmentainerContext`](src/NetPdf.Paginate/FragmentainerContext.cs) (per-page state — page index, content-area dimensions, used height, named-string carry-forward); [`IBreakResolver`](src/NetPdf.Paginate/IBreakResolver.cs) + [`BreakDecision`](src/NetPdf.Paginate/BreakDecision.cs) + [`BreakAction`](src/NetPdf.Paginate/BreakAction.cs) + [`BreakOpportunity`](src/NetPdf.Paginate/BreakOpportunity.cs) + `BreakOpportunityClass` (the layouter↔paginator API surface); [`LayoutCheckpoint`](src/NetPdf.Paginate/LayoutCheckpoint.cs) + `LayoutCheckpointPool` (mutable + pooled, ConcurrentBag with 64-instance soft cap matching the Phase 2 ComputedStyle pattern); [`LayoutContinuation`](src/NetPdf.Paginate/LayoutContinuation.cs) hierarchy (`BlockContinuation` / `InlineContinuation` / `TableContinuation` / `FlexContinuation` / `GridContinuation`); [`LayoutContext`](src/NetPdf.Paginate/LayoutContext.cs) ref struct (containing-block dimensions + writing mode + bidi block-direction + counter map; lazy-allocated counter dict so a layout pass that doesn't use author counters pays zero allocation); [`WritingMode`](src/NetPdf.Paginate/WritingMode.cs) enum (`HorizontalTb` / `VerticalRl` / `VerticalLr` — sideways-rl/lr emit the existing `CSS-WRITING-MODE-SIDEWAYS-UNSUPPORTED-001`); [`CostModel`](src/NetPdf.Paginate/CostModel.cs) with documented penalty constants from the Phase 3 plan's table (`BreakInsideAvoidViolation = 1_000_000`, `StrandedHeading = 1000`, `Orphan = 500`, `Widow = 500`, `FlexOrGridLineSplit = 400`, `TableRowMidCellSplit = 300`, `LargeBlankTrailingArea = 200`, `SectionBoundaryReward = -100`); [`BreakResolver`](src/NetPdf.Paginate/BreakResolver.cs) Task-1 stub implementation that always picks Continue when the next chunk fits + BreakHere when it doesn't (greedy; the bounded DP optimizer replaces this in Task 4). New diagnostic codes [`PAGINATION-OPTIMIZER-FALLBACK-001`](docs/diagnostics-codes.md) (Info) + [`PAGINATION-FORCED-OVERFLOW-001`](docs/diagnostics-codes.md) (Warning) wired to the registry. New [`PaginationFoundationTests`](tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Phase3/PaginationFoundationTests.cs) — 23 tests covering FragmentainerContext clone/named-string carry-forward, LayoutCheckpoint pool rent-reset semantics + null-Return safety, LayoutContext counter lazy alloc + IncrementCounter + Read-default-zero, the full CostModel penalty matrix (BreakInsideAvoid effectively-infinite + SectionBoundary negative-reward + Orphan / Widow / TableRowMidCell / LargeBlankTrailing + clean-block-boundary-zero-cost), BreakResolver Continue/BreakHere/RegisterCheckpoint/GetLastCheckpoint + custom-orphan/widow override, BreakDecision.Continue singleton, and continuation-record value-equality. Tests: **3506 unit / solution-wide passing** (+23 over Phase D's 3483; 1 skipped). AOT/JIT byte-parity gate stays green. Active-task pointer remains **Phase 3 — Fragmentainer-aware layout + pagination** (Tasks 4-30 ahead — DP optimizer, BlockLayouter, InlineLayouter, FloatManager, TableLayouter, MulticolLayouter, FlexLayouter, GridLayouter, AbsoluteLayouter, @page rules, page-margin boxes, string()/element()/counter() generated content, W3C conformance integration, performance tuning, `0.7.0-beta` tag.

Phase A security hardening shipped — pre-Phase-3 hardening pass addressing 8 high-confidence findings from the dedicated HTML-to-PDF security audit (Neodyme html-renderer-to-RCE, Intigriti SSRF guide, DomPDF @font-face RCE, Apryse argument-injection, Stirling-PDF SSRF, hacktricks dynamic-PDF survey, libwebp CVE-2023-4863, HarfBuzz CVE-2024-56732 + cycle-2 backlog). All 8 land before Phase 3 builds layout on top of the Phase 2 surface. (1) [SEC] **A-1 widened HTML URL strip** — [`HtmlParsingHost.StripJavaScriptUrls`](src/NetPdf/HtmlParsingHost.cs) cycle 1 only covered `<a href>` / `<area href>` / `xlink:href`; the deep-review threat model + the DomPDF / Apryse / EvoPDF CVE survey confirm that `<form action>`, `<iframe src>`, `<object data>`, `<embed src>`, `<base href>`, and `<meta http-equiv="refresh" content="0;url=...">` all reach a sink that interprets URLs in real-world engines. New `StripDangerousUrlOnAttribute` helper covers all 6 attribute paths; recognized schemes widened from `javascript:` to also include `vbscript:` (legacy IE) and `data:` (the standard SSRF/XSS sneak path). One `HTML-JAVASCRIPT-URL-IGNORED-001` per stripped attribute. Safe `https:` / `http:` URLs pass through unchanged — Phase 5's `IResourceLoader` is the right control point for those once fetching is wired. (2) [SEC] **A-2 event-handler attribute strip** — `on*`-prefixed attributes (`onclick`, `onload`, `onerror`, `onmouseover`, etc.) stripped from every element with new `HTML-EVENT-HANDLER-IGNORED-001` (Info severity). Cycle 1's documented decision was "leave in place because PDF readers can't dispatch them"; the deep review reversed this — Phase 5's PDF/UA tagged-structure emission could surface attribute values into accessibility metadata, where dispatch becomes the consumer's problem. ASCII case-insensitive match catches `OnClick` / `ONLOAD` etc. (3) [SEC] **A-3 cumulative `var()` expansion budget per element** — [`VarSubstitution.Substitute`](src/NetPdf.Css/Cascade/VarSubstitution.cs) cycle 1's `MaxOutputLength = 1 MiB` was a per-CALL cap; `VarResolver` calls Substitute repeatedly per element (once per custom property + once per non-custom declaration), so N properties each near the cap totaled N MiB. New `VarSubstitution.Budget` class threaded through every Substitute call sharing the same element; default 10 MiB per element. Charge the final output length against the budget; on exhaustion emit `CSS-VAR-EXPANSION-LIMIT-001` once + return Invalid for this and subsequent calls. Pseudos on the same element share the budget (otherwise an attacker could amplify by 5–10× via `::before`/`::after`/`::marker`/`::first-line`/`::first-letter`). (4) [SEC] **A-4 nested at-rule depth limit** — [`CascadeResolver.CollectFromRules`](src/NetPdf.Css/Cascade/CascadeResolver.cs) cycle 1 had no depth bound on `@media` / `@supports` / `@layer` / `@import` recursion; a stylesheet with 1000 nested `@media` rules would blow the stack. New `MaxAtRuleNestingDepth = 32` constant; threaded through `CollectAtRule`, `CollectLayerAtRule`, `CollectImportRule`. On excess nesting emit `CSS-AT-RULE-UNKNOWN-001` once + return cleanly. (5) [SEC] **A-5 `CssContentList` output cap** — generated content from `::before` / `::after` / `::marker` is rendered into the output PDF; without a cap, an attacker can bloat the box tree + downstream PDF via `<span data-x="...10MB...">` + `::before { content: attr(data-x) attr(data-x) attr(data-x) }`. New `MaxContentOutputChars = 64 KiB` cap with `TryAppendBounded` helper; on overflow emit `CSS-CONTENT-FUNCTION-UNSUPPORTED-001` + the pseudo generates no box. (6) [SEC] **A-6 factored `DiagnosticTextSanitizer`** — central utility for sanitizing untrusted text fragments before they flow into `CssDiagnostic.Message`. Originally inlined in `CascadeResolver` (deep review C-2 selector ANSI-injection defense); centralizing prevents drift across 8+ emission sites. Strips C0 (0x00..0x1F) + DEL (0x7F) + C1 (0x80..0x9F) → U+FFFD; truncates at 120 chars + appends ellipsis. Applied at: `CascadeResolver` selector-parse warnings (already done), `ColorResolver.EmitInvalid` + `LengthResolver.EmitInvalid` (untrusted property values), `CssContentList.Truncate` (now delegates to the central util). (7) [SEC] **A-7 `SourceLocation.File` path normalization** — `PublicDiagnosticsSinkAdapter.ConvertLocation` was passing the host-supplied `BaseUri` verbatim into the diagnostic; an absolute filesystem path like `file:///C:/Users/Foo/secret/index.html` leaked host filesystem topology. New `DiagnosticTextSanitizer.SanitizeFilePath` reduces absolute paths to basename; sentinels (`<inline>`, `<unknown>`, `about:blank`) + `https:` / `http:` URLs pass through unchanged. (8) [SEC] **A-8 per-stylesheet selector-parse-warning budget cap** — new `SelectorParseWarningBudgetSink` decorator throttles `CSS-PARSE-WARNING-001` to 100 per stylesheet + emits one summary diagnostic when the cap is exceeded. A hostile CSS with thousands of broken selectors otherwise floods the consumer's sink (CI logs, structured-log infrastructure, etc.); the cap keeps the signal intact (first 100 still surfaced) while silencing the spam tail. Other diagnostic codes pass through unbudgeted. New tests: **+24 unit** in [`PhaseASecurityHardeningTests`](tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Phase2/PhaseASecurityHardeningTests.cs) — 5 theory cases for A-1 (one per extended attribute), 2 facts for A-1 data: + meta-refresh + a passthrough check, 6 theory + 1 fact for A-2 (case-insensitive event-handler match), 1 fact for A-3 cumulative budget, 1 fact for A-4 deep-nesting protection, 1 fact for A-5 content-cap, 2 facts for A-6 sanitizer (control-char strip + length cap), 3 facts for A-7 path normalization, 1 fact for A-8 budget. Existing tests updated: `HtmlParsingHostTests.ParseAsync_event_handler_attributes_are_left_in_place` flipped to `_are_stripped` (contract reversal); `HtmlParsingHostCorpusTests.Corpus_tailwind_cdn_emits_script_diagnostic` widened to allow either `HTML-SCRIPT-IGNORED-001` or `HTML-EVENT-HANDLER-IGNORED-001` in the diagnostic set. Snapshot regenerated for fixture `09-script-and-javascript-urls` to reflect the new uniform diagnostic-message format. Tests: **3262 unit / 3388 solution-wide passing** (+33 over the previous 3229/3355 baseline — +24 new Phase A facts + +9 from prior deep-review hardening that landed alongside this branch). AOT/JIT byte-parity gate stays green. Active-task pointer remains **Phase 3 — Fragmentainer-aware layout + pagination**.

Phase 2 deep review hardening pass shipped — addressed all 7 review recommendations spanning the full Phase 2 surface. (1) [P1] [`CssParserAdapter`](src/NetPdf.Css/Parser/CssParserAdapter.cs) style-rule slot alignment by selector identity, not just by kind. Cycle-1 paired any `CssRuleSlotKind.StyleRule` slot with any next `ICssStyleRule` from AngleSharp — so a dropped rule like `li::marker { ... }` (AngleSharp.Css 1.0.0-beta.144 emits an empty-selector rule for it) consumed the NEXT rule's slot, corrupting source location ordinals + recovery merging downstream. New `SlotMatchesAngleSharpRule` two-tier check: (a) AngleSharp's empty selector pairs with any slot prelude (covers the `::marker`-drop case while preserving the parsed declarations); (b) non-empty AngleSharp selectors must match the slot's normalized prelude (whitespace-collapsed, combinator-canonicalized) ordinal-equal; (c) otherwise demote slot to opaque without advancing the AngleSharp cursor. New `AdaptStyleRule(rule, preprocess, slot, ctx)` overload uses the slot's prelude when AngleSharp's selector is empty, restoring the authored selector text. (2) [P1] `EmitOpaqueFromSlot` recovers declarations from `RawBody`. Cycle-1 emitted dropped style rules with `Declarations: ImmutableArray<CssDeclaration>.Empty` — losing every declaration in the dropped block. New `CssPreprocessor.ScanAllDeclarations(string)` parses every property:value pair from a body string (sibling to the existing modern-only `ScanForModernDeclarations`); `EmitOpaqueFromSlot` invokes it on `slot.RawBody` then materializes via `ToCssDeclarations`. A dropped `li::marker { content: counter(items); color: red }` now lands in the AST with both declarations populated, so the CSS-CONTENT-FUNCTION-UNSUPPORTED-001 emission becomes reachable through the production path. (3) [P1] Inline `style=""` runs through `CssPreprocessor` recovery. Cycle-1's [`CascadeResolver.WalkInlineStylesRecursive`](src/NetPdf.Css/Cascade/CascadeResolver.cs) called `CssParserAdapter.AdaptInlineStyle(anglesharpStyle)` which fed AngleSharp's already-corrupted parsed `ICssStyleDeclaration` to the typed pipeline — `style="color: oklch(...)"` and modern multi-arg `attr()` were lost or misdiagnosed. New public `AdaptInlineStyleWithRecovery(style, rawStyleText, location)` constructs a synthetic `CssStyleRuleRecovery` from `ScanForModernDeclarations(rawStyleText)` and feeds the same merge pipeline as `<style>` blocks. End-to-end: `<p style="color: oklch(...)">` now emits CSS-MODERN-COLOR-FUNCTION-UNSUPPORTED-001 via the production path. (4) [P2] `@supports` validates the VALUE per CSS Conditional L3 §4.1.3, not just the property name. Cycle-1's `SupportsParser.ParsePrimary` returned `PropertyMetadata.NameToId.ContainsKey(prop)` — `@supports (color: not-a-real-color)` returned true because `color` is a registered property, so the guarded block applied. New probe: when the property name is registered, run the value through `PropertyResolverDispatch.Resolve(propertyId, rawValue, diagnostics: null)` and accept any `ResolutionState` other than `Invalid` (Resolved + Deferred both count, so var()/calc() values that resolve at layout time correctly count as "supported"). (5) [P2] [`CalcResolver`](src/NetPdf.Css/Cascade/CalcResolver.cs) finite guards on numeric parsing + binary arithmetic per IEEE 754 boundary semantics. Cycle-1 silently propagated `1e500 → Infinity` and `1e150 * 1e150 → Infinity` into the rewritten CSS text — downstream consumers saw the literal "Infinity" / "NaN" string instead of `CSS-CALC-INVALID-001`. New literal-time `IsFinite(n)` check on parsed numbers + new `Finite(magnitude, unit, reason)` wrapper applied at every Add / Subtract / Multiply / Divide site so overflow on composition also lands in the diagnostic dispatcher rather than the rewritten value text. Subsequent `var()`/`calc()` consumers see the original text preserved + can fall back to the property's initial value per CSS L4 §4.1. (6) [P2] [`CancellationToken`](src/NetPdf/Phase2/Phase2Pipeline.cs) threads INTO each major walker, not just between stages. Cycle-1's Task 17 hardening Rec 5 added `ThrowIfCancellationRequested()` at every stage boundary in `Phase2Pipeline.Run`; on a hostile-sized document a single stage (cascade matching against a 100k-element doc) ran to completion before the next boundary check. New `cancellationToken` parameter on `CascadeResolver.Resolve` + `BoxBuilder.Build` + `SemanticTreeBuilder.Build`; checked at every stylesheet, every DOM element walk in `WalkElement` / `WalkInlineStyles` / `BuildElementBoxes` / `WalkNode`. `SemanticTreeBuilder`'s `WalkContext` record struct gains a `CancellationToken` field so `with` expressions automatically propagate it to nested calls. Pre-cancelled token throws `OperationCanceledException` from inside the stage, not at the next boundary. (7) [P2] [`Phase2Result.Dispose`](src/NetPdf/Phase2/Phase2Result.cs) returns box-owned `ComputedStyle` instances to the pool. Cycle-1 marked styles attached to `Box` nodes as `IsBoxOwned` so the cascade-time `Dispose()` couldn't return them (premature pool release would let re-rental clear the slots while the box still references them) — but no explicit disposal sweep existed, so every conversion leaked one `ComputedStyle` per styled box / pseudo / fragment-pseudo to GC instead of recycling. New `ComputedStyle.ReleaseFromBox()` clears `_isBoxOwned` + delegates to `Dispose()`; new `Phase2Result.Dispose()` walks the box tree once, deduping by `ReferenceEqualityComparer` (in case future cascade optimizations share styles across siblings), and calls `ReleaseFromBox` on every unique style + `FirstLineStyle` + `FirstLetterStyle`. Phase2Result becomes `IDisposable` (still a `record struct`) so `using var result = await Phase2Pipeline.RunFromHtmlAsync(...)` is the typical call site. New tests: **+9 unit** in [`Phase2DeepReviewHardeningTests`](tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Phase2/Phase2DeepReviewHardeningTests.cs) — one per Rec, plus an extra calc-overflow case + a Dispose-idempotency case. Tests: **3229 unit / 3355 solution-wide passing** (+9 unit / +9 solution-wide over the previous 3220/3346 baseline). AOT/JIT byte-parity gate stays green. Active-task pointer remains **Phase 3 — Fragmentainer-aware layout + pagination**.

Phase 2 Task 19 hardening review pass shipped — addressed all 5 review recommendations: (1) [BLOCKER] Made [`ComputedStyleTests.Dispose_then_post_dispose_access_throws`](tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Css/ComputedValues/ComputedStyleTests.cs) deterministic by adding a test-only `internal static ComputedStyle.RentForExclusiveTesting()` factory that bypasses the production pool. The flake reproduces under xUnit's parallel runner: another test class's `ComputedStyle.Rent()` can race the just-disposed instance from the `ConcurrentBag`, call `Reset()` (which flips `_disposed = false`), and silently neutralize the assertion. The production soft-guard contract documents this race as best-effort by design — the test only needs to verify the soft guard fires when no re-rent occurs. The fix adds a `_excludedFromPool` flag set by the test-only factory; `Dispose()` checks it + skips the `_pool.Add(this)` call, so the disposed flag stays observably true regardless of concurrent rent activity. Verified deterministic across 3 full-suite runs (3220/3346 each). (2) [BLOCKER] 100 KB invoice perf criterion documented honestly. The exit-criterion (`< 50 ms p50`) is not satisfied — measured p50 (extracted from BDN's `*-report-full-compressed.json`) is **51.4 ms** (~2.8% over target). CHANGELOG now lists explicit p25 / p50 / p75 / mean instead of just mean ± error. The criterion is **borderline-waived** for ship: cycle-1 prioritizes correctness over perf; the 100 KB synthetic stresses cascade matching at ~3700 elements (O(rules × elements) hot path); Phase 3 layout/paint will dominate total convert wall-clock anyway (Phase 2 pipeline becomes ~1% once fragmentainer-aware layout lands). Deferring optimization until Phase 3+5 lets us set the perf budget against rendering-bound measurements rather than synthetic-bound ones. Phase 2 doc exit-criterion checkbox updated from ✅ to ⚠️ with waiver rationale. (3) [BLOCKER] [`README.md`](README.md) updated to reflect Phase 2's actual scope: status banner now reads "Phase 1 ✅ + Phase 2 ✅ (pending tag)"; the "every overload throws NotImplementedException" warning correctly cites `0.3.0-alpha` (was `0.1.0-alpha`) and notes that the throws stay until Phase 5 wires the facade (was claimed to land in Phase 2); code samples corrected from `// works at 0.3.0-alpha+` to `// still throws at 0.3.0-alpha; wired at v1.0`; the "What's actually shipped" capability table renamed from "at 0.1.0-alpha" to "at 0.3.0-alpha" with new rows for the Phase 2 surface (HTML parsing host, CSS cascade + var/calc subset contract, box-tree generation, semantic-tree generation, diagnostics emission); the public-facade row clarifies "Phase 5 wires the facade through Phase 2 + 3 + 4". (4) [BLOCKER] CHANGELOG release marker reframed: section header changed from `## [0.3.0-alpha] — 2026-05-07` (implies released) to `## [0.3.0-alpha] — staged for 2026-05-07 (tag pending PR merge)`; the `[Unreleased]` section gains an explanatory paragraph "treat the section as the staged contents of the next release"; the `[Unreleased]` compare-link now points to `0.1.0-alpha...HEAD` (was prematurely `0.3.0-alpha...HEAD`). Maintainer creates the actual `git tag 0.3.0-alpha` after PR merge. (5) [BLOCKER] Aligned CHANGELOG technical claims with implementation. Three corrections: (a) ComputedStyle is a `sealed class` (NOT a struct) holding `[InlineArray]`-backed inline buffers; pooled via a process-wide `ConcurrentBag<ComputedStyle>` (NOT `ArrayPool<T>`); `Rent()` clears via `Reset()` on take, `Dispose()` returns to the bag with a soft-guard `_disposed` flag. (b) `calc` resolver subset contract spelled out: absolute lengths/percentages/angles/times/frequencies/resolutions reduce; font-relative + viewport-relative + container-relative units **defer** to Phase 3's typed-value pipeline; mixed-unit-across-incompatible-dimensions also defers. Length resolver section parallel-corrected — `em`/`rem`/`vh`/`vw`/`vmin`/`vmax` etc. are NOT in the supported-units list; deferred to Phase 3. (c) `:has()` corrected from "parsed + matches" to "parsed + bytecode-flagged; matcher always returns false at runtime in v1 + emits CSS-HAS-RENDERING-NOT-IMPLEMENTED-001 once per flagged sub-group" — the previous wording suggested `:has()` actually matched, when in v1 it deterministically does not. Tests: **3220 unit / 3346 solution-wide passing** (unchanged — Task 19 hardening updates docs + the test-only Rent path; no production-test count impact). AOT/JIT byte-parity gate stays green across 3 full-suite runs. Active-task pointer remains **Phase 3 — Fragmentainer-aware layout + pagination**.

Phase 2 Task 19 shipped — release prep for `0.3.0-alpha`. Verified all 8 Phase 2 exit criteria: (1) ✅ all unit tests pass — 3220/3346 solution-wide; (2) ✅ layout snapshot tests pass — 30/30 for the 9-fixture corpus shipped in Task 18 + hardening 2; (3) ✅ all 4 invoice corpus files parse to BoxTree without exception — verified by `Phase2EndToEndTests` (Task 17); (4) ✅ Tailwind-CDN samples emit `HTML-SCRIPT-IGNORED-001` + inline `<style>` blocks parse correctly — verified by `Phase2HardeningTests` (Task 17 hardening) + new `09-script-and-javascript-urls` snapshot fixture (Task 18 hardening 2); (5) ✅ Anvil running-elements `@page { @bottom-* { content: element(...) } }` parses without error — verified through corpus integration tests since Task 12 cycle 1; (6) ✅ AOT smoke test green — `./scripts/aot-parity.sh` passes every cycle; (7) ✅ Performance gate within tolerance — new [`Phase2PipelineBenchmarks`](tests/NetPdf.Benchmarks/Phase2PipelineBenchmarks.cs) measures the full pipeline against 4 corpus invoices + 1 synthetic 100 KB invoice. Apple M4 Pro, .NET 10.0.7, in-process toolchain (BDN's spawn-via-csproj resolution conflicts with the stale Task 11 worktree at `.claude/worktrees/`; in-process sacrifices some isolation but the numbers stay well within Phase 5's containerized-gate +25% tolerance, documented in the benchmark XML doc). Numbers: 01-classic-pure-css (3.7 KB) **561 µs / 1.43 MB**; 02-tailwind-cdn (10.8 KB) **547 µs / 1.34 MB**; 03-tailwind-cdn-responsive (13.6 KB) **702 µs / 1.61 MB**; 04-anvil-running-elements (6.3 KB) **717 µs / 1.58 MB**; 100 KB synthetic invoice **50.9 ms ± 0.6 ms / 51.3 MB**. The 100 KB synthetic sits at the < 50 ms p50 exit-criterion boundary — documented honestly in CHANGELOG; the per-byte allocation regression at scale (509 µs/KB at 100 KB vs 52 µs/KB at 14 KB) reflects cycle-1 prioritization of correctness over perf and is acceptable for ship since Phase 3 layout/paint will dominate runtime cost (the Phase 2 pipeline is roughly 1% of total convert time once layout + paint land); (8) ✅ CHANGELOG updated, version bumped in MSBuild source-of-truth + the informational JSON copy. Ready for `git tag 0.3.0-alpha` after PR merge — Roland tags. Phase 2 Task 18 hardening 2 review pass shipped — addressed all 4 review recommendations: (1) [P2] Unified diagnostics capture via the public [`IDiagnosticsSink`](src/NetPdf/Diagnostics/IDiagnosticsSink.cs) so HTML-stage diagnostics land in snapshots alongside CSS-stage. Cycle 1 captured only the internal `ICssDiagnosticsSink`, leaving `HTML-SCRIPT-IGNORED-001` and `HTML-JAVASCRIPT-URL-IGNORED-001` invisible to the snapshot framework. [`SnapshotTests.RunPipelineAsync`](tests/NetPdf.LayoutSnapshots/SnapshotTests.cs) now constructs `new HtmlPdfOptions { Diagnostics = sink }` + lets `Phase2Pipeline.RunFromHtmlAsync` auto-wire `PublicDiagnosticsSinkAdapter.ForOptions(options)` (per Task 17 hardening Rec 4) — the public sink receives both HTML diagnostics directly from `HtmlParsingHost` + CSS diagnostics adapted from `ICssDiagnosticsSink`. [`DiagnosticsSerializer`](tests/NetPdf.LayoutSnapshots/Serialization/DiagnosticsSerializer.cs) was rewritten to take `IReadOnlyList<NetPdf.Diagnostic>` (public type) instead of `IReadOnlyList<CssDiagnostic>` (internal) — the type change keeps the interface natural for callers + matches what production consumers see. New 9th fixture [`09-script-and-javascript-urls`](tests/NetPdf.LayoutSnapshots/Fixtures/09-script-and-javascript-urls/) exercises the HTML diagnostics path: a `<script>alert('x')</script>` element + an `<a href="javascript:doBad()">` link both emit Warnings (`HTML-SCRIPT-IGNORED-001` + `HTML-JAVASCRIPT-URL-IGNORED-001`) end-to-end via the production pipeline, while a sibling `<a href="https://example.com">` survives intact (proves the strip is targeted, not blanket). The semantic-tree golden also captures the 3-state semantic outcome: `<script>` removed entirely (no node), `<a>` with stripped href becomes transparent (an `InlineText "click"` flows up to its parent), `<a>` with safe href emits `Link @href="https://example.com"`. (2) [P2] Source locations now appear in diagnostic snapshots. Previous format `{Code}\t{Severity}\t{Message}` lost regression-detection on, e.g., a CSS-PROPERTY-VALUE-INVALID-001 that started reporting wrong source lines. New format `{Code}\t{Severity}\t{Location}\t{Message}` with three formats for the location field: `<unknown>` for `SourceLocation.Unknown` (today's typical state for CSS-stage until Task 3 wires real positions — explicit placeholder is more honest than a silent `0:0` that would change meaning when Task 3 lands); `<inline>:Line:Column` for HTML diagnostics on documents parsed without a BaseUri (every snapshot fixture, since file-pathed BaseUris would break CI portability); `{File}:Line:Column` verbatim when a real File is set. The format documents the expected snapshot author practice ("BaseUri stays unset for snapshot fixtures"). Fixture 09's diagnostics correctly carry `<inline>:1:28` (script position) + `<inline>:1:82` (javascript: link position) from AngleSharp's `IsKeepingSourceReferences` mode; fixture 08's modern-color diagnostic now carries `<inline>:1:37` from `CssPreprocessor`'s recovery path while the counter() + replaced-pseudo entries still emit `<unknown>` (Task 3 territory). (3) [P2] Codified the v1 semantic-tree policy on generated content. The `05-pseudo-with-attr` box snapshot DOES carry the `"[WIDGET] "` generated text (BoxBuilder materializes it from the cascade), but the semantic snapshot does NOT (SemanticTreeBuilder walks the static DOM, not the rendered box tree — Task 15 cycle 1 deferral Rec 4). The reviewer flagged the gap as ambiguous: drift vs. intent. The hardening adds explicit policy statement to [`SemanticTreeBuilder`](src/NetPdf.Layout/Semantic/SemanticTreeBuilder.cs)'s XML doc — generated text is intentionally absent in v1, with the v1.1 PDF/UA pass routing `::marker` content to `InlineText` (informational) and `::before`/`::after` to either `InlineText` (when carrying `attr()`/`counter()` substitution) or `/Artifact` (purely decorative) per WCAG 1.1.1 + the rendered-tree-driven rebuild. New `PseudoWithAttr_generated_text_is_absent_from_semantic_tree_until_phase_5_pdfua` Fact pins the current state explicitly: the box tree's `::before`/`::after` `InlineBox` carries `"[WIDGET] "` and `"."` text on its TextRun children, while the semantic tree's `AggregateText` reads only `"item description"` (no `[WIDGET]`, no `.`). When Phase 5 changes the policy, the named-test failure tells the future author "you're crossing an intentional v1 boundary" rather than the snapshot drift looking like an accidental regression. (4) [P3] Narrowed `.gitignore` Finder-duplicate patterns from `* [0-9].*` (any extension) to source-shaped extensions only: `*.cs` + `*.csproj` + `*.props` + `*.targets` + `*.json`. Legitimate numbered docs/fixtures/assets (`Sample 2.html`, `screenshot 3.png`, `notes 4.md`) are now tracked normally — verified by creating `tests/sample 2.html` + `tests/notes 3.md` + `tests/asset 5.png` and seeing all three in `git status`, while `tests/cs-dup 2.cs` is correctly ignored. Comment in `.gitignore` documents the `git add -f path/to/file` escape hatch for legitimate numbered source files (rare but possible — e.g., a deliberate partial class file split). Tests: **3220 unit / 3346 solution-wide passing** (+4 LayoutSnapshots over Task 18 hardening's 3220/3342 — added 1 new fixture × 3 trees + 1 pinning Fact = 4 net new tests; total 30). AOT/JIT byte-parity gate stays green. Active-task pointer remains **Task 19 — Phase 2 release prep**.

Phase 2 Task 18 hardening review pass shipped — addressed all 5 review recommendations: (1) [P0] Removed 8 untracked `* 2.cs` macOS Finder / iCloud / Time Machine duplicates that were silently breaking the snapshot project's compile (`ModernColorFunctions 2.cs` produced duplicate-type-definition errors in `NetPdf.Css`, cascading through the dependency chain). Two layers of defensive infrastructure prevent recurrence: [`Directory.Build.props`](Directory.Build.props) gains `<Compile Remove="**/* [2-9].cs" />` + `<None Remove="..." />` so any future Finder duplicate is silently excluded from compilation instead of cratering the build; [`.gitignore`](.gitignore) gains `* [0-9].*` + `* 1[0-9].*` so they can never enter version control. Verified by creating `Tmp 2.cs` mid-build — solution compiles clean (0 warnings/errors) + git status doesn't list it. Glob is constrained to numeric suffix so legitimate files with trailing digits (`UAX29*`, `Type8x8*`) are unaffected. All 8 fixtures now sit at one logical line per file. The trailing-newline-after-`</html>` artifact (one residual `AnonymousBlock` per fixture from the file's terminating `\n`) is HTML5-spec-correct (whitespace post-`</html>` is reparented into `<body>`); kept since it's identical across fixtures + minimal. Snapshots are now ~60–80% shorter + dominated by structural lines. (3) [P2] Diagnostics emission captured per fixture via new [`Diagnostics_match_snapshot`](tests/NetPdf.LayoutSnapshots/SnapshotTests.cs) Theory + new [`DiagnosticsSerializer`](tests/NetPdf.LayoutSnapshots/Serialization/DiagnosticsSerializer.cs). Format: `{Code}\t{Severity}\t{NormalizedMessage}` per line, sorted by `(Code, Severity, Message)` ordinal for stable run-to-run output; messages whitespace-collapsed + truncated at 120 chars to keep diff readable; source location intentionally omitted (`CssSourceLocation.Unknown` until Task 3 wires real positions — emitting placeholder coordinates would churn every snapshot once Task 3 lands). Empty-content file = "fixture runs clean". Wired through [`Phase2Pipeline.RunFromHtmlAsync(html, options, sink)`](src/NetPdf/Phase2/Phase2Pipeline.cs) using a recording `ICssDiagnosticsSink`. New 8th fixture `08-unsupported-css-features` proves the non-empty path: `content: counter(items)` + `color: oklch(0.7 0.15 250)` + `img::before { content: "X" }` produces 3 distinct codes (`CSS-CONTENT-FUNCTION-UNSUPPORTED-001` Warning + `CSS-MODERN-COLOR-FUNCTION-UNSUPPORTED-001` Info + `CSS-PSEUDO-SUPPRESSED-ON-REPLACED-001` Info — all from Task 16's emission paths, end-to-end via the production pipeline). The 7 pre-existing fixtures' diagnostics files are correctly empty — proves they hit only spec-supported features without silent regression risk. (4) [P3] Auto-discovery replaces hard-coded `FixtureNames`. Fixture directories under `Fixtures/` are now enumerated at test-discovery time + sorted ordinal, so a new fixture directory is automatically picked up by all three Theory drivers. Snapshot files (`box-tree.txt`, `semantic-tree.txt`, `diagnostics.txt`) are NOT required up-front — the bootstrap behavior in `SnapshotAssert` writes them on first run; once committed they serve as regression goldens. The `05-pseudo-with-attr` fixture's value coverage (attr() substitution) is already proven by the box-tree snapshot showing the resulting `TextRun "[WIDGET] "` text. Phase 2 Task 18 cycle 1 shipped — layout snapshot test infrastructure. New test project [`NetPdf.LayoutSnapshots`](tests/NetPdf.LayoutSnapshots/) gains three pieces of machinery and 7 golden-file fixtures so future Phase 2 / Phase 3 changes that reshape the box or semantic trees fail loud instead of silently regressing. (a) Deterministic serializers: [`BoxTreeSerializer`](tests/NetPdf.LayoutSnapshots/Serialization/BoxTreeSerializer.cs) walks `Box` trees emitting `{indent}{Kind}{source-tag?}{pseudo-tag?}{text?}` lines with 2-space indent — `BlockContainer @element=p`, `TextRun @element=p "Hello world."`, `Marker @element=li ::marker`, `InlineReplacedElement @element=img`; escapes `\\` `\"` `\n` `\r` `\t` in TextRun text. [`SemanticTreeSerializer`](tests/NetPdf.LayoutSnapshots/Serialization/SemanticTreeSerializer.cs) mirrors the format for `SemanticNode` trees with extra metadata tags `@href` (Link), `@alt=<missing>/<decorative>/"value"` tri-state (Image/Figure per Task 15 Rec 6), `@rowspan`/`@colspan`/`@scope`/`@headers`/`@abbr` (TableCell/TableHeaderCell per Task 15 Rec 5). Both are AOT-clean (no reflection, no LINQ in serialization paths), Span-friendly, and identical-by-bytes across runs. (b) Golden-file comparison: [`SnapshotAssert.MatchesFile(actual, snapshotRelativePath)`](tests/NetPdf.LayoutSnapshots/Serialization/SnapshotAssert.cs) reads the snapshot from `Fixtures/<name>/box-tree.txt` (or `semantic-tree.txt`), normalizes line endings, and throws an `XunitException` with a unified-diff-style report on mismatch (first-divergence + 9 more lines of context, capped at 10 to keep failure output readable). The `NETPDF_UPDATE_SNAPSHOTS=1` (or `=true`) environment variable flips to update mode — writes `actual` to the source-tree fixture instead of comparing. Source-tree path resolution walks up from `AppContext.BaseDirectory` until it finds the `NetPdf.slnx` repo root marker, then descends into `tests/NetPdf.LayoutSnapshots/Fixtures/<...>` so update mode writes the source tree, not the bin/ output. First-run bootstrap behavior: when a fixture file doesn't exist, the helper writes the initial snapshot to the source tree AND fails the test (avoids the silent-green-on-no-snapshot trap). (c) Theory driver: [`SnapshotTests`](tests/NetPdf.LayoutSnapshots/SnapshotTests.cs) runs both serializers against every fixture: `BoxTree_matches_snapshot(fixtureName)` × 7, `SemanticTree_matches_snapshot(fixtureName)` × 7. Each test parses `Fixtures/<name>/input.html`, runs the full Phase 2 pipeline via [`Phase2Pipeline.RunFromHtmlAsync(html, new HtmlPdfOptions())`](src/NetPdf/Phase2/Phase2Pipeline.cs), serializes both trees, and asserts against the goldens. The 7 fixtures cover the principal Phase 2 surface area: `01-simple-paragraph` (`<p>Hello world.</p>` smoke); `02-list-with-markers` (ordered list with 3 items, decimal markers from Task 14); `03-table-with-caption` (table fixup wrapper+grid pair from Task 13, caption preservation, scope+colspan); `04-var-and-calc` (`:root { --base: 8px; --doubled: calc(var(--base) * 2); }` chain from Tasks 8/9); `05-pseudo-with-attr` (`.label::before { content: "[" attr(data-tag) "] "; }` covering Task 14 multi-string-concat + attr() substitution); `06-hidden-and-aria` (display:none + aria-hidden="true" + visible content covering Task 15 Rec 1 hidden filtering); `07-figure-with-img` (figure+figcaption + alt="" decorative + missing alt covering Task 15 Rec 6 alt tri-state). The csproj gains `NetPdf.Css` project ref + `<None Include="Fixtures\**\*.*" CopyToOutputDirectory="PreserveNewest" />` so goldens are co-located with the test binary at runtime. Replaces the original `PhaseZeroSmoke.Solution_Compiles` placeholder. Cycle-1 deferrals: snapshot doesn't yet capture computed-style fields (deferred until Phase 3 layout actually consumes them — capturing them now would lock in cycle-1 internals), pagination output (Phase 3 cost-model owns that), or paint display-list (Phase 4). New tests: **+14 snapshot** in [`NetPdf.LayoutSnapshots`](tests/NetPdf.LayoutSnapshots/SnapshotTests.cs) (7 fixtures × 2 trees). Tests: **3220 unit / 3330 solution-wide passing** (+13 over Task 17 hardening's 3220/3317 — the new project's `PhaseZeroSmoke` placeholder is replaced by 14 theory cases, net +13). AOT/JIT byte-parity gate stays green. Active-task pointer flipped to **Task 19 — Phase 2 release prep**.

Phase 2 Task 17 hardening review pass shipped — addressed all 6 review recommendations: (1) [P1] Diagnostics sink now threaded through every stage. [`Phase2Pipeline.Run`](src/NetPdf/Phase2/Phase2Pipeline.cs) forwards the supplied `ICssDiagnosticsSink` to `CascadeResolver.Resolve` + `VarResolver.Resolve` in addition to `BoxBuilder.Build`. Cycle 1 only forwarded to BoxBuilder, losing `CSS-CONTAINER-QUERY-UNSUPPORTED-001` / `CSS-AT-RULE-UNKNOWN-001` / `CSS-HAS-RENDERING-NOT-IMPLEMENTED-001` / `CSS-PARSE-WARNING-001` (cascade-emitted) and `CSS-VAR-CIRCULAR-001` / `CSS-VAR-EXPANSION-LIMIT-001` / `CSS-CALC-INVALID-001` / `CSS-CALC-DIV-BY-ZERO-001` (var-resolver-emitted). All now reach the supplied sink. (2) [P1] `CssMediaContext` is now built from `HtmlPdfOptions` instead of the hardcoded `DefaultPrint`. New `BuildMediaContext(options)` helper maps `HtmlPdfOptions.MediaType` (Print/Screen) to the lower-cased media string and projects the viewport from `HtmlPdfOptions.PageSize` (WidthPx + HeightPx). DevicePixelRatio + PreferredColorScheme stay at their defaults until `HtmlPdfOptions` grows matching options (post-v1). Authors who pass `MediaType = Screen` or non-default `PageSize` (Letter / Tabloid / etc.) now get correct `@media`-query evaluation against their actual viewport. (3) [P1] Stylesheet media + disabled metadata preserved per HTML5 §4.2.6. `ExtractStylesheets` now reads each owner element's `media` attribute (authoritative for inline `<style>`) and falls back to `rawSheet.Media.MediaText` when missing (covers `<link>` sheets where AngleSharp populates Media from the link's media attribute). The `IsDisabled` state from `rawSheet.IsDisabled` is also propagated. Cycle 1 hardcoded `mediaQuery: null, isDisabled: false`, so `<style media="screen">` rules applied during print. (4) [P2] New [`PublicDiagnosticsSinkAdapter`](src/NetPdf/Diagnostics/PublicDiagnosticsSinkAdapter.cs) wraps the public `IDiagnosticsSink` as the internal `ICssDiagnosticsSink`, converting each `CssDiagnostic` into the public `Diagnostic` shape (severity 1:1, `CssSourceLocation` → `SourceLocation`). The adapter sits in the facade assembly where both types are visible (NetPdf.Css can't reference NetPdf without a project-cycle). New `ForOptions(options)` static returns null when `HtmlPdfOptions.Diagnostics` is null so downstream stages fast-skip emission. `RunFromHtmlAsync` auto-wires the adapter when no explicit sink is supplied — a single public sink now collects HTML + CSS + layout diagnostics. (5) [P2] `CancellationToken` honored at every stage boundary. New `cancellationToken` parameter on `Run(...)` calls `ThrowIfCancellationRequested()` after parsing + before each of CascadeResolver / VarResolver / BoxBuilder / SemanticTreeBuilder. Pre-cancelled tokens throw immediately. (Stage internals don't yet support cancellation, but stage boundaries are now responsive.) (6) [P2] Owner-node-based stylesheet pairing replaces ordinal-index pairing. `ExtractStylesheets` now reads each `ICssStyleSheet.OwnerNode` to associate the sheet with its `<style>` element directly. Cycle 1's `QuerySelectorAll("style")[styleIdx]` matched by ordinal which silently corrupted when disabled / external `<link>` sheets entered `document.StyleSheets`. Phase 2 Task 17 cycle 1 shipped — HTML+CSS → BoxTree end-to-end integration tests. New [`Phase2Pipeline`](src/NetPdf/Phase2/Phase2Pipeline.cs) composition helper stitches every Phase 2 stage (`HtmlParsingHost` → `CssPreprocessor` → `CssParserAdapter` → `CascadeResolver` → `VarResolver` → `BoxBuilder` + `SemanticTreeBuilder`) behind two entry points: `RunFromHtmlAsync(html, options, sink)` for the test-friendly path that parses raw HTML; `Run(document, sheets, sink)` for callers that already have a parsed document. Returns a [`Phase2Result`](src/NetPdf/Phase2/Phase2Result.cs) record struct carrying the box tree, semantic tree, resolved cascade, and adapted stylesheets. This is the canonical pipeline composition the public `HtmlPdf.Convert` facade will eventually invoke (Phase 5 wires the public surface). New tests: **+30 integration** in two new test files: 15 in [`Phase2EndToEndTests`](tests/NetPdf.RealDocuments/Phase2/Phase2EndToEndTests.cs) covering all 4 corpus invoices (smoke + box/semantic-tree non-triviality), diagnostic budget on the classic invoice, cross-stage invariants (`display: none` filters both trees, `aria-hidden=\"true\"` filters semantic only, `var() → calc()` chain lands as 20px on the box, list-item marker numbering, replaced-element pseudo suppression with diagnostic, `attr()` substitution end-to-end, `hidden` attribute filtering, determinism across 3 runs (box-tree shape, semantic-tree shape, diagnostic count); 15 in [`Phase2CompositionTests`](tests/NetPdf.RealDocuments/Phase2/Phase2CompositionTests.cs) covering deeper compositions (3-level var() through calc() reduction, var-with-fallback, both `::before`+`::after` materializing with attr() substitution, content with `counter()` rejected via pipeline, modern color functions theory × 4 (oklch/oklab/color-mix/light-dark) emitting through preprocessor recovery → cascade → resolver, multi-arg attr() emitting through preprocessor recovery + content-list rejection, aria-hidden subtree-drops in semantic tree, `<style>` rule text doesn't leak into semantic InlineText, table wrapper+grid present in box tree end-to-end, `thead`/`tbody`/`tfoot` transparency in semantic tree, mixed `<li>` + `<div display:list-item>` numbering continuously per Task 14 review Rec 3, replaced-pseudo dedup across 5 imgs → 1 diagnostic). New helper `FindPrincipalBoxes(root, localName)` filters out TextRun children that inherit `SourceElement` from the parent inline (caught a bug in initial test draft where `WalkBoxes(...).Where(b => b.SourceElement?.LocalName == \"p\")` matched both the principal `<p>` box AND its TextRun children). Cycle-1 deferrals: the canonical pipeline doesn't yet wire `HtmlPdfOptions.Diagnostics` (the public sink) — tests use `ICssDiagnosticsSink` directly; Phase 5 wires the public sink at the facade boundary.
