Inputs like `calc(1+2)`, `calc(16px-4px)`, `calc(1 +2)` (asymmetric) all emit `CSS-CALC-INVALID-001` and preserve text.
  - **Rec 4 — same-unit dimension division returns a unitless `Number` per L4 §10.10**: The Task 9 implementation rejected `calc(16px / 2px)` as invalid. Per the spec, dividing two values of the same unit cancels the dimension and yields a `Number`, so `calc(16px / 2px) = 8` (unitless), and the result composes naturally into further math (`calc((16px / 2px) * 4px) = 32px`). `Divide` now returns `new CalcValue(a/b, Number)` for same-unit dimension division, keeps Number-divisor unchanged, and throws `CalcParseException` for cross-class division (length / angle, time / frequency) where no unit-algebra solution exists. Same-unit multiplication remains invalid because CSS doesn't define area units (no `px²`).
  - **Rec 5 — VarResolver var()→calc end-to-end pipeline tests**: New `VarToCalcPipelineTests` (11 tests) drives small synthetic stylesheets through `CascadeResolver.Resolve` → `VarResolver.Resolve` and asserts the joined pipeline behaves correctly: `var()` holding a `calc()` expression reduces; two `var()`s feeding a single `calc()` reduce; inherited custom property feeds a calc on a descendant; `var(--missing, calc(16px + 4px))` falls back through to the calc; nested var chain `--a: var(--b)` then `calc(var(--a) * 4)` reduces; calc runs after var (not before — reverse order would cause spurious deferral); circular var keeps the value invalid (no calc reduction, `CSS-VAR-CIRCULAR-001` fires); `var()` carrying `clamp` reduces; deferred mixed-unit `calc(100% - 16px)` survives intact; `var()` carrying `calc(2em)` defers with no diagnostic; `calc(16px / var(--d))` with `--d: 0` emits `CSS-CALC-DIV-BY-ZERO-001`. Catches drift between the two resolvers.
  - **Rec 6 — docs aligned with the calc subset**: [`docs/compatibility-matrix.md`](docs/compatibility-matrix.md) `calc()` row now reflects the implemented subset (🧪 status until Task 10 ships typed-value reduction): documents what reduces, what defers (font/viewport/container-relative + percentage-mixed), what's invalid (`dim * dim`, cross-class division, missing whitespace), and what's post-v1 (`sin`/`cos`/`tan`, `pow`/`sqrt`/`hypot`, `mod`/`rem`/`round`). [`docs/phases/phase-2-css-engine.md`](docs/phases/phase-2-css-engine.md) `calc()` resolver entry mirrors the matrix and links the test files. The test plan row points at all three test files (`CalcResolverTests`, `CalcResolverReviewCycle1Tests`, `VarToCalcPipelineTests`) so future contributors don't accidentally treat one file as the full coverage surface.
  - **Test deltas**: `CalcResolverReviewCycle1Tests` (58 tests covering all four spec-correctness recs) + `VarToCalcPipelineTests` (11 var → calc pipeline tests). Two pre-existing tests rewrote their expectations against the new spec-correct behavior: `Calc_em_resolves_to_16px_per_em` → `Calc_with_em_defers_to_typed_value_stage` (asserts deferral); `Dividing_by_dimensioned_value_emits_diagnostic` split into `Calc_same_unit_dimension_division_returns_unitless_number` (now valid per spec) + `Calc_dividing_by_dimensioned_value_of_different_class_emits_diagnostic` (cross-class still invalid).
  - Total tests: **2480 unit / 2523 solution-wide passing** (+70 unit over Task 9's 2410). AOT/JIT byte-parity gate stays green.

- **Task 10 cycle 1 — per-property typed-value resolvers (length / color / number / keyword)** ✅ (2026-05-05)
  - **`src/NetPdf.Css/ComputedValues/PropertyResolvers/PropertyResolverDispatch.cs` (new)** — single entry point: `Resolve(PropertyId, string resolvedValue, ICssDiagnosticsSink?, CssSourceLocation) → ComputedSlot`. Dispatches off `PropertyMeta.Type` (looked up via `PropertyMetadata.Table` from Task 4's source generator) to a per-type leaf resolver. Whitespace at the value's edges is tolerated; empty / whitespace-only input returns `Unset`. Out-of-range PropertyIds return `Unset` defensively. The four wired families: `Color` → `ColorResolver`; `Length`/`LengthPercentage`/`LengthPercentageAuto`/`Percentage`/`TextSpacing` → `LengthResolver`; `Number`/`Integer` → `NumberResolver`; `Keyword` → `KeywordResolver`. PropertyTypes that are intentionally cycle-2 work return `Unset` with no diagnostic so the cascade falls through to initial / inherited per CSS Cascade L4 §4.4.
  - **`LengthResolver.cs` (new)** — handles the dimension family per CSS Values L4 §6 + §7. Absolute-unit conversion: `1in = 96px`, `1cm = 96/2.54 px`, `1mm = 96/25.4 px`, `1Q = 96/(25.4 × 4) px ≈ 0.945 px`, `1pt = 96/72 px`, `1pc = 16 px` (12pt). Bare `0` is a valid length; bare non-zero number rejected per §6.2 with `CSS-PROPERTY-VALUE-INVALID-001`. Percentages packed via `ComputedSlot.FromPercentage` fixed-point; rejected on `Length` (which doesn't admit %); range-checked against `MinFixedPercentage`/`MaxFixedPercentage`. `auto` accepted only on `LengthPercentageAuto`; `normal` only on `TextSpacing` — wrong keyword on wrong type emits the invalid-value diagnostic. **Deferred (no diagnostic, returns `Unset` for layout to finalize):** font-relative units (`em`, `rem`, `ch`, `ex`, `lh`, `rlh`, `cap`, `ic`), viewport-relative + small/large/dynamic variants (`vw`/`vh`/`svw`/`lvw`/`dvw`/`vmin`/`vmax`/`vi`/`vb` etc.), container-relative units (`cqw`/`cqh`/`cqi`/`cqb`/`cqmin`/`cqmax`). Numeric splitter has the `2em` scientific-notation lookahead trap fixed (consumes `e` as exponent only when followed by digits, optional sign — same fix as `CalcResolver.ParseNumberOrDimension`).
  - **`ColorResolver.cs` + `CssNamedColors.cs` (new)** — handles every cycle-1 color form per CSS Color L4 §4. `transparent` → `0x00000000`; `currentcolor` → `CurrentColorSentinel = 0x00000001` (distinct from transparent's all-zero pattern; the paint stage substitutes the cascaded `color` value when it sees this exact pattern). Named-color table: 147 entries from CSS Color L4 §6.1 in a `FrozenDictionary<string, uint>` keyed lower-case (covers all CSS-1/2/3 keywords + `rebeccapurple` + grey/gray spelling aliases + cyan/aqua and magenta/fuchsia synonyms; every entry is opaque). Hex parser handles `#rgb`/`#rgba`/`#rrggbb`/`#rrggbbaa` with proper nibble doubling for the short forms. Functional parser handles `rgb()`/`rgba()`/`hsl()`/`hsla()` in BOTH legacy comma-separated and modern whitespace-separated + slash-alpha syntax (CSS Color L4 §4.2 lets the modern syntax accept either as long as the rest is well-formed; cycle 1 is permissive). RGB channels accept `<number>` 0..255 and `<percentage>` 0..100% (mixed forms allowed); alpha accepts `<number>` 0..1 and `<percentage>`. **Critical correctness fix during implementation:** percentage-to-byte conversion uses `pct * 255.0 / 100.0` not `pct * 2.55` because 2.55 is not exactly representable in IEEE-754 (`50 * 2.55 = 127.4999...` → rounds to 127 not 128). Both rounding paths now use `MidpointRounding.AwayFromZero` for predictable behavior at midpoints. HSL parser converts hue via the standard L4 algorithm; accepts `deg`/`rad`/`grad`/`turn` units + bare degrees; normalizes to `[0, 360)`. **Deferred with diagnostic** (`CSS-PROPERTY-VALUE-INVALID-001`): modern color spaces `oklch()`/`oklab()`/`lab()`/`lch()`/`color()`/`color-mix()` — they need Task 3's pre-pass capture (AngleSharp.Css silently corrupts these to wrong rgba). System colors (`canvas`, `canvastext`, etc. per CSS Color 4 §10) likewise need a color-scheme context they don't have here.
  - **`NumberResolver.cs` (new)** — `ResolveNumber` accepts any finite real (no unit suffix); `ResolveInteger` accepts a signed 32-bit integer with optional leading sign but rejects decimals + exponents + units. Both reject NaN/±Infinity. New `ComputedSlotTag.Number = 8` + `ComputedSlot.FromNumber(double)` + `AsNumber()`/`AsNumberFloat()` accessors keep numbers distinct from lengths (different tag, same float32 storage) so the decoder knows the value is dimensionless.
  - **`KeywordResolver.cs` (new)** — per-property keyword tables (frozen dicts) for the 24 `Keyword`-typed properties in `properties.json`: `align-items`/`align-self`/`justify-content` (CSS Box Alignment L3 §4); the four `border-*-style` (CSS Backgrounds 3 §4.4) sharing one table; `border-collapse` (Tables 3 §6); `box-sizing` (Basic UI 4 §10); `break-inside` (Fragmentation 3 §3.2); `clear` (CSS 2.2 §9.5.2); `cursor` (Basic UI 4 §8.1.1 — bare-keyword subset; URL forms cycle 2); `display` (Display 3 §2 — single-keyword forms only; multi-keyword `inline flex` syntax cycle 2); `flex-direction`/`flex-wrap` (Flexbox 1 §5); `float` (CSS 2.2 §9.5.1); `font-style` (Fonts 4 §3.5 — single-keyword form); both `overflow-{x,y}` (Overflow 3 §3.1) sharing one table; `position` (Positioned Layout 3 §2 — `static`/`relative`/`absolute`/`fixed`/`sticky`); `text-align` (Text 3 §7.1); `text-decoration-line` (Text Decoration 3 §2 — single-keyword form); `text-transform` (Text 3 §6.1); `white-space` (Text 3 §3.1 — legacy single-keyword form). Keyword ids are dense zero-based by source-code declaration order — that's the contract downstream switch-on-id consumers depend on. Unknown keywords on a covered property emit `CSS-PROPERTY-VALUE-INVALID-001`. Properties with no table registered (e.g., `font-weight` is `FontWeight` PropertyType, not `Keyword`) return `Unset` with no diagnostic. CSS-wide values (`inherit`/`initial`/`unset`/`revert`/`revert-layer`) are NOT this resolver's job — the cascade handles them at declaration assignment time and they never reach a per-property resolver.
  - **Diagnostics**: new `CssPropertyValueInvalid001` ("CSS-PROPERTY-VALUE-INVALID-001", Warning) on both `NetPdf.DiagnosticCodes` (facade) and `NetPdf.Css.Diagnostics.CssDiagnosticCodes` (internal CSS pipeline). Registry-doc parity test + cross-pipeline parity test added. Doc registered in `docs/diagnostics-codes.md` between `CSS-CALC-DIV-BY-ZERO-001` and `CSS-CONTAINER-QUERY-UNSUPPORTED-001`.
  - **Cycle-2 deferrals** (each returns `Unset` with no diagnostic — cycle 1 deliberately leaves the specialized union types unresolved): `FontFamilyList` (needs side-table for variable-length), `FontWeight` (named keywords + 100..900 numeric range), `FontSize` (absolute-size + relative-size keywords + length-percent + math), `LineHeight` (`normal | <number> | <length-percentage>`), `LineWidth` (`thin/medium/thick | <length>`), `FlexBasis` (`content | <length-percentage> | auto`), `VerticalAlign` (keyword | length-percentage), `Content` (complex content-list per CSS Content 3 §2), `Url` / `String` / `Time` / `Angle` / `Resolution` (no current consumer; will land alongside specific properties that need them).
  - **Test plan honored** per the testing-discipline rule:
    - Unit (`LengthResolverTests`, 30+ tests): every absolute unit family + the bare-zero special case + bare-nonzero rejection; percentage on each admitted PropertyType + percentage rejection on `Length`; `auto`/`normal` keyword acceptance per type; the full deferred-unit grid (8 font-relative + 13 viewport-relative + 6 container-relative); garbled inputs.
    - Unit (`ColorResolverTests`, 50+ tests): `transparent` + `currentcolor` round-trip; named-color cases incl. case-insensitivity + aliases; every hex form + hex malformed-shape rejection; `rgb()`/`rgba()` modern + legacy + slash-alpha + percentage channels + clamp on overflow + 5-component rejection; `hsl()`/`hsla()` modern + legacy + every hue unit + 0%/100% lightness extremes; modern color spaces all 6 emit diagnostic; garbage rejection.
    - Unit (`CssNamedColorsTests`, 20+ tests): high-coverage spot checks + alias parity + opacity invariant.
    - Unit (`NumberResolverTests`, 12 tests): finite-real round-trip + NaN/Infinity rejection + unit-suffix rejection + integer round-trip + decimal/exponent rejection.
    - Unit (`KeywordResolverTests`, 20+ tests): admitted keyword cases per major property + case-insensitivity + dense-id contract verification + unknown-keyword diagnostic + no-table-registered fallthrough.
    - Unit (`PropertyResolverDispatchTests`, 11 tests): dispatch wiring per PropertyType + empty/whitespace-only handling + diagnostic propagation through the dispatch.
    - Unit (`ComputedSlotTests` extension, 7 new): `Number` tag round-trip across positive/negative/zero/decimal + NaN+Infinity rejection.
    - Unit (`DiagnosticCodesTests` extension, 2 new): registry-doc parity + literal stability for `CSS-PROPERTY-VALUE-INVALID-001`.
  - Total tests: **2677 unit / 2720 solution-wide passing** (+197 unit over Task 9 cycle 1's 2480/2523 baseline). AOT/JIT byte-parity gate stays green.

- **Task 10 cycle 1 review pass — structural correctness + spec strictness** ✅ (2026-05-06)
  - **Rec 1 — `ResolverResult` structured return**: cycle 1 conflated three semantically-distinct outcomes ("typed value resolved", "valid but needs context", "parse failure") under a shared `ComputedSlot.Unset` sentinel. Without the distinction, the cascade can't choose between (a) carrying raw text forward for layout-time finalization vs (b) falling back to initial / inherited per the cascade's "invalid at computed value time" rule. Introduced `ResolverResult(Slot, State, RawText)` + `ResolutionState{Resolved=0, Deferred=1, Invalid=2}` with factory methods (`Resolved(slot)`, `Deferred(rawText)`, `Invalid()`) and predicate properties (`IsResolved`/`IsDeferred`/`IsInvalid`). Refactored every resolver + the dispatch to return `ResolverResult`. Cycle-2 PropertyTypes (FontFamilyList, FontWeight, etc.) now `Deferred` instead of silently `Unset` — same for cascade-deferred lengths like `2em`. Downstream BoxBuilder (Task 12) will switch on `State` to choose its handling.
  - **Rec 2 — `CssSystemColors` so property defaults parse**: the `properties.json` default for `color` is `canvastext` per CSS Color 4 §10. Cycle 1's `ColorResolver` rejected system colors as unknown identifiers, which would have flooded the diagnostic sink with `CSS-PROPERTY-VALUE-INVALID-001` for every styled element with no explicit color. Added [`CssSystemColors`](src/NetPdf.Css/ComputedValues/PropertyResolvers/CssSystemColors.cs) — frozen dict of 20 system colors mapped to fixed sRGB values appropriate for print: `canvas` = paper white, `canvastext` = ink black, `linktext`/`visitedtext`/`activetext` from the historical Mosaic palette, `buttonface`/`buttontext`/`buttonborder` for form controls, `highlight`/`highlighttext`/`selecteditem`/`selecteditemtext` for selection rendering, `mark`/`marktext` for `<mark>`, `graytext` for disabled state, `accentcolor`/`accentcolortext` per CSS Color 4 §10.2. Clean-room values (no source-reading from any browser); print-context palette so the cascade default for `color` resolves cleanly through dispatch. Screen-browser color-scheme switching is post-v1.
  - **Rec 3 — dedicated `CurrentColor` tag**: cycle 1 used `0x00000001u` packed as a `Color` slot for the `currentcolor` keyword. A user authoring `rgba(0, 0, 1, 0)` (transparent very-dark-blue) would pack to the same slot value, making the two indistinguishable downstream. Added [`ComputedSlotTag.CurrentColor = 9`](src/NetPdf.Css/ComputedValues/ComputedSlot.cs) with `ComputedSlot.CurrentColor` factory + `IsCurrentColor` accessor. Slot has no payload bits — the tag alone says "the paint stage substitutes the cascaded `color` value". No user color value can collide. Removed the old `CurrentColorSentinel` constant entirely.
  - **Recs 4 + 5 — non-negative property gates**: added [`NonNegativeProperties`](src/NetPdf.Css/ComputedValues/PropertyResolvers/NonNegativeProperties.cs) set covering `padding-{top,right,bottom,left}` (Box Model 3 §7.1), `width`/`height`/`min-width`/`min-height`/`max-width`/`max-height` (Sizing 3 §5), `flex-grow`/`flex-shrink` (Flexbox 1 §7.1). `LengthResolver` now rejects negative lengths AND negative percentages for these properties; `NumberResolver` rejects negative numbers for flex-grow + flex-shrink. Margins, top/right/bottom/left, letter-spacing, word-spacing keep accepting negatives (their specs allow them).
  - **Rec 6 — split `TextSpacing` per `PropertyId`**: per CSS Text 3 §10.1, `letter-spacing` accepts `normal | <length>` (no percentage), while `word-spacing` accepts `normal | <length-percentage>` per CSS Text 4. `LengthResolver`'s `IsPercentageAllowed` gate now branches on `PropertyId` within the `TextSpacing` PropertyType — `letter-spacing: 5%` emits `CSS-PROPERTY-VALUE-INVALID-001` with a helpful spec-citing message; `word-spacing: 5%` resolves cleanly. Both still accept negative lengths (Text 3 lets you tighten spacing).
  - **Rec 7 — strict modern vs legacy color syntax**: per CSS Color 4 §4.2 the two syntaxes are mutually exclusive — legacy uses commas only (no slash), modern uses whitespace + optional `/` for alpha (no commas). `ColorResolver.TrySplitColorArgs` now does a top-level scan for `,` and `/`; if both are present the value is rejected with "mixed comma + slash syntax forbidden per CSS Color 4 §4.2". Two test cases for the canonical mix (`rgb(255, 0, 0 / 0.5)` and `hsl(0, 100%, 50% / 0.5)`); other malformed arrangements (e.g., `rgba(255 0 0, 0.5)`) still emit a diagnostic via the per-channel parse failure path.
  - **Rec 8 — finite/range pre-validation in resolvers**: `ComputedSlot.FromLengthPx`, `FromNumber`, and `FromPercentage` factories throw `ArgumentException` on NaN/Infinity (defensive guards against programmer errors). The cycle-1 resolvers passed parsed values through directly, which meant a `1e308in` input or a NaN from upstream calc would surface as an unhandled exception. `LengthResolver` now checks `double.IsFinite(number)` after parsing the numeric, checks the converted px value against `float.MaxValue`/`float.MinValue` after unit conversion, and bounds percentages against `ComputedSlot.{Min,Max}FixedPercentage` — all on the diagnostic path before constructing the slot. `NumberResolver` checks `double.IsFinite(n)` directly. The defensive throws stay as a last-resort programmer-error guard.
  - **Rec 9 — compatibility matrix + Phase 2 doc updates**: [`docs/compatibility-matrix.md`](docs/compatibility-matrix.md) now has explicit rows for the cycle-1 color surface: `color (named/hex/rgb/hsl)` ✅ with strict-syntax note, `color (system colors)` ✅ via CssSystemColors, `color (currentcolor)` ✅ via dedicated tag, `color (lab/lch/hwb)` 🧪 cycle-2, `color (oklab/oklch)` 🧪 cycle-2 paired with Task 3 capture, `color-mix()` 🧪 cycle-2 per CSS Color 5 §2, `light-dark()` 🧪 cycle-2.
  - **Rec 10 — `PropertyDefaultsParityTests`**: 4-test parity gate (every PropertyMetadata default × 4 invariants) covering all 63 properties: (i) every default resolves to non-Invalid (would flood diagnostics on cascade-default path); (ii) every default emits no diagnostic on resolution; (iii) defaults for cycle-1 PropertyTypes Resolve (catches resolver coverage gaps); (iv) defaults for cycle-2 PropertyTypes Defer with non-null RawText (catches resolvers that mis-classify deferred as invalid). Plus a representative valid + invalid corpus exercising the full surface — `color: red`, `color: rgb(255 128 0 / 0.8)`, `color: transparent`, `width: 75%`, `padding-top: -10px` (rejected), `letter-spacing: 5%` (rejected), `flex-grow: -1` (rejected), `display: fleks` (typo rejected), etc.
  - **New test files**: [`ResolverResultTests`](tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Css/ComputedValues/PropertyResolvers/ResolverResultTests.cs) (4 tests for the structured return), [`CssSystemColorsTests`](tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Css/ComputedValues/PropertyResolvers/CssSystemColorsTests.cs) (22 tests for the system color table + opacity invariant), [`PropertyDefaultsParityTests`](tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Css/ComputedValues/PropertyResolvers/PropertyDefaultsParityTests.cs) (6 tests). Existing resolver tests refactored to assert `result.IsResolved`/`IsDeferred`/`IsInvalid` instead of slot-tag-and-equality. New regression cases in `LengthResolverTests` (non-negative grid + letter-spacing rejecting %, word-spacing accepting %, length overflow), `ColorResolverTests` (system colors, dedicated CurrentColor tag, no-collision regression with `rgba(0, 0, 1, 0)`, mixed comma+slash rejection), `NumberResolverTests` (flex-grow/shrink rejecting negatives), `PropertyResolverDispatchTests` (Deferred state surfacing).
  - Total tests: **2745 unit / 2788 solution-wide passing** (+68 unit over Task 10's 2677/2720 baseline). AOT/JIT byte-parity gate stays green.

- **Task 10 hardening review pass — UnsupportedUnvalidated + materialization API + strict Color 4 + alignment compounds + finite guards** ✅ (2026-05-06)
  - **Rec 1 — `ResolutionState.UnsupportedUnvalidated = 3`**: cycle-1 review's `Deferred` state lumped together two semantically distinct outcomes — "the resolver validated the value but cannot reduce without context" (e.g., `width: 2em` — well-formed length, needs font metrics) versus "no resolver wired yet for this PropertyType" (e.g., `font-family: Arial` — cycle-2 work, raw text passed through unchecked). The conflation hides the cycle-2 work surface and lets typos like `font-family: <garbled>` silently masquerade as valid CSS. Added the new state with `ResolverResult.UnsupportedUnvalidated(rawText)` factory + `IsUnsupportedUnvalidated` predicate + `HasRawText` helper (true for both Deferred AND UnsupportedUnvalidated — catches the consumer footgun of "I should preserve the raw text"). Dispatch + `KeywordResolver` now route cycle-2 PropertyTypes to UnsupportedUnvalidated.
  - **Rec 2 — strict CSS Color 4 §4.2.1 / §4.3.1 syntax**: cycle-1 review's loose splitter accepted `rgb(255 0 0 0.5)` (modern shape, 4 args, NO slash) as a 4-component legacy parse. Per spec: modern syntax REQUIRES `/` before the alpha; legacy syntax requires the three RGB components to be all-numbers OR all-percentages (mixing is a §4.2.2 violation; modern allows mixing). New flag `ColorSyntax.AlphaWasSlash` lets `TryParseRgbFunction` and `TryParseHslFunction` reject modern-4-arg-without-slash. New `IsPercentageToken` helper + legacy mixed-channel check rejects e.g. `rgb(100%, 0, 0)` with a spec-citing diagnostic. Modern with mixed forms (e.g. `rgb(255 50% 0 / 0.5)`) still accepted per spec.
  - **Rec 3 — `IsFinite` guards on every numeric color input**: cycle-1 review's channel/alpha/hue/sat/light parsers ran `double.TryParse` then went straight to clamp/round, which silently accepted `1e500` (parses as `Infinity` → `(int)Math.Round(Infinity)` saturates to 255 / clamps to 1.0). Added `if (!double.IsFinite(...)) return false;` after every `TryParse` in `TryParseRgbChannel`, `TryParseAlphaComponent`, `TryParseHueComponent`, `TryParsePercentComponent` so non-finite inputs surface as `CSS-PROPERTY-VALUE-INVALID-001` with a clean error message instead of producing surprising clamped values.
  - **Rec 4 — alignment keyword tables corrected per CSS Box Alignment 3 §4**: cycle-1 review's tables had three correctness bugs: (i) bare `first` and `last` were admitted, but per §4.4 `<baseline-position>` is `[first | last]? baseline` — bare forms are NOT in the grammar; (ii) compound `first baseline` / `last baseline` were absent; (iii) the `<overflow-position> <self-position>` and `<overflow-position> <content-position>` grids (`safe center`, `unsafe end`, etc.) were missing entirely. Restructured the tables via three builder helpers — `BuildAlignItemsTable`, `BuildAlignSelfTable`, `BuildJustifyContentTable` — that compose from `SelfPositions[]`, `ContentPositions[]`, `ContentDistributions[]` and the safe/unsafe prefix list. Resolver now normalizes interior whitespace + ASCII-folds via `NormalizeKeywordWhitespace` (collapses `"first  baseline"` and `"FIRST BASELINE"` to `"first baseline"`). Per spec: align-items / align-self correctly REJECT `left` / `right` (those are content-position-only); justify-content correctly REJECTS `self-start` / `self-end` (those are self-position-only); justify-content's content-distribution set (`space-between` / `space-around` / `space-evenly` / `stretch`) and content-position extras (`left` / `right`) are present. **One subtle bug caught during implementation**: the `Tables` static-field initializer ran BEFORE the `SelfPositions[]` / `ContentPositions[]` arrays were initialized (C# static-field ordering is textual), causing a cctor `NullReferenceException`. Fixed by moving the arrays above the Tables declaration with a comment explaining the constraint.
  - **Rec 5 — `MaterializeInto` API + `ComputedStyle` deferred-text store**: cycle-1 review introduced the structured `ResolverResult` but consumers could still drop the raw text by writing `result.Slot` (which is `Unset` for Deferred / UnsupportedUnvalidated) directly into ComputedStyle. The footgun fix: a new `ResolverResult.MaterializeInto(ComputedStyle, PropertyId)` method that switches on State — Resolved → `style.Set(slot)`, Deferred + UnsupportedUnvalidated → `style.SetDeferred(rawText)`, Invalid → no-op (cascade falls back per L4 §4.4). New `ComputedStyle.SetDeferred(PropertyId, string)` + `IsDeferred(PropertyId)` + `TryGetDeferred(PropertyId, out string?)` API backed by a lazily-allocated `Dictionary<PropertyId, string>` side store. Bitmap bit is set so `IsSet(pid)` returns true (the cascade still knows an explicit declaration applied — just typed as raw text). `Set(typedSlot)` clears any prior deferred entry for the same property; `Unset(pid)` clears both; pool `Reset()` clears the deferred-text dict so re-rented instances start clean.
  - **Rec 6 — Phase 2 doc sync**: [`docs/phases/phase-2-css-engine.md`](docs/phases/phase-2-css-engine.md) "Modern syntax tokens" table now has explicit cycle-1 status for `rgb`/`rgba`/`hsl`/`hsla` (✅ with strict-syntax callout) and named/system/currentcolor (✅ with table+tag links); cycle-2 status for `oklch`/`oklab`/`color-mix`/`light-dark`/`lab`/`lch`/`hwb` (🧪, paired with Task 3 pre-pass capture); each row links the resolver and the L4/L5 spec section. Cleaner contributor map for the cycle-2 work.
  - **New test file**: [`HardeningReviewTests`](tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Css/ComputedValues/PropertyResolvers/HardeningReviewTests.cs) — 30+ tests covering all 6 recs end-to-end: Resolved/Deferred/UnsupportedUnvalidated/Invalid mutual distinction; modern-4-arg-without-slash rejection (4 cases for rgb + hsl); legacy mixed-channel rejection (4 cases) with modern mixing still accepted (2 cases); `IsFinite` rejection across channels/alpha/hue/sat/light (6 cases); alignment compound-keyword acceptance (10 cases) + bare-first/last rejection + cross-property keyword rejection (`left`/`right` on align-items, `self-start`/`self-end` on justify-content); MaterializeInto round-trip across all 4 states + Set-clears-deferred + Unset-clears-deferred + pool-reset-clears-deferred. Existing tests adjusted: `KeywordResolverTests.Property_with_no_table_*` → expects UnsupportedUnvalidated; `PropertyResolverDispatchTests.Unsupported_PropertyType_*` → expects UnsupportedUnvalidated; `PropertyDefaultsParityTests.Cycle_2_property_types_*` → expects UnsupportedUnvalidated; `ResolverResultTests` extended for the 4th state.
  - Total tests: **2799 unit / 2842 solution-wide passing** (+54 unit over the cycle-1 review's 2745). AOT/JIT byte-parity gate stays green.

- **Task 11 — `Box` hierarchy + `BoxKind` enum** ✅ (2026-05-06)
  - **`src/NetPdf.Layout/Boxes/BoxKind.cs` (new)** — single-byte enum classifying every box's layout role per CSS Display L3 §2.4 (outer/inner display dichotomy) plus module-specific kinds. The full set: `Root` (single root corresponding to the initial containing block); block-level: `BlockContainer`, `ListItem`, `Table`, `FlexContainer`, `GridContainer`, `AnonymousBlock`; inline-level: `InlineBox`, `AtomicInline` (for `inline-block`/`inline-table`/`inline-flex`/`inline-grid`), `TextRun` (contiguous text characters), `AnonymousInline`; structural: `LineBox` (per-line container produced by inline-formatting-context layout per Inline L3 §3 — distinct from `AnonymousInline` which is a box-generation construct), `Marker` (`::marker` pseudo + Lists L3 §3.1 list-item marker), `ReplacedElement` (img/video/canvas/iframe/object/embed); table model per Tables L3 §2: `TableRowGroup`/`TableHeaderGroup`/`TableFooterGroup`/`TableRow`/`TableCell`/`TableColumnGroup`/`TableColumn`/`TableCaption`; Flexbox 1 §3: `FlexItem`; Grid 2 §3: `GridItem`. **Granularity choice**: a single concrete `Box` with a `BoxKind` discriminator (rather than a class hierarchy) keeps allocation simple, matches the codebase's pattern for typed-value dispatch (e.g., `PropertyType`), and avoids the deep-inheritance navigability problem larger engines suffer from.
  - **`BoxPseudo.cs` (new)** — orthogonal enum (`None`/`Before`/`After`/`Marker`/`FirstLine`/`FirstLetter`) per CSS Pseudo L4 §3 so any `BoxKind` can carry a pseudo designation without multiplying the kind matrix (a `::before` box can be `BlockContainer` if `display: block`, `InlineBox` by default, `AtomicInline` if `display: inline-block`). Highlight pseudos (`::selection`, etc.) are post-v1 — they're paint-time overlays, not box-generation pseudos.
  - **`Box.cs` (new)** — `internal sealed class` (reference identity is meaningful: parent pointers + mutable child list during box generation; pure-class trumps record class for the use case). Fields: `Kind`, `Style` (shared with parent for anonymous boxes; the cascade owns the `ComputedStyle` lifetime), `SourceElement` (AngleSharp `IElement?` — null for anonymous + root), `Pseudo`, `Text` (only meaningful for `TextRun` — phase 3 segments + shapes + breaks per UAX #14/#29), `Parent`, `Children` (`IReadOnlyList<Box>` view over a `List<Box>` — random-access splices for table-fixup + anonymous-box insertion in Tasks 12+13). **Constructor + four static factories** encode the construction patterns BoxBuilder will use: `ForElement(kind, style, element)` for the principal box of an element; `ForPseudo(kind, style, element, pseudo)` for `::before`/`::after`/etc. boxes (rejects `BoxPseudo.None`); `Anonymous(kind, inheritedStyle)` for line/anonymous-block/anonymous-inline boxes (no source element); `TextRun(text, style, source?)` for text boxes; `CreateRoot(initialStyle)` for the page root. Constructor + factories defensively throw on null style/text + pseudo-without-source-element.
  - **Mutation API** — `AppendChild`, `InsertChild(int index, child)`, `RemoveChild` — all maintain the parent pointer invariant (set on attach, clear on detach). Defensive throws on null arg, double-attach, self-attach, out-of-range index, removing a non-child. Sibling navigation goes through `Parent.Children[index ± 1]` — no explicit prev/next pointers, avoids the doubly-linked-invariant maintenance burden.
  - **Convenience predicates** Phase 3 layout will dispatch on: `IsBlockLevel` (true for `Root`/`BlockContainer`/`ListItem`/`AnonymousBlock`/`Table`/`FlexContainer`/`GridContainer` per Display L3 §2.4); `IsInlineLevel` (`InlineBox`/`AtomicInline`/`TextRun`/`AnonymousInline` per Inline L3 §2); `IsAnonymous` (no source element + no pseudo + not root); `IsPseudoElement` (Pseudo != None); `IsTablePart` (every Tables L3 box kind); `FirstChild`/`LastChild`; `CountDescendants` (recursive, for snapshot tests + debugging).
  - **NetPdf.Layout placeholder removed** — `Placeholder.cs`'s `LayoutEngineMarker` was unreferenced (verified via grep across `**/*.cs`); deleted to keep the project surface clean.
  - **Test plan honored** per the testing-discipline rule:
    - Unit (`tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Layout/Boxes/BoxTests.cs`, 50 tests): factory-pattern coverage (ForElement attaches source + no pseudo; ForPseudo requires non-None pseudo; ForPseudo+null source rejection; Anonymous has no source+no pseudo; TextRun carries text + is inline-level; TextRun rejects null text; CreateRoot is root + parentless + block-level; constructor null-style/null-text rejection; pseudo-without-source rejection); parent/child mutation invariants (AppendChild links pointers; AppendChild rejects double-attach + self + null; InsertChild positional + bounds + append-at-count; RemoveChild clears pointer + permits re-attach + rejects non-child); per-kind classification grids (block-level: 7 kinds × IsBlockLevel/IsInlineLevel, inline-level: 4 kinds, neither: 3 kinds, IsTablePart: 9 kinds + 4 negative); `CountDescendants` recursive traversal; `Anonymous_box_shares_parent_style_instance` pinning the style-sharing contract.
    - No integration tests at this stage — Task 11 is purely a data-model deliverable. Task 12 (BoxBuilder) will exercise the model end-to-end against the corpus.
  - Total tests: **2849 unit / 2892 solution-wide passing** (+50 unit over the hardening review's 2799/2842 baseline). AOT/JIT byte-parity gate stays green.

- **Task 11 hardening review pass — outer × inner display split + ancestor cycles + truly read-only Children + style ownership + table wrapper/grid + layout-time pseudo cleanup** ✅ (2026-05-06)
  - **Recs 1 + 5 — `BoxKind` restructure for outer × inner display + table wrapper/grid split**: cycle-1's `AtomicInline` collapsed inline-block / inline-flex / inline-grid / inline-table / inline-replaced into a single kind, losing the inner formatting context (the flex algorithm and the grid algorithm are completely different — layout dispatch can't recover the inner FC from the discriminator alone). Replaced with explicit kinds: `InlineBlockContainer`, `InlineFlexContainer`, `InlineGridContainer`, `InlineTable`, `InlineReplacedElement`. Cycle-1's `ReplacedElement` similarly conflated outer block + inline; split into `BlockReplacedElement` + `InlineReplacedElement`. Per CSS Tables L3 §2.1 a `display: table` element generates TWO boxes — the **table wrapper** (handles outer display + margins + caption + floating + positioning) and the **table grid** (anonymous inner box that runs the table layout algorithm); cycle-1 conflated both into `Table`, so split into wrapper kinds (`Table` block-level / `InlineTable` inline-level) and the always-anonymous `TableGrid` inner kind. Dropped `FlexItem` and `GridItem` — per Flexbox 1 §4 + Grid 2 §6, item-ness is context-derived (any in-flow child of a flex/grid container), not an intrinsic kind. New convenience predicates: `IsAtomicInline` (the five inline atomic kinds), `IsReplaced` (Block + Inline replaced), `IsTableWrapper` (wrappers only — distinguishes from `TableGrid` and other table parts).
  - **Rec 2 — ancestor-cycle prevention**: cycle-1's `AppendChild` / `InsertChild` checked self-attach + double-attach but missed the case where the would-be child is an ancestor of the prospective parent. Concrete bug: build `A → B → C` (A is the root with no parent), then `C.AppendChild(A)` — A.Parent is null so the parent-null check passes, creating an `A → B → C → A` cycle. Fix: shared `EnsureAttachable` helper walks `this.Parent` chain looking for the prospective child; throws `InvalidOperationException` with "Cycle detected" message on hit. Both `AppendChild` and `InsertChild` go through the helper. Two regression tests cover the grandparent-under-grandchild and parent-under-direct-child cases.
  - **Rec 3 — `Children` is truly read-only**: cycle-1 returned `IReadOnlyList<Box>` over the backing `List<Box>`; consumers could cast to `IList<Box>` and mutate the backing list directly, bypassing the parent-pointer invariant. Wrapped the backing list in `System.Collections.ObjectModel.ReadOnlyCollection<Box>` (allocated once per box in the constructor — small overhead). The wrapper still implements `IList<Box>` but mutation methods throw `NotSupportedException`. Regression test casts to `IList<Box>` and verifies all four mutation methods throw.
  - **Rec 4 — tighter constructor invariants**: cycle-1's constructor only checked the pseudo-without-source case. Added: (a) "always anonymous" kinds (`Root` / `LineBox` / `AnonymousBlock` / `AnonymousInline` / `TableGrid`) reject any `SourceElement` or `Pseudo`; (b) `Marker` pseudo must pair with `Marker` kind (and vice versa); (c) non-empty `Text` only allowed on `TextRun` (rejects stray text on other kinds); (d) `Anonymous(...)` factory rejects non-anonymous kinds (the static helper `IsAlwaysAnonymous` is shared with the constructor's validation). Each invariant has a regression test.
  - **Rec 6 — `ComputedStyle` box-ownership**: `Box` references a `ComputedStyle` rented from the cascade's pool. If `Dispose` returned the instance to the pool while a box still held the reference, the next `Rent` call would clear/repopulate the slots and silently corrupt the box's view. Added `ComputedStyle.MarkAsBoxOwned()` + `IsBoxOwned` flag. `Box`'s constructor calls `MarkAsBoxOwned` on the attached style. `Dispose` is a no-op when the flag is set (the instance stays alive for the box-tree's lifetime). `Reset()` clears the flag so re-rented instances start fresh. Cycle-2 / Phase 3 will add a tree-disposal sweep that releases ownership when the tree is discarded; for cycle 1 the styles live for the process lifetime. Regression tests verify constructing a Box marks the style + Dispose-after-box-attach doesn't return to the pool + multiple boxes can share a style idempotently.
  - **Rec 7 — `BoxPseudo` cleanup (drop `FirstLine` + `FirstLetter`)**: per CSS Pseudo L4 §3.5–§3.6 + Inline L3, the text affected by `::first-line` and `::first-letter` depends on line-breaking decisions made during layout (which characters fit on the first line, which letter is "first" after stripping punctuation, where soft-wrap opportunities lie). They cannot be materialized as boxes during the box-generation DOM walk — the box tree exists before line layout has run. Removed both from the enum; cycle-2 will track them in a separate fragment-style table applied during line layout. Highlight pseudos (`::selection`, etc.) are likewise paint-time overlays, not box-generation pseudos, and are post-v1.
  - **Rec 8 — phase 2 doc sync**: [`docs/phases/phase-2-css-engine.md`](docs/phases/phase-2-css-engine.md) Box-model section had an outdated draft listing ~20 concrete `Box` subclasses (`BlockBox`/`InlineBox`/`FlexContainerBox`/etc.) + a `BoxList` struct that never shipped. Rewritten to describe the actual sealed `Box` + `BoxKind` discriminator + `ReadOnlyCollection<Box>` design with every cycle-1 hardening detail (factory invariants, ancestor-cycle check, style ownership, layout-time pseudo exclusion, Tables wrapper/grid split). The BoxBuilder bullet now correctly notes that `::first-line`/`::first-letter` are NOT materialized in box generation.
  - **Test deltas**: BoxTests rewritten + extended to ~64 tests — 50 prior tests adapted to the new BoxKind set + 14 new hardening tests (ancestor-cycle prevention × 3, ReadOnlyCollection IList rejection, Anonymous factory rejecting non-anonymous kinds × 3, constructor rejecting Root-with-source / LineBox-with-source / Marker-pseudo-on-non-Marker / non-empty-text-on-non-TextRun / non-Marker-kind-with-Marker-pseudo, table wrapper + grid relationship, IsAtomicInline + IsReplaced + IsTableWrapper predicates, Box constructor marks style as box-owned, box-owned style refuses pool re-rental, multiple boxes share style idempotently). The `xUnit1031` analyzer (no blocking task ops in tests) forced a refactor of the predicate-test helper to use AngleSharp's synchronous `HtmlParser.ParseDocument` instead of `OpenNewAsync().GetAwaiter().GetResult()`.
  - Total tests: **2876 unit / 2919 solution-wide passing** (+27 unit over Task 11's 2849/2892). AOT/JIT byte-parity gate stays green. Active-task pointer remains **Task 12 — `BoxBuilder` DOM walk + anonymous box insertion**.

- **Task 12 cycle 1 — `BoxBuilder` DOM walk + display dispatch + anonymous-block insertion + ::before/::after pseudo materialization** ✅ (2026-05-06)
  - **`HtmlDefaultDisplay.cs` (new)** — frozen dict mapping HTML local-name → spec-default `display` keyword per HTML Living Standard "Rendering" §15.3 (the rules a real UA stylesheet would supply). Cycle-1 stand-in for the actual UA stylesheet (which ships as a follow-up). Lookup is ASCII case-insensitive; missing tags fall back to the CSS spec default of `inline`. Coverage: document structure (html/body), block-level flow (div/p/h1-h6/section/article/header/footer/nav/main/aside/blockquote/pre/address/details/dialog/etc.), lists (ul/ol/li/dt/dd → list-item), table model (table/thead/tbody/tfoot/tr/td/th/colgroup/col/caption with the right table-internal display), inline (span/a/em/strong/b/i/u/code/kbd/etc.), and replaced media (img/video/audio/canvas/iframe/object/embed → inline; replaced-ness detected separately).
  - **`HtmlReplacedElements.cs` (new)** — frozen set of HTML replaced elements per HTML Living Standard "Rendering" §15.5: img/video/audio/canvas/iframe/object/embed. Form controls (input/textarea/select/button) are replaced per spec but have internal anonymous structure that v1 doesn't render — they stay non-replaced for now.
  - **`DisplayMapper.cs` (new)** — pure function mapping (display keyword + element local name) → (`BoxKind` + 4-state outcome `Resolved`/`None`/`Contents`/`Unsupported`). Cross-references `HtmlReplacedElements` so a replaced element with `display: inline` resolves to `InlineReplacedElement` (not generic `InlineBox`); same for block. `display: inline-block` on a replaced element collapses to `InlineReplacedElement` since the inner FC is moot for an atomic replaced. Ruby family + unknown values surface as `Unsupported`; `display: none` returns `None` (caller skips); `display: contents` returns `Contents` (cycle-1 caller treats as block — cycle 2 will promote children per Display L3 §3.1.1).
  - **`BoxBuilder.cs` (new)** — main entry point: `Build(IDocument, ResolvedCascadeResult, ICssDiagnosticsSink?)` returns the synthetic `Root` box with the document tree below. Walks elements top-down; for each: rents a `ComputedStyle`, applies registry defaults (skipping `display` so `HtmlDefaultDisplay` engages — writing the registry's `inline` default would mask the UA-default fallback and yield `InlineBox` for every unstyled HTML element), inherits values from parent for inheriting properties (per CSS Cascade 4 §4.2), applies the resolved cascade declarations via `PropertyResolverDispatch.Resolve` + `MaterializeInto` (typed slot or deferred raw text). Reads computed `display` (slot keyword id → name via reverse map; falls back to `HtmlDefaultDisplay` when the cascade didn't set it). Maps to `BoxKind` via `DisplayMapper`. `display: none` skips the element + descendants. Iterates DOM child nodes — `IText` becomes `TextRun` boxes (preserving white-space for now; CSS Text 3 white-space-collapse is Phase 3's job); `IElement` recurses; comments/CDATA/etc. are ignored. Pseudo-element materialization for `::before` (prepended) + `::after` (appended): looks up cascade rule sets for the lowercase pseudo name (no `::` prefix — that's the cascade's storage key per the SelectorCompiler's `PseudoElement(lower)` convention), reads `content`, suppresses on `none`/`normal`/empty, strips quotes for string content (cycle-1 limit — counter()/attr()/image() cycle 2), creates `Box.ForPseudo` + appends a TextRun child for the generated text.
  - **Anonymous-block insertion per CSS Display L3 §3.1**: when a block container has at least one block-level AND one inline-level child, contiguous inline runs get wrapped in `AnonymousBlock` boxes via in-place restructure (snapshot Children, clear, re-append with FlushRun helper). Inline-only blocks and block-only blocks pass through unchanged. The wrapper inherits the parent's `ComputedStyle` instance per the anonymous-style-sharing contract.
  - **One subtle bug caught during testing**: `ApplyDefaults` initially applied the registry default for every property including `display`, which masked `HtmlDefaultDisplay` and yielded `InlineBox` for every unstyled HTML element (the registry default for `display` is `inline` per the CSS spec, not `block`). Fixed by skipping `display` in `ApplyDefaults` so `ReadDisplay` falls back to `HtmlDefaultDisplay` when the cascade hasn't explicitly set it. Documented the constraint in the helper's XML doc.
  - **Another subtle bug**: BoxBuilder initially called `cascade.TryGetStylesForPseudo(host, "::before")` with the `::` prefix, but the cascade stores pseudo names lowercase + WITHOUT the prefix per `SelectorCompiler`'s `PseudoElement(lower)` convention. Fixed by using `"before"` / `"after"` as the lookup keys.
  - **Test plan honored** per the testing-discipline rule:
    - Unit (`HtmlDefaultDisplayTests`, 27 tests): every block-level / inline-level / table-internal / list-item / replaced-media tag returns the expected display; case-insensitive lookup; unknown tags fall back to `inline`; null/empty input falls back to `inline`.
    - Unit (`DisplayMapperTests`, 41 tests): every block-level + inline-level + table-internal display value maps to the correct `BoxKind`; replaced-element detection (img/video/audio/canvas/iframe/object/embed × inline/block); inline-block on replaced collapses to `InlineReplacedElement`; null element treats as non-replaced; `display: none` returns `None`; `display: contents` returns `Contents`; ruby family + unknown values return `Unsupported`.
    - Unit (`BoxBuilderTests`, 21 integration tests): empty document → root + `<html>` block; default display via `HtmlDefaultDisplay` (div, span, li, table, tr, td); explicit cascade `display` overrides default; `display: none` skips; replaced detection (img → InlineReplacedElement default, BlockReplacedElement with `display: block`); text node → `TextRun`; ::before / ::after with string content emits pseudo box + text run; ::before with `content: none` or `content: normal` emits no pseudo box; anonymous-block insertion (mixed inline + block children wraps each contiguous inline run in an `AnonymousBlock`; block-only and inline-only children pass through); multiple contiguous inlines share one wrapper; `Boxes_have_box_owned_styles` confirms BoxBuilder + Box constructor wire `ComputedStyle.MarkAsBoxOwned`.
  - Total tests: **2965 unit / 3008 solution-wide passing** (+89 unit over Task 11 hardening's 2876/2919 baseline). AOT/JIT byte-parity gate stays green.

- **Task 12 hardening review pass — UA metadata defaults + LineBreak + pseudo display fix + single-string content + display:contents + BFC anon-block + source location + corpus tests** ✅ (2026-05-06)
  - **Rec 1 [P1] — metadata-content `display: none` defaults**: cycle-1 `HtmlDefaultDisplay` only listed content elements; metadata defaulted to `inline` (CSS spec fallback) so `<title>Invoice 123</title>` and `<style>p{...}</style>` would emit their text content as visible TextRun boxes. Added the HTML "Rendering" §15.3.1 + §15.5.1 metadata set: `head`, `title`, `style`, `link`, `meta`, `template`, `script` (defensive even though `HtmlParsingHost` strips it), `base`, `noscript`, `area`, `param`, `source`, `track`. Verified by a corpus test that the classic invoice's `font-family:` rule text + `@page` declarations don't surface as visible text.
  - **Rec 2 [P1] — pseudo-element display fallback**: cycle-1 `BuildPseudo` called `ReadDisplay(pseudoStyle, host)` which fell back to `HtmlDefaultDisplay.GetDefault(host.LocalName)` when the cascade hadn't set `display` on the pseudo — meaning `<div>::before` defaulted to `block` instead of the spec-correct `inline` per CSS Pseudo L4 §3.1. Worse, the `DisplayMapper.Map` call passed `host.LocalName` as the element name → `<img>::before` would be detected as a replaced element and become `InlineReplacedElement`. Added a separate `ReadPseudoDisplay` that defaults to literal `"inline"` instead of the host's UA default; the `DisplayMapper.Map` call now passes `null` for element name (pseudo-elements are never replaced).
  - **Rec 3 [P1] — `<br>` as forced line break**: cycle-1 emitted `<br>` as an empty `InlineBox`, losing the line-break semantics — Phase 3 line layout would silently absorb the empty inline. Per HTML "Rendering" §15.3.6 the UA stylesheet defines `br { content: "\A"; white-space: pre-line }`. Added `BoxKind.LineBreak` (inline-level, atomic to line layout) + special-cased `<br>` early in `BuildElementBoxes` so it short-circuits the normal element-build path. Verified inside `<table><tr><td>line1<br>line2</td></tr></table>` too.
  - **Rec 4 [P2] — restrict generated content to single CSS string with escape decoding**: cycle-1 `BoxBuilder.BuildPseudo` rendered ANY non-`none`/`normal` `content` value as a literal text run — `content: counter(items)` would render the string `"counter(items)"` as visible text. Added [`CssStringParser`](src/NetPdf.Layout/Boxes/CssStringParser.cs) — parses a single CSS string token per CSS Syntax 3 §4.3.5 + decodes the four escape sequences per §4.3.7 (hex up to 6 digits + optional whitespace separator; line continuation; literal next-char escape; null/surrogate → U+FFFD). BuildPseudo now silently emits no pseudo box when the content isn't a single string — `counter()`/`attr()`/`url()`/`open-quote`/`close-quote`/multi-token concatenation all skip the pseudo entirely (cleaner than rendering broken text). Cycle-2 will add the typed content-list parser per CSS Content 3 §2 + a `CSS-CONTENT-UNSUPPORTED-001` diagnostic.
  - **Rec 5 [P2] — `display: contents` child promotion**: per CSS Display L3 §3.1.1 a `display: contents` element's principal box disappears and its children become children of the grandparent. Refactored `BuildElement` → `BuildElementBoxes` returning `IReadOnlyList<Box>` (usually 1 item, empty for `display: none`, N items for `display: contents` after promoting children). Inheritance still flows through the contents element's style for the children's per-element ComputedStyle build. **End-to-end test deferred to cycle 2** because AngleSharp 1.0.0-beta.144's CSS parser silently drops `display: contents` as an unrecognized value (same issue affects modern color functions); cycle-2 CssPreprocessor work will preserve it. The implementation IS verified by `DisplayMapperTests.contents_returns_Contents_outcome`.
  - **Rec 6 [P2] — BFC-aware anonymous-block insertion**: cycle-1 `FixupAnonymousBlocks` used `IsBlockLevel` as the trigger condition, missing `display: inline-block` (inline-level outer + flow-root inner) and `table-cell`/`table-caption`. Per CSS Display L3 §2.1 + §3.1 the rule applies to "block containers" — boxes whose inner formatting context is flow / flow-root. Added `IsBlockContainer(BoxKind)` predicate covering Root/BlockContainer/ListItem/AnonymousBlock + InlineBlockContainer + TableCell/TableCaption. Verified by 2 new tests: `<span style="display:inline-block">before<p>middle</p>after</span>` correctly wraps the inline runs; `<table><tr><td>before<p>middle</p>after</td></tr></table>` correctly wraps inside the table cell.
  - **Rec 7 [P2] — incomplete-table tests**: cycle-1 maps `<table>` to `BoxKind.Table` directly without inserting the `TableGrid` intermediary that Tables L3 §2.1 requires (Task 13 ships the wrapper + grid + table-fixup pass). Added 2 tests pinning the cycle-1 contract: `<table>` produces `IsTableWrapper=true` Table box but NO `TableGrid` descendant; the HTML5-auto-inserted `<tbody>` + `<tr>` + `<td>` are still in the descendant chain. Updated [`BoxBuilder` XML doc](src/NetPdf.Layout/Boxes/BoxBuilder.cs) with a "**Table output is NOT layout-ready**" callout so layout consumers know not to treat the cycle-1 table subtree as final.
  - **Rec 8 [P2] — source location plumbing**: cycle-1's `ApplyResolvedDeclarations` called `PropertyResolverDispatch.Resolve(id, value, diagnostics)` with the `location` parameter defaulting to `default(CssSourceLocation)`, so any emitted property-value-invalid diagnostic had no source line/column. Now passes `winner.OriginalDeclaration.Location` through. Values are still `CssSourceLocation.Unknown` until Task 3 wires real positions, but the hookup is in place — once Task 3 lands, diagnostics line up automatically without further BoxBuilder changes.
  - **Rec 9 [P2] — production-path corpus integration tests**: cycle-1 BoxBuilder tests went directly through AngleSharp's parse + CssParserAdapter without exercising the full preprocessor + production pipeline. Added [`tests/NetPdf.RealDocuments/Css/BoxBuilderCorpusTests.cs`](tests/NetPdf.RealDocuments/Css/BoxBuilderCorpusTests.cs) with 6 tests: each of the 4 corpus invoices runs through the full pipeline (`HtmlParsingHost` → `CssPreprocessor` → `CssParserAdapter` → `CascadeResolver` → `VarResolver` → `BoxBuilder`) and produces a non-empty box tree without throwing; the classic invoice's metadata text doesn't leak (validates Rec 1); diagnostic noise stays under 50 entries on known-good input. Added `NetPdf.Layout` ProjectReference + `InternalsVisibleTo NetPdf.RealDocuments` so the integration tests can call `BoxBuilder.Build` directly.
  - **New test files**: [`BoxBuilderHardeningTests.cs`](tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Layout/Boxes/BoxBuilderHardeningTests.cs) (~30 unit tests covering Recs 1, 2, 3, 4, 6, 7), [`CssStringParserTests.cs`](tests/NetPdf.UnitTests/Layout/Boxes/CssStringParserTests.cs) (~25 tests covering single-string acceptance + hex/literal/line-continuation escapes + greedy hex consumption + every rejection class), [`BoxBuilderCorpusTests.cs`](tests/NetPdf.RealDocuments/Css/BoxBuilderCorpusTests.cs) (6 production-path tests).
  - **One subtle gotcha caught during testing**: `\09b` per CSS Syntax §4.3.7 greedy hex consumption parses as the 3-digit hex `\09B` = U+009B (because `b` is a valid hex digit), NOT tab + 'b'. To get tab + literal 'b' the author must write `\9 b` with the separating space (which is consumed). Tests pin this contract.
  - Total tests: **3027 unit / 3070 solution-wide passing** (+62 unit + 6 RealDocuments over Task 12 cycle 1's 2965/3008). AOT/JIT byte-parity gate stays green.

---

## Update protocol

When a task or phase ships:
1. Move the task from "Active" to "Subtasks completed" with a 1–2 sentence note.
2. When the phase ships: replace the "⏳ In progress" entry with a "✅ Complete" entry following the same format as Phase 0 above (what was done, what's next, how to verify).
3. Bump the "Active task" pointer for the next phase.
4. Update the "Last updated" date at the top.
5. Commit with message `docs: PROGRESS.md — <phase/task description>`.
